	Chhong3-Se3-Ki3	(1)
[1]	Goan5-khi2-thau5 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 thiN kap toe7.  2). Toe7 si7 khang-khang hun7-tun7; chhim-ian e5 bin7-chiuN7 ou-am3; Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5 un7-tong7 ti7 chui2-bin7.  3). Siong7-te3 kong2, Tioh8 u7 kng, chiu7 u7 kng.  4). Siong7-te3 khoaN3 kng, si7 ho2; Siong7-te3 chiong kng am3 pun-khui.  5). Siong7-te3 kio3 hit e5 kng choe3 Jit8, kio3 am3 choe3 Mi5.  U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 thau5 chit8-jit8.
	6). Siong7-te3 kong2, Chiah e5 chui2 e5 tiong-kan tioh8 u7 kiong-chhong, chiong chui2 kap chui2 pun-khui.  7). Siong7-te3 chiu7 cho7 kiong-chhong, lai5 hun-khui kiong-chhong-e7 e5 chui2 kap kiong-chhong-teng2 e5 chui2; chiu7 u7 an2-ni.  8). Siong7-te3 kio3 kiong-chhong choe3 ThiN.  U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-ji7 jit8.
	9). Siong7-te3 kong2, ThiN-e7 chiah e5 chui2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 kau3 chit8 sou2-chai7, ta-toe7 tioh8 chhut-hian7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni.  10). Siong7-te3 kio3 ta-toe7 choe3 Toe7; kio3 chu7-chip8 e5 chui2 choe3 Hai2; Siong7-te3 khoaN3--i si7 ho2.  11). Siong7-te3 kong2, Toe7 tioh8 hoat-chhau2, i2-kip8 kiat-chi2 e5 chhai3-soe, kap chiau3-lui7 siN ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7, hit lai7-bin7 u7 i e5 chi2, ti7 toe7-chiuN7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni.  12). Toe7 chiu7 hoat-chhau2, kap chiau3-lui7 kiat-chi2 e5 chhai3-soe, kap chiau3-lui7 siN ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7, lai7-bin7 u7 i e5 chi2; Siong7-te3 khoaN3--i si7 ho2.  13). U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-saN jit8.
	14). Siong7-te3 kong2, ThiN--nih e5 kiong-chhong tioh8 u7 hoat-kng e5 the2, lai5 hun-piat jit8-mi5; ia7 thang choe3 tiau7-thau5, su3-kui3, jit8, ni5;  15). iah8 hou7 in choe3 kng-the2 ti7 thiN e5 kiong-chhong, chio3-kng ti7 toe7-chiuN7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni.  16). Siong7-te3 chiu7 cho7 toa7 e5 kng-the2 nng7-e5; toa7 e5 kng-the2 lai5 koan2 jit8--si5, soe3 e5 kng-the2 lai5 koan2 mi5--si5; ia7 cho7 chhiN-sin5.  17). Siong7-te3 he7 in ti7 thiN--nih e5 kiong-chhong, hou7 in chio3 kng ti7 toe7--nih;  18). ia7 beh koan2 u7 jit8 mi5, hun-piat kng am3.  Siong7-te3 khoaN3--i si7 ho2.  19). U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-si3 jit8.
	20). Siong7-te3 kong2, Chui2 tioh8 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 tong7-but8; chiau2 pe ti7 toe7 e5 teng2-bin7, thiN--nih e5 kiong-chhong.  21). Siong7-te3 chiu7 chhong3-cho7 hai2--nih e5 toa7-hi5, i2-kip8 chui2 sou2 siN choe7-choe7 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 tong7-but8, kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, koh chhong3-cho7 tak8-iuN7 e5 pe-chiau2, chiau3 i e5 lui7; Siong7-te3 khoaN3--i si7 ho2.  22). Siong7-te3 su3-hok in, kong2, Tioh8 siN-thoaN3 ke-thiN chin-choe7, chhiong-moa2 ti7 hai2--nih e5 chui2, ia7 hou7 chiau2-chiah siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7 ti7 toe7--nih.  23). U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-gou7 jit8.
	24). Siong7-te3 kong2, Toe7 tioh8 siN u7 oah8-mia7 e5 tong7-but8, chiau3 i e5 lui7, cheng-siN, thang5-thoa7, toe7-chiuN7 e5 chau2-siu3, chiau3 i e5 lui7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni.  25). Siong7-te3 chiu7 cho7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 chau2-siu3 chiau3 i e5 lui7, cheng-siN chiau3 i e5 lui7, toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 thang5-thoa7 chiau3 i e5 lui7; Siong7-te3 khoaN3--i si7 ho2.  26). Siong7-te3 kong2, Lan2 tioh8 cho7 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 e5 siong7, chiau3 lan2 e5 khoan2; hou7 in koan2-li2 hai2--nih e5 hi5, thiN--nih e5 chiau2, kap cheng-siN, kap choan5-toe7, i2-kip8 toe7-chiuN7 teh so5 e5 thang5-thoa7.  27). Siong7-te3 chiu7 chhong3-cho7 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 I ka-ki7 e5 siong7, chiau3 Siong7-te3 e5 siong7 chhong3-cho7 i; chhong3-cho7 in lam5--e5 lu2--e5.  28). Siong7-te3 su3-hok in; Siong7-te3 koh tui3 in kong2, Tioh8 siN-thoaN3 chin-choe7, chhiong-moa2 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, lai5 khah-iaN5 i; ia7 tioh8 ti7-li2 hai2--nih e5 hi5, thiN--nih e5 chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 sou2 tin2-tang7 e5 oah8-mih8.  29). Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 u7 hou7 lin2 pian3 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 kiat-chi2 e5 chhai3-soe, koh it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7, ki5-tiong u7 kiat-chi2 e5 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2; long2 hou7 lin2 choe3 chiah8-mih8.  30). Lun7-kau3 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3, thiN-tiong it-chhe3 e5 chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 oe7 tin2-tang7 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 mih8, Goa2 chiong it-chhe3 chhiN-chhau2 hou7 in choe3 chiah8-mih8; chiu7 u7 an2-ni.  31). Siong7-te3 khoaN3 I it-chhe3 sou2 cho7--e5, khoaN3 ah, chin-ho2.  U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-lak8 jit8.

[2]	ThiN toe7 kap i it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 i2-keng choe3-oan5.  2). Ti7 te7-chhit jit8, Siong7-te3 oan5 I sou2 cho7 e5 kang; chiu7 ti7 te7-chhit jit8 hioh I it-chhe3 sou2 cho7 e5 kang.  3). Siong7-te3 su3-hok ti7 te7-chhit jit8, teng7 choe3 seng3-jit8; in-ui7 ti7 chit-jit8 Siong7-te3 theng5 I it-chhe3 chhong3-cho7 e5 kang, chiu7 an-hioh.
	4). ThiN toe7 chhong3-cho7 e5 lai5-lek8, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 cho7 toe7 kap thiN e5 jit8, chhin-chhiuN7 e7-toe2.  5). SoaN-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 chhau2-bak8 be7 u7 ti7 toe7--nih; soaN-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 chhai3-soe be7 u7 hoat; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 bo5 loh8-hou7 ti7 toe7--nih, ia7 bo5 lang5 thang cheng3-choh hit e5 thou2-toe7.  6). Chong2-si7 u7 bu7 tui3 toe7 khi2, lun7-tek8 pian3 toe7-bin7.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 eng7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thou5-hun2 chhiau choe3 lang5, pun5 oah8 e5 khi3 jip8 i e5 phiN7-khang; lang5 chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 oah8 e5 leng5-hun5.  8). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 ti7 tang-hng, ti7 Ai-tian5, cheng3 chit8 e5 hng5; chiong sou2 cho7 e5 lang5 he7 ti7-hia.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 hou7 tak8-iuN7 e5 chhiu7 tui3 toe7--nih hoat--khi2-lai5, ho2-khoaN3 ia7 ho2-chiah8; ti7 hng5 e5 tiong-kan koh u7 oah8-mia7 e5 chhiu7, kap hun-piat ho2-phaiN2 e5 chhiu7.  10). Ai-tian5 u7 ho5 lau5-chhut lai5 koan3-ak hit e5 hng5; tui3-hia hun-khui choe3 si3-tiau5.  11). Thau5-chit8-tiau5 mia5-kio3 Pi2-sun3; chiu7-si7 seh8-lau5 ti7 Hap-hui-lah8 choan5-toe7--e5; ti7-hia u7 chhut kim;  12). hit-ui7 e5 kim si7 chin-ho2; iah8 chhut chin-chu phek-gek8.  13). Te7-ji7-tiau5 mia5 kio3 Ki-hun3, chiu7-si7 seh8-lau5 ti7 Kou2-sit8 choan5-toe7--e5.  14). Te7-saN-tiau5 mia5-kio3 Hi-ti2-kiat, chiu7-si7 lau5 ti7 A-sut8 e5 tang--si3-e5.  Te7-si3-tiau5 chiu7-si7 Pek-lat.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 chiong hit e5 lang5 he7 ti7 Ai-tian5 hng5, lai5 cheng3-choh kou3-siu2.  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 hoan-hu3 hit e5 lang5 kong2, Hng5-lai7 tak8-ho7 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2, thang sui5-i3 lai5 chiah8.  17). Chong2-si7 hun-piat ho2-phaiN2 e5 chhiu7, i e5 ke2-chi2 m7-thang chiah8; in-ui7 chiah8 e5 jit8 li2 tek-khak si2.
	18). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kong2, Lang5 toaN-sin ka-ki7 toa3 m7-ho2; Goa2 beh ka7 i cho7 chit8 e5 pang-chan7--e5, lai5 phit-phoe3 i.  19). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 eng7 thou5 choe3 soaN-ia2 tak8-iuN7 e5 chau2-siu3, i2-kip8 khong-tiong tak8-iuN7 e5 pe-chiau2; chhoa7 kau3 hit-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, khoaN3 i beh chheng in sim2-mih8 mia5; kiN3-na7 i sou2 chheng tak8-iuN7 oah8-mih8--e5, chiu7 choe3 hit e5 mih8 e5 mia5.  20). Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 ka7 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, kap khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, kap soaN-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3 long2 ho7 mia5; chong2-si7 chhe7 bo5 chit8-e5 thang choe3 hit lang5 e5 pang-chan7, lai5 phit-phoe3 i.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 hou7 hit e5 lang5 khun3 tang7-bin5, i chiu7 khun3; chiu7 theh8 i e5 hiap8-kut chit8-ki, pau-bat8 i e5 bah.  22). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 chiu7 chiong tui3 hit-lang5 sou2 theh8-chhut e5 hiap8-kut, cho7-chiaN5 chit8 e5 cha-bou2-lang5, chhoa7 lai5 chiu7-kun7 hit-lang5.  23). Hit-lang5 kong2, TaN chit-e5 si7 goa2 kut-lai7 e5 kut, bah-lai7 e5 bah; beh chheng-choe3 cha-bou2-lang5, in-ui7 i si7 tui3 ta-pou-lang5 theh8-chhut.  24). Sou2-i2 lang5 beh li7-khui i e5 pe7-bu2, kiat-lian5 i e5 bou2, in chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-the2.  25). Ang-bou2 nng7-lang5 piN5-piN5 thng3-pak-theh, ia7 bo5 kian3-siau3.

[3]	Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 sou2 cho7 soaN-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8, choa5 si7 pi2 in khah kau2-khiat.  Choa5 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Siong7-te3 kiam2 u7-iaN2 kong2, Hng5-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7, lin2 long2 m7-thang chiah8 mah?  2). Hu7-jin5-lang5 tui3 choa5 kong2, Hng5-lai7 chhiu7--nih e5 ke2-chi2 goan2 thang chiah8;  3). chi2-u7 hng5 tiong-ng hit chang5 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2 Siong7-te3 bat kong2, Lin2 m7-thang chiah8--i, iah8 m7-thang bong, kiaN-liau2 oe7 si2.  4). Choa5 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Lin2 bo5 tek-khak oe7 si2.  5). In-ui7 Siong7-te3 chai lin2 chiah8 e5 jit8, lin2 e5 bak8-chiu chiu7 oe7 khui, lin2 beh chhin-chhiuN7 Siong7-te3, oe7 hun-piat ho2-phaiN2.  6). Hu7-jin5-lang5 khoaN3 hit chang5 chhiu7, ho2-chiah8 iah8 kah-bak8; koh hit chang5 chhiu7 si7 thang him-bou7, hou7 lang5 u7 ti3-hui7; chiu7 ban2 i e5 ke2-chi2 chiah8 i, soa3 hou7 i e5 tiong7-hu, i iah8 chiah8 i.  7). In nng7-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu chiu7 khui, chiah chai in si7 thng3-pak-theh; chiu7 pin2 bu5-hoa-ko2 hioh8, ui7 ka-ki7 choe3 kun5.  8). Jit8 liang5-leng2 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kiaN5-iu5 ti7 hng5-lai7; in thiaN-kiN3 I e5 siaN, hit-lang5 kap i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 bih ti7 hng5-lai7 e5 chhiu7-tiong, lai5 siam2-pi7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 e5 bin7.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kio3 hit-lang5, tui3 i kong2, Li2 ti7 tah-loh8?  10). I chiu7 kong2, Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 Li2 e5 siaN ti7 hng5-lai7, goa2 chiu7 kiaN, in-ui7 goa2 thng3-pak-theh; chiu7 ka-ki7 bih.  11). Kong2, Chi7-chui7 ka7 li2 kong2, li2 thng3-pak-theh? Goa2 hoan-hu3 li2 m7-thang chiah8 hit chang5 chhiu7, li2 chiah8 i mah?  12). Hit-lang5 kong2, Li2 sou2 hou7 goa2 choe3-phoaN7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, i eng7 hit chang5 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2 hou7 goa2, goa2 chiu7 chiah8 i.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Li2 sou2 choe3 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? Hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Choa5 in2-iu2 goa2, goa2 chiu7 chiah8.  14). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 tui3 choa5 kong2, Li2 i2-keng choe3 chit-e5, sou2-i2 li2 siu7 chiu3-chou2, pi2 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, kap soaN-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3, khah-tang7; li2 beh eng7 pak-tou2 kiaN5, it-seng chiah8 thou5-hun2.  15). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 kap hu7-jin5-lang5 kiat oan-siu5, li2 e5 hou7-e3 kap i e5 hou7-e3 iah8 kiat oan-siu5; i beh siong li2 e5 thau5-khak, li2 beh siong i e5 kha-au7-tiN.  16). Koh tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Goa2 tek-khak toa7-toa7 ke-thiN li2 hoai5-in7 e5 kan-khou2; li2 beh kan-khou2 siN-kiaN2; li2 beh loan5-bou7 li2 e5 tiong7-hu, i beh koan2-hat li2.  17). Ia7 tui3 A-tong kong2, Li2 i2-keng thiaN-than3 li2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 oe7, lai5 chiah8 Goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang chiah8--i e5; sou2-i2 thou2-toe7 in-ui7 li2 e5 ian5-kou3 siu7 chiu3-chou2; li2 chit8-si3-lang5 lo5-khou2, chiah tui3 i tit-tioh8 chiah8.  18). Thou2-toe7 beh ui7-tioh8 li2 hoat chhi3-phe3 kap chek8-le5; li2 ia7 beh chiah8 hng5--nih e5 chhai3-soe.  19). Li2 beh koaN7-lau5 moa2-bin7 chiah thang tit-tioh8 chiah8, kau3 li2 kui thou2; in-ui7 li2 si7 tui3 thou5 theh8--chhut-lai5; li2 pun2 si7 thou5-hun2, ia7 beh kui ti7 thou5-hun2.  20). Hit-lang5 ka7 i e5 bou2 ho7 mia5, kio3 Ha7-oa; in-ui7 i choe3 cheng3-lang5 e5 lau7-bu2.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 ui7-tioh8 hit-lang5 kap i e5 bou2 eng7 phe5 choe3 i-hok8, hou7 in chheng7.
	22). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kong2, KhoaN3 ah, chit-lang5 i2-keng kap lan2 saN chhin-chhiuN7, oe7 hun-piat ho2-phaiN2; taN kiaN-liau2 i chhun-chhiu2 koh tui3 oah8-mia7 chhiu7 ban2, lai5 chiah8, chiu7 oah8 kau3 eng2-oan2;  23). sou2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kah i chhut Ai-tian5 hng5, lai5 cheng3-choh hit e5 thou5, chiu7-si7 i sou2 tui3 i chhut e5.  24). Sou2-i2 koaN2 hit e5 lang5 chhut; ia7 ti7 Ai-tian5 hng5 e5 tang--si3 an-ti3 Ki-lou7-peng kap si3-bin7 tng2-seh8 hoat he2-iam7 e5 kiam3, lai5 hong5-siu2 oah8-mia7 chhiu7 e5 lou7.

[4]	Hit-lang5 kap i e5 bou2 Ha7-oa tang5-pang5; Ha7-oa chiu7 hoai5-in7 siN Kai-un2, kong2, Goa2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa pi3-iu7 tit-tioh8 kiaN2.  2). Koh siN i e5 sio2-ti7 A-pek.  A-pek si7 kou3-iuN5--e5, Kai-un2 si7 choh-chhan5--e5.  3). Kau3 jit8-au7, Kai-un2 chiong thou2-san2 choe3 le2-mih8 hian3 hou7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  4). A-pek ia7 chiong iuN5-kun5-tiong thau5-chiuN7-siN e5 iuN5 kap i e5 iu5 theh8--lai5 hian3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa koan3-kou3 A-pek kap i e5 le2-mih8;  5). chong2-si7 bo5 koan3-kou3 Kai-un2 kap i e5 le2-mih8.  Kai-un2 chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, piN3-bin7.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Kai-un2 kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 siu7-khi3? li2 siaN2-su7 piN3-bin7?  7). Li2 na7 kiaN5-ho2, kiam2 bo5 tit-tioh8 kam3-lap8? na7 bo5 kiaN5-ho2, choe7-giat8 bai5-hok8 ti7 mng5-khau2; i beh loan5-bou7 li2, li2 beh koan2-hat i.  8). Kai-un2 ka7 i e5 sio2-ti7 kong2.  I2-au7 in ti7 soaN--nih e5 si5, Kai-un2 kong-kek i e5 sio2-ti7 A-pek, ka7 i thai5-si2.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Kai-un2 kong2, Li2 e5 sio2-ti7 A-pek ti7 tah-loh8? I kong2, M7-chai; goa2 kiam2-si7 kou3-siu2 goa2 e5 sio2-ti7--e5 mah?  10). I kong2, Li2 u7 choe3 sim2-mih8? Lin2 sio2-ti7 e5 huih e5 siaN tui3 toe7--nih au5-kio3 Goa2.  11). Toe7 u7 khui-chhui3 tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2 lai5 chiap-siu7 lin2 sio2-ti7 e5 huih, taN li2 tui3 chit e5 toe7 siu7 chiu3-chou2.  12). Li2 cheng3-choh, toe7 bo5 beh chhut thou2-san2 hou7 li2; li2 beh si3-koe3 chau2, phiau-liu5 toe7-chiuN7.  13). Kai-un2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 heng5-hoat8 thai3-tang7, ke3-thau5 ti7 goa2 sou2 oe7-tng--e5.  14). Li2 kin-a2-jit8 koaN2 goa2 li7-khui chit e5 toe7-bin7, bo5 thang toa3 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; goa2 si3-koe3 chau2 phiau-liu5 toe7-chiuN7; kiN3-na7 tu2-tioh8 goa2 e5 beh thai5-si2 goa2.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2, In-ui7 an2-ni, kiN3-na7 thai5-si2 Kai-un2 e5, beh siu7 chhit-pe7 e5 po3-eng3.  Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 ka7 Kai-un2 lip8 chit8 e5 ki3-ho7, bian2-tit tu2-tioh8 i e5 thai5-si2 i.
	16). Kai-un2 chiu7 li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, khi3 ti7 Ai-tian5 e5 tang--si3, Lo5-tek e5 toe7, khia7-khi2.  17). Kai-un2 kap i e5 bou2 tang5-pang5; i e5 bou2 hoai5-in7 siN I2-lok8; Kai-un2 khi2 siaN5, chiu7 chiau3 i e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5 chheng hit e5 siaN5 e5 mia5 choe3 I2-lok8.  18). I2-lok8 siN I2-na2; I2-na2 siN Bi2-hou7-nga2-li7; Bi2-hou7-nga2-li7 siN Ma2-thou2-sat-li7; Ma2-thou2-sat-li7 siN Lah8-bek8.  19). Lah8-bek8 chhoa7 nng7 e5 bou2; chit8-e5 mia5 A-tai7, chit8-e5 mia5 Se2-lah8.  20). A-tai7 siN Nga2-pat; i choe3 khia7-khi2 pou3-piN5 chhi7 cheng-siN e5 lang5 e5 chou2.  21). I e5 sio2-ti7 mia5 Iu5-pat; i si7 choe3 it-chhe3 toaN5-khim5 pun5-siau e5 lang5 e5 chou2.  22). Se2-lah8 ia7 siN Thou2-pat-kai-un2; i chiu7-si7 che3-cho7 tak8-iuN7 tang5 thih lai7-khi3 e5; Thou2-pat-kai-un2 e5 chi2-be7 chiu7-si7 Na2-ma2.  23). Lah8-bek8 tui3 i nng7 e5 bou2 kong2: 
	A-tai7 kap Se2-lah8 ah, tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN, 
	Lah8-bek8 e5 bou2 ah, tioh8 ti3-i3 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7;
	Lang5 siong goa2, goa2 thai5 i,
	Siau3-lian5 lang5 hai7 goa2, goa2 thai5 i.
24).	Kai-un2 e5 sin-oan na7 si7 chhit-pe7,
	Chiu7 Lah8-bek8 e5 sin-oan tek-khak chhit-chap8-chhit pe7.
	25). A-tong koh kap i e5 bou2 tang5-pang5; i e5 bou2 siN-kiaN2, piau2-mia5 kio3 Siat; si7 kong2, Siong7-te3 koh ka7 goa2 siat-lip8 chit8 e5 kiaN2 lai5 thoe3 A-pek, in-ui7 Kai-un2 ka7 i thai5--si2.  26). Siat ia7 siN-kiaN2, piau2-mia5 I2-lo5-su7; hit-si5 lang5 chiah khi2-thau5 kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.

[5]	A-tong e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Tng Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 lang5 e5 jit8, si7 chiau3 Siong7-te3 e5 khoan2-sit lai5 cho7 i;  2). chhong3-cho7 in ta-pou kap cha-bou2; ti7 in siu7 chhong3-cho7 e5 jit8, su3 in hok-khi3, chheng in e5 mia5 kio3 Lang5.  3). A-tong chit8-pah saN-chap8 he3 siN-kiaN2 chiau3 i e5 khoan2, chhin-chhiuN7 i e5 siong7, piau2 mia5 kio3 Siat.  4). A-tong siN Siat liau2-au7 koh lek8-ke3 poeh-pah ni5; ki5-tiong iau2 u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  5). A-tong ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah saN-chap8 he3, chiah si2.
	6). Siat chit8-pah lian5 gou7 he3, siN I2-lo5-su7.  7). Siat siN I2-lo5-su7 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah lian5 chhit ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  8). Siat ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah it-chap8-ji7 he3, chiah si2.
	9). I2-lo5-su7 kau2-chap8 he3, siN Kai-lam5.  10). I2-lo5-su7 siN Kai-lam5 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah it-chap8-gou7 ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  11). I2-lo5-su7 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah lian5 gou7 he3, chiah si2.
	12). Kai-lam5 chhit-chap8 he3, siN Ma2-lek8-liat8.  13). Kai-lam5 siN Ma2-lek8-liat8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah si3-chap8 ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  14). Kai-lam5 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah it-chap8 he3, chiah si2.
	15). Ma2-lek8-liat8 lak8-chap8 gou7 he3, siN Nga2-liat8.  16). Ma2-lek8-liat8 siN Nga2-liat8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah saN-chap8 ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  17). Ma2-lek8-liat8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 poeh-pah kau2-chap8 gou7 he3, chiah si2.
	18). Nga2-liat8 chit8-pah lak8-chap8 ji7 he3, siN I2-lok8.  19). Nga2-liat8 siN I2-lok8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  20). Nga2-liat8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah lak8-chap8 ji7 he3, chiah si2.
	21). I2-lok8 lak8-chap8 gou7 he3, siN Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8.  22). I2-lok8 siN Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8 e5 liau2-au7 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap kiaN5 saN-pah ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  23). I2-lok8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 saN-pah lak8-chap8 gou7 he3.  24). I2-lok8 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap kiaN5, Siong7-te3 chiap i khi3; i chiu7 bo5 ti7-teh.
	25). Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8 chit8-pah poeh-chap8 chhit he3, siN Lah8-bek8.  26). Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8 siN Lah8-bek8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 chhit-pah poeh-chap8 ji7 ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  27). Ma2-thou2-sat-lah8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah lak8-chap8 kau2 he3, chiah si2.
	28). Lah8-bek8 chit8-pah poeh-chap8 ji7 he3, siN chit8 e5 kiaN2,  29). piau2-mia5 kio3 Na2-a, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa bat chiu3-chou2 toe7, hou7 lan2 choe3 kang lo5-khou2; taN chit e5 kiaN2 beh an-ui3 lan2.  30). Lah8-bek8 siN Na2-a e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 gou7-pah kau2-chap8 gou7 ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  31). Lah8-bek8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 chhit-pah chhit-chap8-chhit he3, chiah-si2.
	32). Na2-a gou7-pah he3; siN Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut.

[6]	Lang5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 na2 khah-choe7, ia7 siN cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 si5,  2). Siong7-te3 e5 kiaN2 khoaN3-kiN3 lang5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 sui2, chiu7 chiau3 in sou2 ai3, chhoa7 in choe3 bou2.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lang5 ki3-jian5 siok8 ti7 jiok8-the2, Goa2 e5 Sin5 bo5 beh eng2-oan2 tiam3 ti7 in; na7-si7 in e5 jit8-chi2 beh kau3 chit8-pah ji7-chap8 ni5.  4). Ti7 hit-si5 u7 toa7-han3 lang5 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7; au7-lai5 Siong7-te3 e5 kiaN2 kap lang5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tang5-pang5, in chiu7 siN kiaN2, chiu7-si7 tui3 kou2-cha2 eng-hiong5 u7 mia5-siaN e5 lang5.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-kiN3 lang5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, choe7-ok chin toa7, sim-lai7 sou2 siuN7 e5 liam7-thau5 tak8-jit8 long2 si7 phaiN2.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa the3-hoe2 I cho7 lang5 ti7 se3-kan; sim-lai7 iu-bun7.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 toe7-chiuN7 chau5-biat8 Goa2 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 lang5; chiong lang5 kap chau2-siu3, thang5-thoa7, pe-chiau2, long2 chau5-biat8; in-ui7 Goa2 cho7 in liau2 u7 the3-hoe2.  8). Chi2-u7 Na2-a tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.
	9). Na2-a e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Na2-a si7 gi7-lang5; ti7 hit se3-tai7 e5 tiong-kan si7 oan5-choan5 e5 lang5; Na2-a kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap kiaN5.  10). Na2-a siN saN e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut.  11). Se3-kai3 pai7-hoai7 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5; se3-kai3 chhiong-moa2 kiong5-po7.  12). Siong7-te3 khoaN3 se3-kai3 long2 pai7-hoai7; in-ui7 kiN3 u7 jiok8-the2--e5 in ti7 se3-kai3 e5 kiaN5-choe3 long2 si7 pai7-hoai7.
	13). Siong7-te3 tui3 Na2-a kong2, KiN3 u7 jiok8-the2--e5 Goa2 khoaN3 in e5 boat8-ki5 i2-keng kau3, in-ui7 in e5 kiong5-po7 chhiong-moa2 ti7 se3-kai3; li2 khoaN3, Goa2 beh chiong in kap toe7 choe3 chit8-e7 hui2-biat8.  14). Li2 tioh8 eng7 chheng5-peh-chha5 choe3 toa7-chun5, chun5-lai7 tioh8 keh pang5-keng, lai7-goa7 eng7 lek8-chhiN-iu5 kou5 i.  15). Toa7-chun5 e5 cho7-hoat si7 an2-ni:  tng5 saN-pah tiu2, khoah gou7-chap8 tiu2, koaiN5 saN-chap8 tiu2.  16). Chun5 tioh8 choe3 thang-a2, koaiN5 chit8 tiu2; mng5 tioh8 he7 ti7 chun5-piN; chun5 tioh8 choe3 saN-chan5, hun siong7, tiong, ha7.  17). Li2 khoaN3, Goa2, Goa2 beh hou7 toa7 chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, lai5 hui2-biat8 thiN-e7 kiN3-na7 u7 oah8-khi3 e5 jiok8-the2; kiN3-na7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7--e5 long2 oe7 si2.  18). Chong2-si7 Goa2 beh kap li2 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok.  Li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2, li2 e5 bou2, li2 e5 sim-pu7, long2 tioh8 jip8 toa7-chun5.  19). KiN3-na7 u7 oah8-khi3 e5 jiok8-the2, tak8-iuN7 chit8-tui3, chit8-chiah kang--e5, chit8-chiah bu2--e5, li2 tioh8 toa3 in jip8 toa7-chun5, kap li2 saN-kap po2-choan5 oah8-mia7.  20). Pe-chiau2 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, cheng-siN kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, toe7-chiuN7 e5 thang5-thoa7 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, tak8-iuN7 chit8-tui3 beh kau3 li2 hia lai5 po2-choan5 in e5 oah8-mia7.  21). Li2 tioh8 theh8 tak8-iuN7 e5 chiah8-mih8 chek-chu7--teh, thang choe3 li2 kap in e5 chiah8-mih8.  22). Na2-a chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5; chiau3 Siong7-te3 long2-chong2 sou2 beng7-leng7--e5 khi3 kiaN5.

[7]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Na2-a kong2, Li2 kap li2 choan5-ke long2 tioh8 jip8 toa7-chun5; in-ui7 ti7 chit se3-tai7 e5 tiong-kan Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 si7 gi7-lang5.  2). KiN3-na7 chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-siN, li2 tioh8 toa3 chhit-chiah kang--e5, chhit-chiah bu2--e5; bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-siN, li2 tioh8 toa3 chit8-chiah kang--e5, chit8-chiah bu2--e5.  3). ThiN--nih e5 chiau2 ia7 tioh8 toa3, chhit-chiah kang--e5, chhit-chiah8 bu2--e5, thang lau5 in e5 cheng2 oah8 ti7 choan5-toe7.  4). In-ui7 koh ke3 chhit-jit8, Goa2 beh loh8-hou7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5; chiong Goa2 sou2 cho7 tak8-ho7 e5 oah8-mih8 long2 tui3 toe7-chiuN7 chau5-biat8.  5). Na2-a chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 beng7-leng7 i e5, it-chin7 khi3 kiaN5.
	6). Tng toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7 chiuN7 e5 si5, Na2-a lak8-pah he3.  7). Na2-a chiu7 kap i e5 kiaN2, i e5 bou2, i e5 sim-pu7, long2 jip8 toa7-chun5, siam2-pi7 toa7-chui2.  8). Chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-siN, kap bo5 chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-siN, pe-chiau2, kap toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 thang5-thoa7,  9). long2 chit8-tui3 chit8-tui3, u7 kang--e5 u7 bu2--e5, kau3 Na2-a hia, chin3-jip8 toa7-chun5, chiau3 Siong7-te3 beng7-leng7 Na2-a e5.  10). Ke3 hiah e5 chhit-jit8 toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7.  11). Tng Na2-a lak8-pah he3, ji7-geh8 chap8-chhit jit8, hit-jit8 chhim-ian e5 chui2-goan5 long2 lih8-khui, thiN ia7 phoa3-khiah.  12). Si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5 loh8-hou7 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7.  13). Tu2-tu2 hit-jit8 Na2-a kap i e5 kiaN2, Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut, kap Na2-a e5 bou2, kap i saN e5 sim-pu7, long2 jip8 toa7-chun5;  14). in kap pah-siu3 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, it-chhe3 so5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thang5-thoa7 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, it-chhe3 u7-sit8-e5 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, it-chhe3 e5 pe-chiau2 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, long2-chong2 chin3-jip8 toa7-chun5.  15). KiN3-na7 jiok8-the2 lai7-bin7 u7 oah8-khi3--e5, long2 chit8-tui3 chit8-tui3, kau3 Na2-a hia, jip8 toa7-chun5.  16). KiN3-na7 jip8 toa7-chun5--e5, si7 u7 kang u7 bu2 e5 jiok8-the2, chiau3 Siong7-te3 sou2 beng7-leng7 i--e5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 ka7 i koaiN--teh.  17). Chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 si3-chap8-jit8; chui2 tiong3 na2 koaiN5, hou7 toa7-chun5 chheng3-phu5, chun5 chiu7 li7 toe7.  18). Chui2-se3 chin-toa7, ti7 toe7-chiuN7 tit8-tit8 tiong3--khi2-lai5; chun5 phiau-liu5 ti7 chui2-bin7.  19). Chui2-se3 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 kek8-ki5 toa7; thiN-e7 e5 koaiN5-soaN long2 hou7 i im-bat8.  20). Chui2-se3 pi2 soaN ke-tiong3 koaiN5 chap8-gou7 tiu2; soaN long2 hou7 i im-bat8.  21). KiN3-na7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 tong7-but8, chiu7-si7 pe-chiau2, cheng-siN, chau2-siu3, kap it-chhe3 so5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thang5-thoa7, i2-kip8 sou2 u7 e5 cheng3-lang5, long2 si2.  22). KiN3-na7 ti7 ta-toe7 u7 phiN7-khang chhoan2-khui3 e5 seng-leng5 long2 si2.  23). KiN3-na7 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8 long2 chau5-biat8; lang5 kap cheng-siN, thang5-thoa7, i2-kip8 thiN-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, in long2 tui3 toe7-chiuN7 siu7 chau5-biat8; chi2-u7 Na2-a chham hiah-e5 kap i ti7 chun5-nih--e5 lau5-teh.  24). Chui2-se3 chin-toa7 ti7 toe7-chiuN7, lek8-ke3 chit8-pah gou7-chap8-jit8.

[8]	Siong7-te3 ki3-tit Na2-a, kap it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8, i2-kip8 kap i ti7 toa7-chun5 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN; Siong7-te3 hou7 hong chhe toe7, chui2 chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 siau-sih8.  2). Chhim-ian e5 chui2-goan5, kap thiN e5 khang-khiah, long2 koaiN-bat8; thiN--nih e5 hou7 iah8 soah.  3). Chui2 tui3 toe7-chiuN7 tit8-tit8 the3; chit8-pah gou7-chap8 jit8 au7, chui2 chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 siau.  4). Chhit-geh8 chap8 chhit jit8, chun5 khoa3 ti7 A-lah8-liap8 e5 soaN.  5). Chui2 koh chiam7-chiam7 siau, tit8-tit8 kau3 chap8-geh8.  Chap8-geh8 chhoe-it jit8, soaN-thau5 chiah chhut-hian7.  6). Ke3 si3-chap8 jit8, Na2-a khui i sou2 choe3 toa7-chun5 e5 thang-a2;  7). pang3 chit8 chiah ou-a chhut-khi3; ou-a pe-lai5 pe-khi3, tit8-tit8 kau3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 chui2 ta.  8). I koh pang3 chit8 chiah chiN2-a2 chhut-khi3, beh khoaN3 chui2 tui3 toe7-chiuN7 the3 a2-be7.  9). Chong2-si7 chiN2-a2 chhe7 bo5 hioh-kha e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 to3-tng2 lai5 toa7-chun5 Na2-a hia; in-ui7 pian3-toe7-bin7 iau2 u7 chui2; Na2-a chhun-chhiu2 chih i, liah8 jip8 toa7-chun5.  10). I koh theng3-hau7 chhit-jit8, koh pang3 chiN2-a2 chhut toa7-chun5.  11). Kau3 e5-hng chiN2-a2 to3-lai5 i hia, chhui3 ka7 chit8-hioh8 sin e5 kaN-na2-hioh8; Na2-a chiah chai chui2 tui3 toe7-chiuN7 the3 lah.  12). I koh theng3-hau7 chhit-jit8, pang3 chiN2-a2 chhut-khi3; chiN2-a2 long2 bo5 koh to3--lai5.  13). Kau3 Na2-a lak8-pah lian5 chit8 he3, chiaN-geh8 chhoe-it jit8, toe7-chiuN7 e5 chui2 long2 ta; Na2-a chiu7 hian-khui toa7-chun5 e5 koa3, lai5 khoaN3; chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 toe7-bin7 i2-keng ta.  14). Ji7-geh8 ji7-chhit-jit8, thou5-toe7 long2 ta.
	15). Siong7-te3 tui3 Na2-a kong2,  16). Li2 kap li2 e5 bou2, li2 e5 kiaN2, li2 e5 sim-pu7, long2 tioh8 chhut toa7-chun5.  17). Ti7 li2 hia kiN3-u7 jiok8-the2 e5 oah8-mih8, chiu7-si7 pe-chiau2, cheng-siN, kap it-chhe3 so5 ti7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thang5-thoa7, long2 tioh8 toa3 in chhut; hou7 in heng-ong7 ti7 toe7--nih, siN-thoaN3 chin-choe7.  18). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Na2-a kap i e5 kiaN2, i e5 bou2, i e5 sim-pu7, long2 chhut-lai5.  19). It-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3, it-chhe3 e5 thang5-thoa7, it-chhe3 e5 pe-chiau2, kiN3-na7 toe7-chiuN7 sou2 u7 e5 tong7-but8, kok chiau3 i e5 chok8-lui7, iah8 long2 chhut toa7-chun5.
	20). Na2-a ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5; tui3 tak8-iuN7 chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-siN, tak8-iuN7 chheng-khi3 e5 pe-chiau2, chhu2 lai5 hian3 ti7 toaN5-teng2 choe3 sio-che3.  21). Ia5-ho5-hoa phiN7 i e5 phang-bi7; Ia5-ho5-hoa sim-lai7 chiu7 kong2, Goa2 bo5 koh in-ui7 lang5 e5 ian5-kou3 chiu3-chou2 toe7, in-ui7 lang5 tui3 soe3-han3 e5 si5, sim sou2 siuN7 chiu7 phaiN2; Goa2 bo5 beh chiau3 Goa2 sou2 u7 kiaN5--e5, koh biat8 kok-cheng2 e5 oah8-mih8.  22). Toe7 iau2 ti7-teh e5 si5, chai-cheng3 siu-seng5, koaN5 joah8, tang-thiN, he7-thiN, jit8 mi5, long2 bo5 hioh.

[9]	Siong7-te3 su3-hok Na2-a, kap i e5 kiaN2, iah8 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 tioh8 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7, chhiong-moa2 toe7-chiuN7.  2). KiN3-na7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 chau2-siu3, kap thiN--nih e5 chiau2, long2 beh kiaN lin2 ui3 lin2; lian5 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 thang5-thoa7, kap hai2--nih it-chhe3 e5 hi5, long2 kau-hu3 lin2 e5 chhiu2.  3). KiN3-na7 oah8 e5 tong7-but8 long2 choe3 lin2 e5 chiah8-mih8; chiah-e5 it-chhe3 Goa2 long2 hou7 lin2, chhin-chhiuN7 hou7 lin2 chhai3-soe chit8-iuN7.  4). Tok8-tok8 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 bah, chiu7-si7 u7 kaN5-huih--e5, lin2 m7-thang chiah8.  5). Lau5 lin2 e5 huih, chiu7-si7 lau5 lin2 oah8-mia7 e5 huih e5 choe7, Goa2 beh tho2--i; Goa2 beh tui3 kok-iuN7 chau2-siu3 tho2, iah8 beh tui3 lang5 e5 chhiu2, i2-kip8 tak8-lang5 hiaN-ti7 e5 chhiu2, lai5 tho2 lang5 e5 oah8-mia7.  6). KiN3-na7 hou7 lang5 lau5 huih--e5, lang5 ia7 beh hou7 i lau5-huih; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 cho7 lang5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 I ka-ki7 e5 siong7.  7). Lin2 tioh8 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7, ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 tioh8 heng-ong7, ke-thiN chin-choe7.
	8). Siong7-te3 ka7 Na2-a kap i e5 kiaN2 kong2,  9). Goa2, Goa2 kap lin2 i2-kip8 lin2 e5 hou7-e3 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok;  10). iah8 kap hiah e5 kap lin2 ti7-teh it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8, chiu7-si7 kap lin2 ti7-teh e5 pe-chiau2, cheng-siN, it-chhe3 chau2-siu3; kiN3-na7 tui3 toa7-chun5 chhut-lai5 toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3 lip8-iok.  11). Goa2 kap lin2 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok; kiN3 u7 jiok8-the2 e5, bo5 koh hou7 toa7-chui2 biat8-bo5, iah8 bo5 koh u7 toa7-chui2 hui2-hoai7 thou2-toe7.  12). Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 kap lin2 iah8 kap hiah-e5 kap lin2 ti7-teh tak8-iuN7 e5 oah8-mih8 sou2 lip8 eng2 se3-tai7 e5 iok, si7 u7 ki3-ho7.  13). Goa2 chiong Goa2 e5 kheng7 he7 ti7 hun5--nih, thang choe3 Goa2 kap toe7 lip8 iok e5 ki3-ho7.  14). I2-au7 Goa2 hou7 hun5 khi2 jia toe7 e5 si5, beh u7 kheng7 chhut-hian7 ti7 hun5--nih.  15). Goa2 chiu7 ki3-liam7 Goa2 kap lin2 i2-kip8 tak8-iuN7 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 oah8-mih8 sou2 lip8 e5 iok, chui2 bo5 koh hoan3-lam7 sun2-hoai7 it-chhe3 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 mih8.  16). Kheng7 beh chhut-hian7 ti7 hun5--nih, Goa2 beh khoaN3--i, hou7 Goa2 ki3-liam7 Siong7-te3 kap toe7-chiuN7 tak8-iuN7 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 oah8-mih8 sou2 lip8 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  17). Siong7-te3 tui3 Na2-a kong2, Che chiu7-si7 Goa2 kap toe7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 mih8 sou2 lip8 e5 iok e5 ki3-ho7.
	18). Na2-a e5 kiaN2, chhut toa7-chun5--e5, chiu7-si7 Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut; Ham5 si7 Ka-lam5 e5 lau7-pe7.  19).  Chi2 saN-e5 si7 Na2-a e5 kiaN2; tui3 in pian3-moa2 choan5-toe7.
	20). Na2-a khi2-chhiu2 choe3 long5-hu, chai-cheng3 phu5-to5-hng5;  21). lim hit e5 chiu2 lai5 chui3, ti7 pou3-piN5-lai7 thng3-theh-theh.  22). Ka-lam5 e5 lau7-pe7, Ham5, khoaN3 in lau7-pe7 thng3-theh, khi3 goa7-bin7 ka7 in nng7 e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2.  23). Siam2 kap Nga2-hut theh8 chit8 nia2 saN, khoa3 ti7 in e5 keng-thau5; to3-the3 kiaN5 lai5 jia lau7-pe7 e5 thng3-theh; in e5 bin7 ng3-chhut, bo5 khoaN3-khi3 lau7-pe7 e5 thng3-theh.  24). Na2-a chiu2-chui3 chhiN2, chiah chai te7 ji7-kiaN2 e5 sou2-choe3.  25). Chiu7 kong2, 
	Ka-lam5 tioh8 siu7 chiu3-chou2;
	I beh choe3 i e5 hiaN-ti7 lou5-pok8 e5 lou5-pok8.
Koh kong2,
26).	Tioh8 o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, Siam2 e5 Siong7-te3;
	Ka-lam5 choe3 Siam2 e5 lou5-pok8.
27).	Goan7 Siong7-te3 hou7 Nga2-hut hoat-tian2,
	Hou7 i toa3 ti7 Siam2 e5 pou3-piN5;
	Ka-lam5 iah8 choe3 i e5 lou5-pok8.
28). Toa7-chui2 liau2-au7 Na2-a iau2 oah8 saN-pah gou7-chap8 ni5.  29). Na2-a ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah gou7-chap8 he2, chiah si2.

[10]	Na2-a e5 kiaN2 Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Toa7-chui2 i2-au7, in u7 siN kiaN2.
	2). Nga2-hut e5 kiaN2; Kho2-biat8, Ma2-kok, Ma2-tai7, Nga2-oan5, Thou2-pat, Bi2-siat, The2-lah8.  3). Kho2-biat8 e5 kiaN2; A-sit8-ki-na2, Li7-hoat, To5-ka-ma2.  4). Nga2-oan5 e5 kiaN2; I2-li7-sa, Tai7-sit, Ki-ti2 lang5, To-tan lang5.  5). Chiah e5 lang5 e5 hou7-e3, chiong tak8-kok e5 toe7-thou2, hai2-su7, pun-khui khia7-khi2, kok chiau3 i e5 khiuN-khau2, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, chiau3 in e5 pang-kok.
	6). Ham5 e5 kiaN2; Kou2-sit8, Bek8-se-im, Hut, Ka-lam5.  7). Kou2-sit8 e5 kiaN2; Se-pa, Hap-hui-lah8, Sat-hut-tha, Lah8-ma2, Sat-hut-the5-ka.  Lah8-ma2 e5 kiaN2; Si7-pa, Ti2-tan3.  8). Kou2-sit8 iah8 siN Leng5-liok8; i choe3 se3-chiuN7 eng-hiong5 e5 khi2-thau5.  9). I ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 si7 chit8 e5 eng-hiong5 phah-lah8--e5; sou2-i2 lang5 kong2, Chhin-chhiuN7 Leng5-liok8 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, si7 chit8 e5 eng-hiong5 phah-lah8--e5.  10). I e5 kok e5 khi2-thau5, chiu7-si7 Pa-piat8, I2-lek8, A-kah, Kah-ni5, ti7 Si7-na2 e5 toe7.  11). I tui3-hia chhut-lai5, khi3 A-sut8, khi2-cho7 Ni5-ni5-bi5, Li2-ho5-pek-i-ni2, Ka-lah8,  12). i2-kip8 Ni5-ni5-bi5 Ka-lah8 tiong-kan e5 Li7-sian2; che chiu7-si7 hit e5 toa7-siaN5.  13). Bek8-se lang5 siN Lou7-teng lang5, A-na2-bi2 lang5, Li7-hap lang5, Na2-hut-thou2 lang5;  14). PhaN3-su-lou2 lang5, Ka-su-lou2 lang5, (tui3 in chhut Hui-li7-su7 lang5), Ka-hui-thok lang5.
	15). Ka-lam5 siN toa7-kiaN2 Se-tun3 kap Hek;  16). i2-kip8 Ia5-pou3-su lang5, A-mou5-li7 lang5, Kek-ka-sat lang5;  17). Hi-bi2 lang5, A-ki lang5, Se-ni5 lang5;  18). A-oa2-ti2 lang5, Se2-ma2-li2 lang5, Hap-boat8 lang5; au7-lai5 Ka-lam5 chiah e5 chok8 hun-soaN3.  19). Ka-lam5 e5 keng2-kai3 si7 tui3 Se-tun3 ng3 Ki-lah8-ni2 e5 lou7, kau3 Ka-sat; koh ng3 Sou2-to-ma2, Go5-mou5-lah8, Ap-ma2, Se2-phian e5 lou7, kau3 Lah8-sa.  20). Che chiu7-si7 Ham5 e5 hou7-e3, kok chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, in e5 khiuN-khau2, ti7 in e5 toe7-thou2, in e5 pang-kok.
	21). Nga2-hut e5 hiaN Siam2, choe3 Hi-pek choan5-chok8 e5 chou2, iah8 siN-kiaN2.  22). Siam2 e5 kiaN2; I2-lan5, A-sut8, A-hoat-sat, Lou7-tek, A-lan5.  23). A-lan5 e5 kiaN2; OU-su, Hou7-lek8, Ki-thiap, Ma2-si.  24). A-hoat-sat siN Sa-lah8; Sa-lah8 siN Hi-pek.  25). Hi-pek siN nng7 e5 kiaN2; chit8-e5 mia5-kio3 Hoat-lek8, in-ui7 ti7 i hit-si5 toe7 chiu7 hun-kai3; Hoat-lek8 e5 sio2-ti7 mia5-kio3 Iok-tan.  26). Iok-tan siN A-mou5-tap, Sa-liat8, Hap-sat-ma2-hui, Ia5-lah8;  27). Hap-to-lan5, OU-sat, Tek-lah8;  28). Go5-pa-lou7, A-pi2-ma2-li7, Si7-pa;  29). O-hui2, Hap-hui-lah8, Iok-pa; chiah-e5 long2 si7 Iok-tan e5 kiaN2.  30). In sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 toe7-hng si7 tui3 Bi2-sa kau3 Se-hoat tang--si3 e5 soaN.  31). Che chiu7-si7 Siam2 e5 kiaN2-sun, kok chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, in e5 khiuN-khau2, ti7 in e5 thou2-toe7, chiau3 in e5 pang-kok.
	32). Chiah-e5 long2 si7 Na2-a e5 kiaN2 e5 chong-chok8, kok chiau3 in e5 se3-he7, in e5 pang-kok; toa7-chui2 i2-au7, in ti7 toe7-chiuN7 pun-choe3 pang-kok.

[11]	Hit-si5 thiN-e7 e5 khau2-im, gian5-gu2, long2 chit8-iuN7.  2). In soa2--khi3 tang--si3 e5 si5-chun7, ti7 Si7-na2 toe7 tu2-tioh8 chit8-phian3 e5 piN5-iuN5, chiu7 toa3 ti7-hia.  3). In tai7-ke chham-siong5 kong2, Lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 choe3 chng, sio hou7 i sek8.  In u7 chng thang thoe3 chioh8, koh u7 chioh8-iu5 thang thoe3 he-thou5.  4). Koh kong2, Lai5 ah, lan2 tioh8 khi2 siaN5 kap thah, thah-teng2 tu2-thiN, ui7 lan2 lip8 chit8 e5 mia5, bian2-tit lan2 si3-soaN3 ti7 choan5-toe7.
	5). Ia5-ho5-hoa kang3-lim5, beh khoaN3 se3-kan lang5 sou2 khi2 e5 siaN5 kap thah.  6). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, KhoaN3 ah, chiah e5 peh-siN3 long2 hap8-it, gian5-gu2 iah8 chit8-iuN7; hian7-kim i2-keng khi2-chhiu2 choe3 chit e5 su7; i2-au7 in sou2 beh choe3 e5, bo5 chit8-hang7 oe7 kim3-chi2.  7). Lai5 ah, lan2 loh8--lai5-khi3, ti7-hia phah-loan7 in e5 khau2-im, hou7 in e5 gian5-gu2 tai7-ke boe7 siong-thong.  8). Tui3 an2-ni, Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 in tui3-hia si3-soaN3 ti7 choan5-toe7; in chiu7 theng5-kang, bo5 khi2 hit e5 siaN5.  9). Sou2-i2 hit e5 siaN5 mia5-kio3 Pa-piat8, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7-hia phah-loan7 thiN-e7 e5 gian5-gu2; Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 lang5 tui3-hia si3-soaN3 ti7 choan5-toe7-chiuN7.
	10). Siam2 e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Siam2 chit8-pah he3, toa7-chui2 i2-au7 nng7-ni5 siN A-hoat-sat.  11). Siam2 siN A-hoat-sat liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 gou7-pah ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	12). A-hoat-sat saN-chap8 gou7 he3 siN Sa-lah8.  13). A-hoat-sat siN Sa-lah8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 si3-pah lian5 saN ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	14). Sa-lah8 saN-chap8 he3 siN Hi-pek.  15). Sa-lah8 siN Hi-pek liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 si3-pah lian5 saN ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	16). Hi-pek saN-chap8-si3 he3 siN Hoat-lek8 .  17). Hi-pek siN Hoat-lek8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 si3-pah saN-chap8 ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	18). Hoat-lek8 saN-chap8 he3 siN Lah8-ngou5.  19). Hoat-lek8 siN Lah8-ngou5 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 nng7-pah lian5 kau2 ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	20). Lah8-ngou5 saN-chap8 ji7 he3 siN Se-lok8.  21). Lah8-ngou5 siN Se-lok8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 nng7-pah lian5 chhit ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	22). Se-lok8 saN-chap8 he3 siN Na2-hok8.  23). Se-lok8 siN Na2-hok8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 nng7-pah ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	24). Na2-hok8 ji7-chap8 kau2 he3 siN Tha-lah8.  25). Na2-hok8 siN Tha-lah8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 chit8-pah chap8-kau2 ni5, koh u7 siN kiaN2 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	26). Tha-lah8 chhit-chap8 he3 siN A-pek-lan5, Na2-hok8, Hap-lan5.
	27). Tha-lah8 e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Tha-lah8 siN A-pek-lan5, Na2-hok8, Hap-lan5; Hap-lan5 siN Lo5-tek.  28). Hap-lan5 si2 ti7 i e5 lau7-pe7 Tha-lah8 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 i e5 pun2-toe7 Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 JiN2 siaN5.  29). A-pek-lan5, Na2-hok8, kok u7 chhoa7-bou2.  A-pek-lan5 e5 bou2 mia5 kio3 Sat-lai7; Na2-hok8 e5 bou2 mia5-kio3 Bit8-ka, si7 Hap-lan5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; Hap-lan5 si7 Bit8-ka e5 lau7-pe7, iah8 si7 I2-su7-ka e5 lau7-pe7.  30). Sat-lai7 bo5 hoai5-in7, bo5 kiaN2.
	31). Tha-lah8 chhoa7 i e5 kiaN2 A-pek-lan5, kap i e5 sun Lo5-tek, chiu7-si7 Hap-lan5 e5 kiaN2, i2-kip8 i e5 sim-pu7 Sat-lai7, chiu7-si7 i e5 kiaN2 A-pek-lan5 e5 bou2, in saN-kap chhut Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 JiN2 siaN5; beh khi3 Ka-lam5 toe7; in kau3 Hap-lan5 chiu7 toa3 ti7-hia.  32). Tha-lah8 hiong2-siu7 nng7-pah lian5 gou7 he3; Tha-lah8 si2 ti7 Hap-lan5.

[12]	Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Li2 tioh8 li7-khui pun2-toe7, pun2-chok8, lau7-pe7 e5 ke, khi3 Goa2 sou2 beh chi2-si7 li2 e5 toe7.  2). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 chiaN5-choe3 toa7-kok, Goa2 beh su3-hok li2, hou7 li2 e5 mia5 choe3 toa7, li2 iah8 beh hou7 lang5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3;  3). chiok-hok li2--e5, Goa2 beh su3-hok hou7 in; chiu3-chou2 li2--e5, Goa2 beh chek-hoat8 i; toe7-chiuN7 ban7-chok8 beh in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  4). A-pek-lan5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 e5 oe7, chiu7 khi3; Lo5-tek iah8 kap i khi3.  A-pek-lan5 chhut Hap-lan5 e5 si5 chhit-chap8-gou7 he3.  5). A-pek-lan5 toa3 i e5 bou2 Sat-lai7, kap i e5 tit8-a2 Lo5-tek; i2-kip8 in ti7 Hap-lan5 sou2 chek-chu7 e5 chai5-but8, sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 lang5-giah8; in chiu7 chhut-khi3, beh khi3 Ka-lam5 toe7; in chiu7 kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7.  6). A-pek-lan5 keng-ke3 hit e5 toe7, kau3 ti7 Si7-kiam3 e5 sou2-chai7, kau3 Mou5-li2 e5 siong7-chhiu7; hit-si5 Ka-lam5 chok8 iau2 teh toa3.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 chhut-hian7 kong2, Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 toe7-hng siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hou7-e3; i chiu7 ti7-hia ui7-tioh8 tui3 i chhut-hian7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5.  8). Tui3 hia i soa2 kau3 Pek-tek8-li7 tang--si3 e5 soaN, tah pou3-piN5; sai--si3 si7 Pek-tek8-li7, tang--si3 si7 Ai; ti7-hia ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.  9). A-pek-lan5 chiam7-chiam7 soa2--khi3 lam5--si3 e5 toe7.
	10). Hit e5 toe7 tu2-tioh8 ki-hng, A-pek-lan5 loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8, beh ti7-hia chiam7-si5 khia7-khi2; in-ui7 hit e5 toe7 ki-hng chin toa7.  11). Chiong-kun7 jip8 Ai-kip8, chiu7 tui3 i e5 bou2 Sat-lai7 kong2, Goa2 chai li2 si7 bin7-mau7 ho2-khoaN3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5;  12). Ai-kip8 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 si5 beh kong2, Chit-e5 si7 i e5 bou2, in beh thai5-si2 goa2, lai5 lau5 li2 oah8--teh.  13). Kiu5 li2 tioh8 kong2, li2 si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7, hou7 goa2 in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8 peng5-an; goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 iah8 tui3 li2 lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8.  14). A-pek-lan5 kau3 Ai-kip8 e5 si5, Ai-kip8 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kek8-ki5 sui2.  15). Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5 khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 o-lo2 i; hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 hou7 lang5 toa3 i jip8 Hoat-lo2 e5 ong5-kiong.  16). Hoat-lo2 in-ui7 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 ho2 khoan2-thai7 A-pek-lan5; A-pek-lan5 chiu7 tit-tioh8 iuN5, gu5, kang e5 lu5, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, bu2 e5 lu5, i2-kip8 lok8-to5.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa in-ui7 A-pek-lan5 e5 bou2 Sat-lai7 e5 ian5-kou3, kang3 toa7 chai-e7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 kap i choan5-ke.  18). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 kio3 A-pek-lan5 lai5 kong2, Li2 tui3 goa2 sou2-choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? siaN2-su7 bo5 ka7 goa2 kong2 i si7 li2 e5 bou2?  19). SiaN2-su7 chheng i choe3 sio2-be7? ti3-kau3 goa2 chiong i chhoa7 lai5 choe3 goa2 e5 bou2; taN li2 e5 bou2 ti7-chia, thang chhoa7 i, choe3 li2 khi2.  20). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Hoat-lo2 ui7-tioh8 i lai5 hoan-hu3 lang5; in chiu7 chiong i kap i e5 bou2 kap i sou2-u7--e5, long2 sang3 i khi3.

[13]	A-pek-lan5 tui3 Ai-kip8 chiuN7--khi3, i kap i e5 bou2 kap i sou2-u7--e5, lian5 Lo5-tek, long2 khi3 Lam5-toe7.  2). A-pek-lan5 e5 gu5, gun5, kim chin-choe7.  3). I tui3 Lam5-toe7 chiam7-chiam7 khi3 Pek-tek8-li7, kau3 Pek-tek8-li7 kap Ai e5 tiong-kan, cha2-cheng5 tah pou3-piN5 e5 sou2-chai7;  4). kau3 i khi2-thau5 khi2 toaN5 e5 sou2-chai7; A-pek-lan5 ti7-hia kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.  5). Kap A-pek-lan5 tang5 kiaN5 e5 Lo5-tek iah8 u7 iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, pou3-piN5.  6). Hit e5 toe7 chiu7 boe7 iong5-un2--tit in saN-kap khia7; in-ui7 in e5 chai5-but8 choe7, in chiah boe7-oe7 saN-kap khia7.  7). A-pek-lan5 e5 bok8-chia2 kap Lo5-tek e5 bok8-chia2 saN-chiN; tng-si5 Ka-lam5 lang5 kap Pi2-li7-se2 lang5 ti7 hit e5 toe7 khia7-khi2.  8). A-pek-lan5 ka7 Lo5-tek kong2, Li2 goa2 m7-thang oan-ke, li2 e5 bok8-chia2 kap goa2 e5 bok8-chia2 iah8 m7-thang oan-ke; in-ui7 lan2 si7 kut-jiok8 e5 chhin.  9). Choan5-toe7 kiam2 bo5 ti7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 mah? chhiaN2 li2 li7-khui goa2; li2 to3-peng5, goa2 chiu7 chiaN3-peng5; li2 chiaN3-peng5, goa2 chiu7 to3-peng5.  10). Lo5-tek kiah8-bak8 khoaN3 Iok-tan3 ho5 it-phian3 e5 PiN5-iuN5, tit8-kau3 So2-jiN2 e5 lou7, long2 chin lun7-tek8; hit e5 toe7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa be7 biat8 Sou2-to-ma2 Go5-mou5-lah8 i2-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hng5, iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 Ai-kip8 e5 toe7.  11). Tui3 an2-ni Lo5-tek keng2 Iok-tan3 ho5 it-phian3 e5 PiN5-iuN5, chhian-soa2 khi3 tang--si3; in chiu7 tai7-ke pun-khui.  12). A-pek-lan5 khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 toe7, Lo5-tek khia7-khi2 PiN5-iuN5 chiah e5 siaN5; soa2 i e5 pou3-piN5 kau3 Sou2-to-ma2.  13). Sou2-to-ma2 lang5 kek8-phaiN2, toa7-toa7 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.
	14). Lo5-tek li7-piat8 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Li2 kiah8-bak8, tui3 li2 sou2 tiam3 e5 sou2-chai7, ng3 tang sai lam5 pak lai5 khoaN3;  15). in-ui7 li2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 it-chhe3 e5 toe7, Goa2 long2 beh hou7 li2, kap li2 e5 hou7-e3, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2.  16). Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 chhin-chhiuN7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thou5-soa; lang5 na7 oe7 sng3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thou5-soa, chiah oe7 sng3 li2 e5 hou7-e3.  17). Li2 khi2-lai5 pian3-kiaN5 chit e5 toe7 e5 hoaiN5-tit8, in-ui7 Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 hou7 li2.  18). A-pek-lan5 chiu7 poaN-soa2 pou3-piN5 kau3 Hi-pek-lun5, oa2 Ban7-li7 hiah e5 siong7-chhiu7 khia7-khi2; ti7-hia ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5.

[14]	Tng Am3-lah8-hui choe3 Si7-na2 ong5, A-liok8 choe3 I2-lah8-sat ong5, Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2 choe3 I2-lan5 ong5, The5-tat8 choe3 Ko-in3 ong5 e5 si5,  2). in lai5 kong-kek Sou2-to-ma2 ong5 Pi2-lah8, Go5-mou5-lah8 ong5 Pi2-sa, Ap-ma2 ong5 Si7-lap8, Se2-phian ong5 Si7-bi2-piat8, i2-kip8 Pi2-lah8 ong5 (Pi2-lah8 chiu7-si7 So2-jiN2).  3). In long2 chu7-hoe7 ti7 Se-teng5 e5 soaN-kok; Se-teng5 soaN-kok chiu7-si7 Iam5-hai2.  4). In hok8-sai7 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2 chap8-ji7 ni5 ku2; kau3 chap8-saN--ni5 poe7-poan7.  5). Chap8-si3--ni5 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2, kap tang5 hoe7-beng5 chiah e5 ong5, long2 lai5, ti7 A-tek8-lut8-ka-leng5 thai5-iaN5 Li2-hoat8-im lang5, ti7 Ham5 Sou-se lang5, ti7 Sa-bi5-ki-liat8-teng5 I2-bi2 lang5,  6). ti7 Ho5-li7 lang5 e5 Se-jiN2 soaN Ho5-li7 lang5, kau3 kun7 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 I2-lek8-pa-lan5.  7). In to3-tng2 kau3 An-bit8-pa, chiu7-si7 Ka-te-su, kong-kek A-ma2-lek8 choan5-toe7, kap khia7-khi2 ti7 Hap-se2-sun7-tha-ma2 e5 A-mou5-li7 lang5.  8). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Sou2-to-ma2 ong5, Go5-mou5-lah8 ong5, Ap-ma2 ong5, Se2-phian ong5, Pi2-lah8 ong5, (Pi2-lah8 chiu7-si7 So2-jiN2), long2 chhut-lai5 ti7 Se-teng5 e5 soaN-kok pai5-tin7, kap in kau-chian3;  9). chiu7-si7 kap I2-lan5 ong5 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2, Ko-in3 ong5 The5-tat8, Si7-na2 ong5 Am3-lah8-hui, I2-lah8-sat ong5 A-liok8 kau-chian3; si3 e5 ong5 tui3-tek8 gou7 e5 ong5.  10). Se-teng5 soaN-kok long2 si7 chioh8-iu5 khiN; Sou2-to-ma2 Go5-mou5-lah8 chiah e5 ong5 to5-chau2, poah8 ti7-hia; ki5-u5--e5 chau2 chiuN7-soaN.  11). In chiu7 chiong Sou2-to-ma2 Go5-mou5-lah8 e5 chai5-but8, i2-kip8 in e5 kan-niu5 long2 chhiuN2, choe3 in khi3.  12). Koh chiong A-pek-lan5 e5 tit8 Lo5-tek, kap i e5 chai5-but8 chhiuN2-khi3; hit-si5 Lo5-tek toa3 ti7 Sou2-to-ma2.
	13). U7 chit8 e5 to5-chau2 e5 lang5 lai5 ka7 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 A-pek-lan5 kong2; hit-si5 A-pek-lan5 khia7-khi2 ti7 A-mou5-li7 lang5 Ban7-li7 e5 siong7-chhiu7 hit sou2-chai7, Ban7-li7 kap I2-sit8-kok kap A-nai2 long2 si7 hiaN-ti7, u7 kap A-pek-lan5 lian5-beng5.  14). A-pek-lan5 thiaN-kiN3 i e5 tit8 hou7 lang5 liah8--khi3, chiu7 chhoa7 seng-iong2 ti7 i e5 ke--nih cheng-lian7 e5 chong3-teng, saN-pah chap8-poeh lang5, tui-jip kau3 Tan3.  15). I kap i e5 lou5-pok8 thau3-mi5 pun-tui7, kong-kek--in; tui kau3 Tai7-ma2-sek to3-peng5 e5 Ho5-pa.  16). Chiong it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8 chhiuN2 to3-tng2, lian5 i e5 tit8-a2 Lo5-tek kap i e5 chai5-but8, i2-kip8 hu7-lu2 peh-siN3, iah8 long2 chhiuN2 to3-tng2.
	17). A-pek-lan5 thai5-iaN5 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2, i2-kip8 kap i choe3-tin7 chiah e5 ong5, to3--lai5 e5 si5, Sou2-to-ma2 ong5 chhut-lai5, kau3 Sa-bi2 e5 soaN-kok, ngia5-chih i; Sa-bi2 e5 soaN-kok chiu7-si7 Ong5 e5 soaN-kok.  18). Iah8 u7 Sat-leng2 ong5 Bek8-ki-se2-tek toa3 piaN2 kap chiu2 chhut-lai5; i si7 Chi3-koaiN5 Siong7-te3 e5 che3-si;  19). chiok-hok i kong2, Goan7 thiN-toe7 e5 Chu2, Chi3-koaiN5 e5 Siong7-te3 su3-hok A-pek-lan5.  20). Chi3-koaiN5 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong tui3-tek8 kau ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, eng-kai o-lo2 I.  A-pek-lan5 chiong long2-chong2 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5, chap8-hun7 theh8 chit8-hun7 hou7 i.  21). Sou2-to-ma2 ong5 ka7 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Chiong lang5 kui goa2; mih8 long2 hou7 li2.  22). A-pek-lan5 ka7 Sou2-to-ma2 ong5 kong2, Goa2 u7 ki2 thiN-toe7 e5 Chu2 Chi3-koaiN5 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 chiu3-choa7,  23). hoan7-na7 li2 e5 mih8, chiu7 chit8 tiau5 soaN3 chit8 tiau5 oe5-toa3, goa2 long2 m7-theh8, bian2-tit li2 kong2, Goa2 hou7 A-pek-lan5 ho2-giah8;  24). chi2-u7 siau3-lian5 lang5 sou2 chiah8 e5, i2-kip8 kap goa2 tang5-kiaN5 e5 lang5 A-nai2, I2-sit8-kok, Ban7-li7, sou2 eng3-tit e5 hun7-giah8, thang chhut-chai7 in theh8.

[15]	Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 ti7 iN7-siong7-tiong lim5-kau3 A-pek-lan5, kong2, A-pek-lan5 ah, li2 m7-bian2 kiaN, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 tin5-pai5, si7 li2 kek8-toa7 e5 po3-siuN2.  2). A-pek-lan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh hou7 goa2 sim2-mih8, goa2 i2-keng bo5 kiaN2; seng5-chiap goa2 e5 ke-giap8--e5, chiu7-si7 Tai7-ma2-sek lang5 I2-li7-i2-sia7?  3). A-pek-lan5 koh kong2, Li2 bo5 hou7 goa2 u7 hou7-e3, hit e5 siN ti7 goa2 ke-lai7--e5 si7 goa2 e5 hou7-su5.  4). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh lim5-kau3, ka7 i kong2, Chit-lang5 m7-si7 beh choe3 li2 e5 hou7-su5; tui3 li2 pun2-sin chhut--e5, chiah si7 choe3 li2 e5 hou7-su5.  5). Chiu7 chhoa7 i chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 kong2, Li2 khoaN3 thiN, sng3 hiah e5 chhiN, li2 sng3 oe7 liau2 a2-boe7; koh tui3 i kong2, Li2 e5 hou7-e3 iah8 beh chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni.  6). A-pek-lan5 sin3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; I chiu7 ka7 i sng3 choe3 gi7.  7). Koh tui3 i kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bat chhoa7 li2 chhut Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 JiN2 siaN5, ui7-tioh8 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 hou7 li2 choe3-giap8.  8). A-pek-lan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 oe7 chai beh tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8 ah?  9). I ka7 i kong2, Li2 ka7 Goa2 chhu2 chit8-chiah saN-ni5 bu2 e5 gu5, chit8-chiah saN-ni5 bu2 e5 soaN-iuN5, chit8-chiah saN-ni5 kang e5 mi5-iuN5, chit8-chiah ka-chui, chit8-chiah chiN2-a2.  10). I chiu7 chhu2 chiah e5 mih8 lai5, tak8-iuN7 tui3-tiong phoa3-khui choe3 nng7-peng5, chit-peng5 kap hit-peng5 pai5 saN-tui3; chi2-u7 chiau2 bo5 phoa3-khui.  11). U7 eng-chiau2 loh8--lai5 ti7 si2 e5 cheng-siN e5 teng2-bin7; A-pek-lan5 chiu7 koaN2 i khi3.  12). Jit8 beh loh8 e5 si5, A-pek-lan5 khun3 tang7-bin5; hut-jian5 u7 chin ou-am3 e5 toa7 kiaN-hiaN5 kau3 ti7 i.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Li2 tek-khak tioh8 chai, li2 e5 hou7-e3 beh chhut-goa7 ti7 pat8-lang5 e5 toe7, koh hok8-sai7 hit-ui7 e5 lang5; hit-ui7 e5 lang5 beh khou2-chhou2 in si3-pah ni5.  14). In sou2 beh hok8-sai7 e5 kok, Goa2 beh pan7 in; au7-lai5 in beh toa3 choe7-choe7 chai5-but8 tui3-hia chhut-lai5.  15). Li2 beh an-jian5 to3-chou2, chiah8 tng5-he3-siu7, hou7 lang5 bai5-chong3.  16). Kau3 te7-si3 tai7, in beh to3--lai5 chia; in-ui7 A-mou5-li7 chok8 e5 choe7 iau2-be7 koan3-boan2.  17). Jit8-loh8 thiN-am3, u7 chhut ian e5 lou5, kap teh-toh8 e5 he2-pe2, tui3 hiah e5 phoa3-peng5 e5 bah keng-ke3.  18). Tng hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap A-pek-lan5 lip8-iok, kong2, Goa2 u7 chiong chit e5 toe7, tui3 Ai-kip8 ho5 kau3 hit e5 toa7-ho5, chiu7-si7 Pek-lat ho5, hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3;  19). chiu7-si7 Ki-ni5, Ki-ni5-se2, Kah-mou5-ni5,  20). Hek, Pi2-li7-se2, Li2-hoat8-im,  21). A-mou5-li7, Ka-lam5, Kek-ka-sat, Ia5-pou3-su, chiah e5 chok8 e5 toe7.

[16]	A-pek-lan5 e5 bou2 Sat-lai7 bo5 ka7 i siN-kiaN2; i u7 chit8 e5 lu2-pi7 mia5 Ha7-kah; si7 Ai-kip8 lang5.  2). Sat-lai7 ka7 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kim3 goa2 siN-kiaN2; chhiaN2 li2 kap goa2 e5 lu2-pi7 tang5-pang5; kiam2-chhai2 goa2 thang tui3 i tit-tioh8 gin2-a2.  A-pek-lan5 thiaN-than3 Sat-lai7 e5 oe7.  3). Tui3 hit-tiap8 A-pek-lan5 e5 bou2 Sat-lai7 chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Ai-kip8 lang5 Ha7-kah hou7 i tiong7-hu A-pek-lan5 choe3-bou2; hit-si5 A-pek-lan5 i2-keng toa3 Ka-lam5 chap8 ni5.  4). I kap Ha7-kah tang5-pang5, Ha7-kah chiu7 hoai5-in7; i chai ka-ki7 u7-sin, chiu7 khoaN3-khin chu2-bu2.  5). Sat-lai7 ka7 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Goa2 e5 oan-ong2 kui ti7 li2; goa2 chiong goa2 e5 lu2-pi7 he7 ti7 li2 e5 sim-hoai5-tiong; i khoaN3 ka-ki7 u7-sin, chiu7 khoaN3-khin goa2; goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan phoaN3-toan3.  6). A-pek-lan5 tui3 Sat-lai7 kong2, Li2 e5 lu2-pi7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, li2 thang sui5-i3 khoan2-thai7 i.  Sat-lai7 khou2-chhou2 i, i chiu7 tui3 Sat-lai7 e5 bin7-cheng5 to5-chau2.  7). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tu2-tioh8 i ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 chui2-choaN5-piN; hit e5 chui2-choaN5 ti7 Su-jiN2 e5 lou7-chiuN7.  8). Tui3 i kong2, Sat-lai7 e5 lu2-pi7 Ha7-kah, li2 tui3 tah-loh8 lai5? beh tah-loh8 khi3? I kong2, Goa2 tui3 goa2 e5 chu2-bu2 Sat-lai7 e5 bin7-cheng5 chau2--chhut-lai5.  9). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tui3 i kong2, Li2 to3--khi3 li2 e5 chu2-bu2 hia, hang5-hok8 ti7 i e5 chhiu2-e7.  10). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 koh tui3 i kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 kek8-ki5 choe7, sim7-chi3 boe7-sng3--tit.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 koh tui3 i kong2, Li2 taN hoai5-in7, beh siN chit8 e5 kiaN2, tioh8 ka7 i ho7 mia5 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 li2 e5 khou2-cheng5.  12). I choe3 lang5 beh chhin-chhiuN7 ia2-lu5, i e5 chhiu2 beh kong-kek cheng3-lang5, cheng3-lang5 e5 chhiu2 beh kong-kek i; i beh khia7-khi2 ti7 cheng3 hiaN-ti7 e5 thau5-cheng5.  13). Ha7-kah chiu7 chheng hit e5 tui3 i kong2 oe7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5 kong2, Li2 si7 khoaN3-kiN3 tak8-hang7 e5 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 kong2, Lian5 ti7-chia goa2 iah8 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 mah?  14). Sou2-i2 chit e5 chiN2 mia5-kio3 Pi2-jiN2-lah8-hai2-lai5, chiu7-si7 Ka-te-su kap Pa-liat8 e5 tiong-kan.  15). Au7-lai5 Ha7-kah ka7 A-pek-lan5 siN chit8 e5 kiaN2; A-pek-lan5 ka7 i e5 kiaN2 ho7 mia5 kio3 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, chiu7-si7 Ha7-kah sou2 siN--e5.  16). Ha7-kah ka7 A-pek-lan5 siN I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 si5, A-pek-lan5 poeh-chap8-lak8 he3.

[17]	A-pek-lan5 kau2-chap8-kau2 he3 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 hian2-hian7, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 si7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3, li2 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kiaN5-choe3 tioh8 oan5-choan5.  2). Goa2 beh kap li2 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 kek8-ki5 choe7.  3). A-pek-lan5 chiu7 phak-loh8 ti7 toe7--nih; Siong7-te3 koh kap i kong2-oe7, kong2,  4). Goa2 kap li2 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, li2 beh choe3 choe7-choe7 kok e5 pe7.  5). Tui3 taN i2-au7, li2 e5 mia5 bo5 koh kio3-choe3 A-pek-lan5, si7 beh kio3-choe3 A-pek-lah8-han2, in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng lip8 li2 choe3 choe7-choe7 kok e5 pe7.  6). Goa2 beh hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 kek8-ki5 choe7, kok-tou7 tui3 li2 lai5 lip8, kun-ong5 tui3 li2 lai5 chhut.  7). Goa2 beh kap li2, i2-kip8 li2 lek8-tai7 e5 hou7-e3, siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 iok; si7 beh choe3 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 e5 Siong7-te3.  8). Goa2 beh chiong li2 hian7-chai7 chhut-goa7 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Ka-lam5 choan5-toe7, siuN2-su3 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 giap8; Goa2 iah8 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3.  9). Siong7-te3 koh tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 tioh8 lek8-tai7 chun-siu2 Goa2 e5 iok.  10). Lin2 tiong-kan sou2 u7 e5 ta-pou--e5, long2 tioh8 siu7 kat-le2; che chiu7-si7 Goa2 kap li2 i2-kip8 li2 e5 hou7-e3 sou2 lip8 e5 iok, si7 lin2 sou2 tioh8 chun-siu2--e5.  11). Lin2 tioh8 koah lin2 iong5-but8 e5 phe5; che si7 beh choe3 Goa2 kap lin2 sou2 lip8 e5 iok e5 ki3-ho7.  12). Lin2 lek8-tai7 e5 ta-pou--e5, bo5-lun7 ke-lai7 siN--e5, a2-si7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 i2-goa7, eng7 gun5 tui3 goa7-bin7 lang5 boe2--e5, i2-keng chhut-si3 poeh-jit8, long2 tioh8 siu7 kat-le2.  13). Li2 ke-lai7 siN--e5, kap li2 eng7 gun5 boe2--e5, long2 tek-khak tioh8 siu7 kat-le2; an2-ni Goa2 e5 iok beh he7 ti7 lin2 e5 sin-chiuN7, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  14). Bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 ta-pou--e5, i sin-khu ki3-jian5 bo5 siu7 kat-le2, si7 poe7 Goa2 e5 iok; tek-khak tui3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan tu5--khi3.
	15). Siong7-te3 koh tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 e5 bou2 Sat-lai7, m7-thang koh kio3 i e5 mia5 Sat-lai7; i e5 mia5 beh kio3-choe3 Sat-lah8.  16). Goa2 beh su3-hok i, Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 li2 tui3 i tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 kiaN2; Goa2 beh su3-hok i, i iah8 beh choe3 liat8-kok e5 lau7-bu2; beh u7 pang-kok e5 ong5 tui3 i chhut.  17). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 phak--teh chhio3, sim-lai7 kong2, Chit8-pah he3 e5 lang5 iau2 oe7 siN-kiaN2 mah? Sat-lah8 i2-keng kau2-chap8 he3, iau2 oe7 seng-iong2 mah?  18). A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Siong7-te3 kong2, Tan7 goan7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 oah8 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  19). Siong7-te3 kong2, M7-si7 lah, li2 e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 beh ka7 li2 siN chit8 e5 kiaN2, li2 beh ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 I2-sat; Goa2 beh kap i siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, choe3 i e5 hou7-e3 eng2-oan2 e5 iok.  20). Lun7-kau3 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, Goa2 iah8 thiaN li2 kiu5; li2 khoaN3, Goa2 i2-keng su3-hok i, beh hou7 i heng-ong7, ke-thiN kek8-ki5 choe7.  I beh siN chap8-ji7 e5 chok8-tiuN2, Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 toa7-kok.  21). Kau3 me5-ni5 chit-si5, Sat-lah8 beh ka7 li2 siN I2-sat; Goa2 beh kap i siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok.  22). Siong7-te3 kap A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2 soah, chiu7 li7-khui i chiuN7--khi3.  23). Tu2-tu2 hit-jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 chiau3 Siong7-te3 sou2 ka7 i kong2--e5, ka7 i e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, kap A-pek-lah8-han2 ke-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 ta-pou-lang5, bo5-lun7 ti7 ke--nih siN--e5, a2-si7 eng7 i e5 gun5 boe2--e5, long2 kiaN5 kat-le2.  24). A-pek-lah8-han2 siu7 kat-le2 e5 si5 kau2-chap8-kau2 he3;  25). i e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 siu7 kat-le2 e5 si5 chap8-saN he3.  26). Tu2-tu2 hit jit8 A-pek-lah8-han2 kap i e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 tang5 siu7 kat-le2.  27). Ke-lai7 sou2-u7 e5 lang5, bo5-lun7 ti7 ke--nih siN--e5, a2-si7 eng7 gun5 tui3 goa7-bin7 lang5 boe2--e5, long2 kap i tang5 siu7 kat-le2.

[18]	Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ban7-li7 e5 siong7-chhiu7 hia, tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 chhut-hian7; hit-si5 jit8 tng joah8; A-pek-lah8-han2 che7 ti7 pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2;  2). kiah8-bak8 khi2-lai5 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 saN lang5 ti7 tui3-bin7 teh khia7; i chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 tui3 pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2, chau2 khi3 ngia5-chih in,  3). phak ti7 toe7--nih, kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2, goa2 na7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, kiu5 li2 m7-thang li7-khui lou5-pok8 choe3 li2 khi3;  4). iong5-un2 theh8 tam7-poh8 chui2, hou7 lin2 soe2-kha; chhiaN2 hioh-khun3 ti7 chhiu7-kha;  5). goa2 koh theh8 tam7-poh8 piaN2, hou7 lin2 tiam2-sim; jian5-au7 chin3-cheng5 khi3; in-ui7 lin2 si7 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, chiah kau3 lin2 e5 lou5-pok8 chia.  In kong2, Thang chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 khi3 kiaN5.  6). A-pek-lah8-han2 koaN2-kin2 jip8 pou3-piN5, kiN3 Sat-lah8 kong2, Li2 kin2-kin2 eng7 saN se3-a e5 mi7-hun2, noa2 choe3 piaN2.  7). A-pek-lah8-han2 koh chau2 kau3 gu5-kun5 e5 sou2-chai7, khan chit8 chiah chiN2 koh ho2 e5 gu5-a2 lai5; kau hou7 lou5-pok8, i chiu7 koaN2-kin2 khi3 pi7-pan7.  8). A-pek-lah8-han2 koh theh8 lin-iu5 kap lin, kap sou2 pi7-pan7 e5 gu5-a2 lai5, pai5 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5; ka-ki7 ti7 chhiu7-kha khia7 ti7 in e5 sin-piN; in chiu7 chiah8.  9). In ka7 i kong2, Li2 e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 ti7 tah-loh8? I kong2, Ti7 pou3-piN5-lai7.  10). In tiong-kan chit8-e5 kong2, Kau3-ki5 Goa2 tek-khak beh koh lai5 li2 chia; li2 e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 beh siN chit8 e5 kiaN2.  Sat-lah8 ti7 au7-bin7, pou3-piN5 mng5-khau2, teh thiaN.  11). A-pek-lah8-han2 kap Sat-lah8 ni5-he3 i2-keng lau7; Sat-lah8 e5 geh8-keng i2-keng choat8.  12). Sat-lah8 sim-lai7 chhio3 kong2, Goa2 i2-keng soe-lam2, goa2 e5 chu2 iah8 lau7--lah; kiam2 iau2 u7 chit-ho7 e5 hoaN-hi2?  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Sat-lah8 ui7 siaN2-su7 chhio3, kong2, Goa2 i2-keng lau7, ko2-chin oe7 siN-kiaN2 mah?  14). Kiam2 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7 choe3-boe7-lai5 e5 su7 mah? Kau3-ki5, me5-ni5 chit-si5, Goa2 beh koh lai5 li2 chia, Sat-lah8 beh siN chit8 e5 kiaN2.  15). Sat-lah8 kiaN, m7-jin7, kong2, Goa2 bo5 chhio3.  Hit-lang5 kong2, Bo5-iaN2; li2 sit8-chai7 u7 chhio3.
	16). Hiah e5 lang5 chiu7 tui3 hia khi2--lai5, ng3 Sou2-to-ma2 khi3; A-pek-lah8-han2 ia7 kap in saN-kap kiaN5, beh sang3 in chit8-cham7.  17). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 sou2 beh choe3 e5 su7, kiam2 thang tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 un2-khng3 mah?  18). In-ui7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tek-khak beh chiaN5-choe3 kiong5-toa7 e5 kok, toe7-chiuN7 ban7-kok beh in-ui7 i lai5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  19). Goa2 bat i, si7 beh hou7 i beng7-leng7 i e5 kiaN2 kap i e5 ke-koan3; hou7 in tng5-tng5 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to7-li2, peng2-kong kiaN5-gi7; ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chi2 A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, long2 kui hou7 i.  20). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Sou2-to-ma2, Go5-mou5-lah8 hoah-hiam3 e5 siaN chin-toa7, in e5 choe7-ok sit8-chai7 tang7.  21). Goa2 taN beh loh8--khi3, khoaN3 in sou2 kiaN5--e5, ko2-jian5 it-chin7 chiau3 Goa2 sou2 thiaN e5 siaN a2 bo5; na7 bo5 an2-ni, Goa2 iah8 oe7 chai.
	22). Hiah e5 lang5 tui3-hia oat8-tng2-sin, ng3 Sou2-to-ma2 khi3; A-pek-lah8-han2 iau2 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.  23). A-pek-lah8-han2 kun7-cheng5 lai5 kong2, Ho2-lang5 kap phaiN2-lang5, Li2 long2 beh chau5-biat8 mah?  24). Siat-su2 siaN5-lai7 u7 gou7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5, Li2 iu5-goan5 beh chau5-biat8 hit sou2-chai7 mah? bo5-beh ui7-tioh8 siaN5-lai7 chi2 gou7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5, lai5 sia3-bian2 in mah?  25). Goan7 Li2 koat-toan3 bo5 an2-ni kiaN5, chiong ho2-lang5 kap phaiN2-lang5 choe3-chit8-e7 hai7-si2; ti3-kau3 ho2-lang5 kap phaiN2-lang5 saN-tang5; goan7 Li2 koat-toan3 bo5 an2-ni kiaN5; sim2-phoaN3 choan5-toe7 e5 Chu2 kiam2 bo5 kiaN5 kong-gi7 mah?  26). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 Sou2-to-ma2 siaN5-lai7 tu2-tioh8 u7 gou7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5, Goa2 chiu7 ui7-tioh8 in e5 ian5-kou3 khoan-iong5 hit sou2-chai7.  27). A-pek-lah8-han2 in3 kong2, Goa2 sui-jian5 si7 he2-hu thou5-hun2, iau2-ku2 kaN2 tui3 Chu2 kong2-oe7;  28). siat-su2 chiah e5 gou7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5 khiam3 gou7-e5; Li2 chiu7 in-ui7 khiam3 gou7-e5, chau5-biat8 choan5-siaN5 mah? I kong2, Goa2 ti7-hia na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 si3-chap8-gou7 e5, iah8 bo5 beh chau5-biat8.  29). A-pek-lah8-han2 koh tui3 I kong2, Siat-su2 ti7-hia tu2-tioh8 si3-chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 si3-chap8-e5 e5 ian5-kou3, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh choe3 chit e5 su7.  30). I koh kong2, Kiu5 Chu2 boh8-tit siu7-khi3, goa2 beh koh kong2; siat-su2 ti7-hia na7 tu2-tioh8 saN-chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Goa2 ti7-hia na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 saN-chap8-e5, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh choe3 chit e5 su7.  31). I kong2, Goa2 iau2-ku2 kaN2 tui3 Chu2 kong2; siat-su2 ti7-hia tu2-tioh8 u7 ji7-chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 ji7-chap8-e5 e5 ian5-kou3, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh chau5-biat8.  32). I kong2, Kiu5 Chu2 boh8-tit siu7-khi3, goa2 koh kong2 chi2 chit8-pai2; siat-su2 ti7-hia tu2-tioh8 u7 chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 chap8-e5 e5 ian5-kou3, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh chau5-biat8.  33). Ia5-ho5-hoa kap A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2 beng5-pek8, chiu7 chiuN7--khi3.  A-pek-lah8-han2 iah8 to3-khi3 i e5 sou2-chai7.

[19]	Jit8-am3, hit nng7 e5 su3-chia2 kau3 Sou2-to-ma2; Lo5-tek che7 ti7 Sou2-to-ma2 siaN5-mng5--nih; Lo5-tek khoaN3-kiN3 in, chiu7 khi2-lai5 ngia5-chih in; kiok-kiong bin7 ng3 toe7,  2). kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, chhiaN2 oat lai5 lou5-pok8 e5 chhu3 hioh-mi5, soe2-kha; bin5-a2-cha2-khi2 khi2-lai5, kiaN5 lin2 e5 lou7.  In kong2, M7-bian2; goan2 beh ti7 toa7 koe-bin7 ke3-mi5.  3). Lo5-tek chhiat-chhiat chhiaN2 in; in chiah oat8-tng2-kha, oat-jip8 i e5 chhu3; Lo5-tek ui7 in pi7-pan7 ian5-siah8, pek bu5-kaN3-piaN2; in chiu7 chiah8.  4). In iau2-be7 khi3 khun3, siaN5-lai7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 Sou2-to-ma2 lang5, tui3 siau3-lian5 kau3 lau7, si3-bin7 lai5 ui5 i e5 chhu3;  5). kio3 Lo5-tek kong2, Kin-am3 kau3 li2 chia e5 lang5 ti7 tah-loh8? hou7 in chhut-lai5, chiau3 goan2 sou2 ai3 choe3.  6). Lo5-tek chhut-khi3 kau3 mng5-goa7, cheng3-lang5 hia, chiu7 chiong mng5 koaiN--teh;  7). kong2, HiaN-ti7 ah, chhiaN2 lin2 boh8-tit choe3 chit-ho7 phaiN2;  8). li2 khoaN3, goa2 u7 nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, iau2 si7 chai7-sek-lu2; iong5-un2 goa2 chhoa7--chhut-lai5, chhut-chai7 lin2 sou2 ai3 lai5 kiaN5; tok8-tok8 chi2 nng7-lang5, i2-keng kau3 goa2 e5 chhu3, m7-thang tui3 in choe3 sim2-mih8.  9). Cheng3-lang5 kong2, Li2 the3--khi3.  Koh kong2, Chit-lang5 kia3-ku ti7-chia, soa3 beh koan2-hat goan2 mah? taN goan2 beh hai7 li2 pi2 hai7 in khah siong-tiong7.  Chiu7 oe-khoeh Lo5-tek, chin3-cheng5 beh kong-phoa3 i e5 mng5.  10). Chong2-si7 hit nng7-lang5 chhun-chhiu2, khan Lo5-tek jip8 chhu3, chiong mng5 koaiN--khi3.  11). Koh hou7 mng5-goa7 e5 lang5, tui3 soe3 kau3 toa7, bak8-chiu ian-ng7, long2 boe7 khoaN3-kiN3; chhe7 kau3 sian7 chhe7 bo5 mng5.
	12). Hit nng7-lang5 tui3 Lo5-tek kong2, Li2 ti7-chia iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 lang5? hek8-si7 kiaN2-sai3, hek8-si7 kiaN2, hek8-si7 cha-bou2-kiaN2, i2-kip8 siaN5-lai7 it-chhe3 siok8 li2 e5 lang5; li2 tioh8 hou7 in long2 chhut chit sou2-chai7.  13). In-ui7 goan2 beh chau5-biat8 chit e5 sou2-chai7, si7 ui7-tioh8 in hoah-hiam3 e5 siaN ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 chin-toa7; Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe goan2 lai5 beh chau5-biat8--i.  14). Lo5-tek chhut-khi3, tui3 chhoa7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 kiaN2-sai3 kong2, Lin2 khi2-lai5, li7-khui chia; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh biat8-bo5 chit e5 siaN5; i e5 kiaN2-sai3 liah8-choe3 i si7 kong2-chhio3.  15). ThiN-kng su3-chia2 chhui-pek Lo5-tek kong2, Khi2--lai5, chhoa7 li2 e5 bou2, i2-kip8 li2 ti7-chia nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 khi3; kiaN-liau2 kap chit e5 siaN5 e5 choe7-ok saN-kap siu7 biat8-bo5.  16). Lo5-tek ian5-chhian5; hit nng7-lang5, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin5-bin2 Lo5-tek, chiu7 khan i e5 chhiu2, kap i e5 bou2 e5 chhiu2, kap i nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 chhiu2, chiong i chhoa7-chhut, an-ti3 ti7 siaN5-goa7.
	17). Chhoa7 in chhut-khi3 liau2, kong2, Li2 tioh8 to5-mia7, m7-thang oat8-thau5 khoaN3, iah8 m7-thang toa3 ti7 PiN5-iuN5; tioh8 chau2--khi3 soaN--nih, kiaN-liau2 siu7 biat8-bo5.  18). Lo5-tek tui3 in kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, m7-thang an2-ni.  19). Li2 khoaN3, li2 e5 lou5-pok8 i2-keng tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 iah8 tui3 goa2 hian2-chhut kek8-toa7 e5 jin5-chu5, kiu3 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7; goa2 boe7-oe7 chau2 kau3 soaN--nih, kiaN-liau2 chit e5 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 goa2, goa2 chiu7 si2.  20). Li2 khoaN3, chit e5 siaN5 kun7-kun7 thang to5-chau2, iah8 si7 soe3; chhiaN2 iong5-un2 goa2 to5-siam2 ti7-hia, lai5 po2-choan5 goa2 e5 oah8-mia7; chit e5 siaN5 kiam2 m7-si7 soe3--e5 mah?  21). I tui3 i kong2, Chit e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 iah8 un2-chun2 li2; li2 sou2 kong2 e5 siaN5, goa2 bo5 beh chhia-to2.  22). Li2 tioh8 kin2-kin2 chau2-khi3 hia; in-ui7 li2 iau2-be7 kau3 hia, goa2 boe7-oe7 choe3 sim2-mih8.  In-ui7 an2-ni hit e5 siaN5 mia5-kio3 So2-jiN2.  23). Lo5-tek kau3 So2-jiN2, jit8 i2-keng chhut.  24). Hit si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiong jiu5-ng5 kap he2, tui3 thiN-teng2, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia, kang3-loh8 ti7 Sou2-to-ma2 kap Go5-mou5-lah8.  25). Chiong hiah e5 siaN5, i2-kip8 choan5 Pi5-iuN5, kap siaN5-lai7 sou2-u7 e5 peh-siN3, lian5 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 seng-tiong2--e5, long2 hui2-hoai7.  26). Lo5-tek e5 bou2 ti7 au7-bin7, chit8-e7 oat8-thau5 khoaN3, chiu7 piN3-choe3 chit8 ki iam5-thiau7.  27). A-pek-lah8-han2 thau3-cha2 khi2--lai5, kau3 i cheng5-jit8 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 hit-ui7;  28). ng3 Sou2-to-ma2 Go5-mou5-lah8, kap PiN5-iuN5 e5 choan5-toe7 lai5 khoaN3; khoaN3-kiN3 hit sou2-chai7 he2-ian chheng3-koaiN5, chhin-chhiuN7 he2-lou5 e5 ian.
	29). Tng Siong7-te3 chau5-biat8 PiN5-iuN5 chiah e5 siaN5 e5 si5, Siong7-te3 siau3-liam7 A-pek-lah8-han2; tu2-tu2 ti7 chhia-to2 Lo5-tek sou2 khia7-khi2 e5 siaN5 e5 si5, chiu7 kah Lo5-tek tui3 chhia-to2 e5 tiong-kan chhut-khi3.
	30). Lo5-tek tiam3 ti7 So2-jiN2 kiaN-hiaN5; chiu7 kap i nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tui3 So2-jiN2 chiuN7--khi3 tiam3 ti7 soaN--nih; i kap nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tiam3 ti7 chit8 e5 tong7-lai7.  31). Toa7 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tui3 soe3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kong2, Lan2 e5 lau7-pe7 lau7--lah, toe7-chiuN7 koh bo5 lang5 kap lan2 choe3 phit-phoe3, lai5 chiau3 jin5-to7.  32). Lai5--lah, thang hou7 lau7-pe7 lim chiu2, kap i saN-kap khun3; an2-ni lan2 ho2 thang tui3 i liu5-chun5 hou7-e3.  33). Hit-mi5 in hou7 lau7-pe7 lim chiu2; toa7 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chiu7 jip8--khi3 kap lau7-pe7 saN-kap khun3; i sim2-mih8 si5 khi3 khun3, sim2-mih8 si5 khi2--lai5, lau7-pe7 long2 m7-chai.  34). Ke3-jit8 toa7 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ka7 soe3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 kong2, Goa2 cha7-mi5 kap lau7-pe7 saN-kap khun3; kin-am3 lan2 koh hou7 i lim chiu2, li2 thang jip8--khi3 kap i saN-kap khun3.  An2-ni, lan2 ho2 thang tui3 lau7-pe7 liu5-chun5 hou7-e3.  35). Hit-mi5 in koh hou7 lau7-pe7 lim chiu2, soe3 cha-bou2-kiaN2 khi2--lai5 khi3 kap i khun3; i sim2-mih8 si5 khi3 khun3, sim2-mih8 si5 khi2--lai5, lau7-pe7 iah8 long2 m7-chai.  36). An2-ni Lo5-tek nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 long2 tui3 in lau7-pe7 lai5 hoai5-in7.  37). Toa7--e5 siN kiaN2, kio3 i e5 mia5 Mou5-ap, chiu7-si7 hian7-kim Mou5-ap lang5 e5 chou2.  38). Soe3--e5 iah8 siN-kiaN2, kio3 i e5 mia5 Pian7-a2-bi2, chiu7-si7 hian7-kim A-bun5 lang5 e5 chou2.

[20]	A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3-hia cham7-cham7 ng3 lam5-hng soa3--khi3; toa3 ti7 Ka-te-su kap Su-jiN2 e5 tiong-kan, kia3-ku ti7 Ki-lah8-jiN2.  2). A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2 kau3 i e5 bou2 Sat-lah8, chiu7 kong2, Si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7; Ki-lah8-jiN2 ong5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chhe lang5 chiong Sat-lah8 chhoa7--khi3.  3). Mi5-si5, bin5-bang7-tiong, Siong7-te3 lai5 ka7 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kong2, Li2 si7 kai si2 e5 lang5, in-ui7 li2 sou2 chhoa7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 si7 lang5 e5 bou2.  4). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 iau2-be7 chhin-kun7 i, chiu7 kong2, Chu2 ah, kiaN5-gi7 e5 peh-siN3, Li2 iah8 beh biat8 i mah?  5). Hit-lang5 kiam2 m7-si7 pun2-sin tui3 goa2 kong2, I si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7 mah? Chiu7 hu7-jin5-lang5 iah8 pun2-sin kong2, I si7 goa2 e5 hiaN; goa2 choe3 chit e5 su7, si7 sim toan-cheng3, chhiu2 chheng-khi3.  6). Siong7-te3 ti7 bang7-tiong tui3 i kong2, Goa2 pun2 chai li2 choe3 chit e5 su7, si7 sim-tiong toan-cheng3; Goa2 chiah chou2-tong3 li2, bian2-tit li2 tek-choe7 Goa2; sou2-i2 Goa2 bo5 iong5-un2 li2 bong--tioh8 i.  7). TaN li2 tioh8 chiong chit lang5 e5 bou2 heng5--i, in-ui7 i si7 sian-ti; i beh thoe3 li2 ki5-to2, li2 chiah oe7 oah8; li2 na7 m7 heng5--i, li2 tioh8 chai, li2 kap li2 sou2 u7 e5 lang5 long2 tit-beh si2.  8). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, kio3 cheng3 lou5-pok8 lai5, chiong chiah e5 tai7-chi3 long2 kong2 hou7 in thiaN; hiah e5 lang5 long2 chin kiaN.  9). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kio3 A-pek-lah8-han2 lai5, tui3 i kong2, Li2 tui3 goan2 sou2 kiaN5--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? goa2 u7 sim2-mih8 tek-choe7 li2, li2 keng2-jian5 hou7 goa2 kap goa2 kok-lai7 e5 lang5 ham7-loh8 tang7-choe7? li2 tui3 goa2 kiaN5 m7 eng-kai kiaN5 e5 su7.  10). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 koh tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8, chiah choe3 chit e5 su7?  11). A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Goa2 phah-sng3 chit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 long2 bo5 kiaN Siong7-te3; in beh ui7-tioh8 goa2 e5 bou2 e5 ian5-kou3 thai5-si2 goa2.  12). Koh i iah8 sit8-chai7 si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7, siang5-pe7 koh-bu2, au7-lai5 choe3 goa2 e5 bou2.  13). Tng Siong7-te3 kah goa2 li7-khui lau7-pe7 e5 ke, si3-koe3 kiaN5 e5 si5, goa2 ka7 i kong2, chiong-lai5 lan2 sou2 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7, chhiaN2 li2 chheng goa2 kong2, I si7 goa2 e5 hiaN; che chiu7-si7 li2 khoan2-thai7 goa2 e5 un.  14). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chiong iuN5, gu5, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2; koh chiong i e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 heng5--i.  15). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 koh kong2, Li2 khoaN3, goa2 e5 toe7 long2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 thang sui5-i3 khia7-khi2.  16). Koh ka7 Sat-lah8 kong2, Goa2 hou7 li2 e5 hiaN chit8 chheng gun5, ka7 li2 tui3 choan5-ke choe3 jia bak8-chiu--e5; taN li2 ti7 it-chhe3 long2 bo5 put-si7.  17). A-pek-lah8-han2 ki5-to2 Siong7-te3; Siong7-te3 chiu7 i-ho2 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kap i e5 bou2 kap lu2-pi7, in chiu7 oe7 siN kiaN2.  18). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 e5 ian5-kou3, i2-keng hou7 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 ke-lai7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 boe7-oe7 siN-kiaN2.

[21]	Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 I cheng5 e5 oe7 koan3-kou3 Sat-lah8; tui3 an2-ni Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 I sou2 kong2--e5 ka7 Sat-lah8 choe3-chiaN5.  2). A-pek-lah8-han2 ni5-lau7 e5 si5, Sat-lah8 hoai5-in7; kau3 Siong7-te3 tui3 i kong2 e5 jit8-ki5, chiu7 ka7 i siN chit8 e5 kiaN2.  3). A-pek-lah8-han2 ka7 Sat-lah8 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2, ho7 mia5 kio3 I2-sat.  4). I2-sat chhut-si3 poeh-jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 chiau3 Siong7-te3 sou2 hoan-hu3-e5, ka7 i e5 kiaN2 kiaN5 kat-le2.  5). I e5 kiaN2 I2-sat chhut-si3 e5 si5, A-pek-lah8-han2 chit8-pah he3.  6). Sat-lah8 kong2, Siong7-te3 hou7 goa2 hoaN-hi2 chhio3; kiN3-na7 thiaN-kiN3--e5, beh kap goa2 tang5 hoaN-hi2 chhio3.  7). Koh kong2, Chi7-chui7 oe7 tai7-seng ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Sat-lah8 beh hou7 eN-a2 suh-leng? in-ui7 ti7 i ni5-lau7 e5 si5, goa2 ka7 i siN chit8 e5 kiaN2.
	8). Gin2-a2 chiam7-chiam7 toa7, chiu7 tng7-leng; I2-sat tng7-leng e5 jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 pai5-siat toa7 ian5-siah8.  9). Tng-si5 Ai-kip8 lang5 Ha7-kah ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2 teh leng2-chhio3, hou7 Sat-lah8 khoaN3-kiN3;  10). chiu7 tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Tioh8 koaN2-chhut chit e5 lu2-pi7 kap i e5 kiaN2; in-ui7 lu2-pi7 e5 kiaN2 boe7-thang kap goa2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sat tang5 choe3 hou7-su5.  11). A-pek-lah8-han2 in-ui7 i e5 kiaN2 e5 ian5-kou3 put-chi2 iu-bun7.  12). Siong7-te3 ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang ui7-tioh8 chit e5 gin2-a2 i2-kip8 li2 e5 lu2-pi7 iu-bun7; kiN3-na7 Sat-lah8 tui3 li2 kong2 e5, li2 long2 tioh8 thiaN; in-ui7 tui3 I2-sat siN--e5, chiah beh chheng-choe3 li2 e5 hou7-e3.  13). Lun7-kau3 lu2-pi7 e5 kiaN2, Goa2 iah8 beh hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 chit8-kok, in-ui7 i iah8 si7 li2 siN--e5.  14). A-pek-lah8-han2 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5, theh8 piaN2 kap chit8 phe5-te7 e5 chui2 hou7 Ha7-kah; he7 ti7 i e5 keng-thau5-teng2; lian5 gin2-a2 soa3 kah i khi3; i chiu7 khi3, kau3 Piat8-si7-pa e5 khong3-ia2 chiu7 kiaN5 bo5 lou7.  15). Phe5-te7 lai7 e5 chui2 eng7-liau2, Ha7-kah chiu7 chiong gin2-a2 pang3 ti7 soe3 chang5 chhiu7 kha.  16). Pun2-sin kiaN5-khui, iok-liok8 choh8 chit8 ki chiN3 e5 hng7, saN-tui3-bin7 teh che7; kong2, Goa2 put-jim2 khoaN3 gin2-a2 si2; chiu7 saN-tui3-bin7 che7, chhut-siaN toa7 thi5-khau3.  17). Siong7-te3 thiaN-kiN3 gin2-a2 e5 siaN; Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 tui3 thiN--nih kio3 Ha7-kah kong2, Ha7-kah, li2 u7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3? m7-bian2 kiaN; Siong7-te3 i2-keng thiaN-kiN3 gin2-a2 ti7-hia e5 siaN.  18). Khi2-lai5, iah8 hou7 gin2-a2 khi2--lai5, khan ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; Goa2 beh hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 toa7-kok.  19). Siong7-te3 khui i e5 bak8-chiu, i chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 chui2-chiN2; chiu7 chiong phe5-te7 khi3 jip8-chui2 kau3 moa2-moa2, soa3 hou7 gin2-a2 lim.  20). Siong7-te3 kap gin2-a2 ti7-teh, i chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 toa7; tiam3 ti7 khong3-ia2, chiaN5-choe3 sia7-chiN3 e5 lang5.  21). I khia7-khi2 ti7 Pa-lan5 e5 khong3-ia2; i e5 lau7-bu2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 ka7 i chhoa7 chit8 e5 bou2.
	22). Tng hit-si5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8, kap i e5 kun-tiuN2 Hui-kok, tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, KiN3-na7 li2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7, Siong7-te3 kap li2 ti7-teh.  23). TaN li2 ti7-chia tioh8 ki2 Siong7-te3 kap goa2 chiu3-choa7, m7-thang khi-hu7 goa2, kap goa2 e5 kiaN2, i2-kip8 goa2 e5 sun; goa2 an3-chaiN2-iuN7 ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2, li2 iah8 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goa2, i2-kip8 li2 sou2 kia3-ku e5 toe7-hng.  24). A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Goa2 beh chiu3-choa7.  25). Cheng5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 e5 lou5-pok8 pa3-chiam3 chit8 khau2 chui2-chiN2, A-pek-lah8-han2 ui7 chit e5 su7 hiam5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8.  26). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kong2, Chi7-chui7 choe3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 m7-chai; li2 iah8 be7 u7 ka7 goa2 kong2, kau3 kin-a2-jit8 goa2 chiah thiaN-kiN3.  27). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong iuN5 kap gu5 hou7 A-pi2-bi2-lek8; nng7-lang5 chiu7 saN-kap lip8-iok.  28). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong chhit chiah bu2 e5 iuN5-ko leng7-goa7 pang3 ti7 chit8 sou2-chai7.  29). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 mng7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 chiong chhit chiah bu2 e5 iuN5-ko leng7-goa7 pang3 ti7 chit8 sou2-chai7, si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3?  30). In3 kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 goa2 e5 chhiu2 siu chi2 chhit chiah bu2 e5 iuN5-ko, choe3 goa2 khui chit khau2 chiN2 e5 cheng3-ku3.  31). Sou2-i2 mia5 hit sou2-chai7 kio3 Piat8-si7-pa, in-ui7 in nng7-lang5 ti7-hia u7 chiu3-choa7.
	32). In ti7 Piat8-si7-pa lip8-iok; A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chiu7 kap i e5 kun-tiuN2 Hui-kok khi2-sin to3--khi3 Hui-li7-su7 toe7.  33). A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7 Piat8-si7-pa chai chit8 chang5 sui5-si-liu2 chhiu7; koh ti7-hia kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng2-eng2 ti7-teh Siong7-te3 e5 mia5.  34). A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 e5 toe7 kia3-ku choe7-choe7 jit8.

[22]	Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7, Siong7-te3 chhi3 A-pek-lah8-han2, kio3 i kong2, A-pek-lah8-han2; i in3 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia.  2). Siong7-te3 kong2, Li2 toa3 li2 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 tok8-siN e5 kiaN2, li2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 I2-sat, khi3 Mou5-li7-a e5 toe7, Goa2 sou2 beh chi2-si7 li2 e5 soaN; ti7-hia chiong i hian3-choe3 sio-che3.  3). A-pek-lah8-han2 thau3-cha2 khi2--lai5, pi7-pan7 lu5, toa3 i e5 nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, kap i e5 kiaN2 I2-sat; iah8 phoa3 sio-che3 e5 chha5; chiu7 khi2-sin khi3 Siong7-te3 sou2 chi2-si7 i e5 toe7.  4). Kau3 te7-saN jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 kiah8-bak8 hng7-hng7 khoaN3 hit e5 sou2-chai7.  5). A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 kap lu5 tiam3 chia theng3-hau7, goa2 kap gin2-a2 khi3 hia keng3-pai3, chiu7 to3--lai5 lin2 chia.  6). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong sio-che3 e5 chha5 he7 ti7 i e5 kiaN2 I2-sat e5 sin-chiuN7, ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 kiah8 he2 kap to; tui3 hit-tiap8 nng7-lang5 saN-kap kiaN5.  7). I2-sat ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Pe7 ah; i kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2, goa2 ti7-chia.  I kong2, Li2 khoaN3, he2 kap chha5 long2 u7; chong2-si7 sio-che3 e5 iuN5-a2 ti7 tah-loh8?  8). A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2, Siong7-te3 beh ka-ki7 pi7-pan7 sio-che3 e5 iuN5-a2; tui3 hit-tiap8 nng7-lang5 saN-kap kiaN5.
	9). In kau3 Siong7-te3 chi2-si7 i e5 sou2-chai7; A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7-hia khi2 toaN5, chiong chha5 pai5-ho2, pak8 i e5 kiaN2 I2-sat, he7 ti7 toaN5--nih e5 chha5-teng2.  10). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 kiah8-to, beh thai5 i e5 kiaN2.  11). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tui3 thiN kio3 i kong2, A-pek-lah8-han2, A-pek-lah8-han2; i in3 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia.  12). Su3-chia2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang ti7 chit e5 gin2-a2 e5 sin-chiuN7 he7-chhiu2, iah8 m7-thang tui3 i chaiN2-iuN7 choe3; in-ui7 goa2 taN chai li2 si7 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3, iah8 bo5 chiong li2 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 tok8-siN--e5, lau5--teh, m7-hou7 goa2.  13). A-pek-lah8-han2 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 au7-bin7 u7 chit8 chiah iuN5-kang2, kak tiN5 ti7 kui-pho7 e5 chhiu7-a2; A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 khi3 liah8 hit chiah iuN5-kang2 lai5, hian3 choe3 sio-che3, lai5 thoe3 i e5 kiaN2.  14). A-pek-lah8-han2 mia5 hit e5 sou2-chai7 kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa-i2-lek8; kau3 kin-a2-jit8 lang5 iau2 teh kong2, Ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 soaN beh pi7-pan7.  15). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 te7-ji7 pai2 tui3 thiN kio3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2,  16). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2 i2-keng kiaN5 chit e5 su7, bo5 lau5 li2 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 tok8-siN e5 kiaN2, Goa2 chiu7 ki2 ka-ki7 chiu3-choa7 kong2,  17). Goa2 su3-hok beh su3-hok li2, ke-thiN beh ke-thiN li2 e5 hou7-e3, chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN, hai2-piN e5 soa; li2 e5 hou7-e3 beh tit-tioh8 chiah e5 tui3-tek8 e5 koan-ai3.  18). Koh toe7-chiuN7 ban7-pang beh in-ui7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; in-ui7 li2 thiaN-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7.  19). Tui3 hit-tiap8 A-pek-lah8-han2 to3--lai5 i hiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 hia; in chiu7 saN-kap khi2-sin khi3 Piat8-si7-pa.  A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 tiam3 ti7 Piat8-si7-pa.
	20). Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, u7 lang5 ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Bit8-ka ka7 li2 e5 sio2-ti7 Na2-hok8 siN-kiaN2;  21). toa7-e5 OU-su, sio2-ti7 Pou3-su, kap A-lan5 e5 lau7-pe7, Ki-bou2-li7;  22). kap Ki-siat, Hap-so2, Pit-tat8, Ek-lah8, Pi2-thou2-li7, (Pi2-thou2-li7 siN Li7-pek-ka).  23). Chi2 poeh-lang5 long2 si7 Bit8-ka ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 sio2-ti7 Na2-hok8 siN--e5.  24). Na2-hok8 e5 soe3-i5, mia5 Liu5-ma2, siN The5-pat, Ka-ham5, Tha-hat, kap Ma2-ka.

[23]	Sat-lah8 hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah ji7-chap8-chhit he3; che si7 Sat-lah8 it-seng e5 ni5-he3.  2). Sat-lah8 si2 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Ki-liat8-a-pa, chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lun5; A-pek-lah8-han2 lai5, ui7-tioh8 Sat-lah8 ai-siong thi5-khau3.  3). Au7-lai5 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 si2-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 khi2--lai5, ka7 Hek-lang5 kong2,  4). Goa2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan si7 kia3-ku e5 chhut-goa7 lang5; kiu5 lin2 ti7-chia hou7 goa2 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7 choe3 thiong2-toe7, thang bai5-chong3 goa2 e5 si2-lang5, hou7 goa2 bo5 koh khoaN3-kiN3 i.  5). Hek-lang5 in3 A-pek-lah8-han2, ka7 i kong2,  6). Goa2 e5 chu2, chhiaN2 thiaN; li2 ti7 goan2 tiong-kan choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 bok8-pek; chhut-chai7 li2 ti7 goan2 e5 thiong2-toe7-lai7 keng2 te7-it-ho2--e5, lai5 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5; goan2 bo5 chit8-lang5 m7 iong5-un2 li2 ti7 i e5 thiong2-toe7-lai7 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5.  7). A-pek-lah8-han2 khi2--lai5, tui3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 Hek-chok8, aN3-io.  8). Tui3 in kong2, Lin2 na7 u7 i3-su3 beh hou7 goa2 bai5-chong3 goa2 e5 si2-lang5, hou7 goa2 bo5 koh khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 chhiaN2 thiaN goa2, thoe3 goa2 kiu5 So2-hat e5 kiaN2 I2-hut-lun5,  9). chiong i e5 chhan5-thau5 Bek8-pi2-lah8 e5 hiat8 hou7 goa2; i thang chiau3 chiok-giah8 e5 ke3-sou3 boe7 hou7 goa2; hou7 goa2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 giap8 thang choe3 bong7-toe7.  10). Tng-si5 I2-hut-lun5 che7 ti7 Hek-lang5 e5 tiong-kan; tui3 hit-tiap8 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 ti7 it-chhe3 jip8 i e5 siaN5-mng5 e5 Hek-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, in3 A-pek-lah8-han2, kong2,  11). M7-bian2, goa2 e5 chu2 thiaN goa2; goa2 beh sang3 li2 hit khu chhan5, lian5 hit lai7-bin7 e5 hiat8 iah8 hou7 li2; ti7 goa2 tang5-chok8 e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, goa2 hou7 li2, thang bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5.  12). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 ti7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5 aN3-io;  13). ti7 hit sou2-chai7 peh-siN3 e5 bin7-cheng5, tui3 I2-hut-lun5 kong2, Li2 na7 kheng2, chhiaN2 thiaN goa2; goa2 beh chiong chhan5 e5 ke3-chiN5 hou7 li2, li2 tioh8 siu; hou7 goa2 thang ti7-hia bai5-chong3 goa2 e5 si2-lang5.  14). I2-hut-lun5 in3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2,  15). Goa2 e5 chu2, chhiaN2 thiaN goa2; chhan5 tat8-tit gun5 si3-pah sia3-khek-lek8, ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan, beh sng3 sim2-mih8? choe3 li2 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5.  16). A-pek-lah8-han2 thiaN I2-hut-lun5 e5 oe7, chiau3 i ti7 Hek-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 sou2 kong2--e5, chiong boe2-boe7 thong-eng7 e5 gun5, pheng5 si3-pah sia3-khek-lek8 hou7 I2-hut-lun5.
	17). Tui3 hit-tiap8 I2-hut-lun5 e5 chhan5, ti7 Bek8-pi2-lah8, Ban7-li7 e5 thau5-cheng5; hit khu chhan5 kap hi2 lai7-bin7 e5 hiat8, kap chhan5-lai7 i2-kip8 si3-ui5 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7-bak8,  18). ti7 Hek-chok8 lang5 kap it-chhe3 jip8 i e5 siaN5-mng5 e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, long2 tiaN7-tioh8 kui hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2 choe3 giap8.  19).  Au7-lai7 A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong i e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 bai5-chong3 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 Ban7-li7 thau5-cheng5 e5 Bek8-pi2-lah8 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8; Ban7-li7 chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lun5.  20). Tui3 an2-ni hit khu chhan5 kap chhan5--nih e5 hiat8, tui3 Hek-lang5 tiaN7-tioh8 kui hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2 choe3 giap8, lai5 choe3 bong7-toe7.

[24]	A-pek-lah8-han2 he3-siu7 tng5, ni5-lau7; Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 it-chhe3 e5 su7 long2 su3-hok hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2.  2). A-peh-lah8-han2 tui3 i ke-lai7 koan2-li2 choan5-giap8 e5 lau7 lou5-pok8 kong2, ChhiaN2 chiong li2 e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 toa7-thui2-e7,  3). goa2 beh kah li2 ki2 Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 thiN e5 Siong7-te3, toe7 e5 Siong7-te3, lai5 chiu3-choa7, goa2 khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, li2 m7-thang ka7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 in e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 bou2.  4). Li2 tioh8 khi3 goa2 e5 pun2-toe7 pun2-chok8, ka7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sat chhoa7 chit8 e5 bou2.  5). Lou5-pok8 in3 i kong2, Siat-su2 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 m7-kheng2 te3 goa2 lai5 chit sou2-chai7, goa2 chiu7 tioh8 chiong li2 e5 kiaN2 toa3 to3--khi3 li2 sou2 tui3 hia chhut-lai5 e5 toe7 mah?  6).
