A-pek-lah8-han2 ka7 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, m7-thang chhoa7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 to3--khi3 hia;  7). thiN e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa, bat chhoa7 goa2 li7-khui lau7-pe7 e5 ke, kap pun2-chok8 e5 toe7, tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7, iah8 tui3 goa2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hou7-e3; I beh chhe I e5 su3-chia2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; li2 chiu7 thang tui3 hia ka7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 chit8 e5 bou2.  8). Siat-su2 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 m7-kheng2 te3 li2 lai5, goa2 kah li2 chiu3 e5 choa7 chiu7 kap li2 bo5 kan-siap8; tok8-tok8 m7-thang toa3 goa2 e5 kiaN2 to3--khi3 hia.  9). Lou5-pok8 chiu7 chiong i e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 chu2-lang5 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 toa7-thui2-e7; ui7-tioh8 chit e5 su7 tui3 i chiu3-choa7.
	10). Hit e5 lou5-pok8 tui3 i chu2-lang5 e5 lok8-to5-tiong, chhu2 chap8-chiah lok8-to5, soa3 toa3 i chu2-lang5 tak8-iuN7 e5 chai5-po2; khi2-sin khi3 Bi2-sou2-pho-tai7-bi2, kau3 Na2-hok8 e5 siaN5.  11). Jit8 beh am3, cheng3 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 chhut-lai5 chhiuN7 chui2; i chiu7 hou7 lok8-to5 kui7 ti7 siaN5-goa7 e5 chiN2-piN.  12). I kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 si-un hou7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 A-pek-lah8-han2, hou7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 ho2 cho-gu7.  13). Goa2 taN khia7 ti7 chiN2-piN, siaN5-lai7 lang5 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 teh chhut-lai5 chhiuN7 chui2;  14). goa2 beh tui3 chit8 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 kong2, ChhiaN2 pang3-loh8 li2 e5 chui2-pan5, hou7 goa2 lim chui2; i na7 kong2, ChhiaN2 lim, goa2 iah8 beh hou7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 lim; goan7 hit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 si7 Li2 sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 hou7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 I2-sat choe3-bou2; an2-ni, goa2 chiu7 chai Li2 si-un hou7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5.  15). Oe7 iau2 kong2 be7 soah, Li7-pek-ka keng-thau5 pe7 chui2-pan5 chhut-lai5, i si7 Pi2-thou2-li7 siN--e5; Pi2-thou2-li7 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 sio2-ti7 Na2-hok8 e5 bou2 Bit8-ka e5 kiaN2.  16). Hit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 bin7-mau7 kek8-ki5 sui2, iau2 si7 chai7-sek-lu2, iah8 be7-bat u7 lang5 chhin-kun7 i; i loh8-khi3 chiN2-piN, chhiuN7-moa2 i e5 pan5 chiu7 khi2-lai5.  17). Lou5-pok8 chau2 chin3-cheng5 ngia5-chih i kong2, Kiu5 li2 chiong pan5-lai7 e5 chui2 tam7-poh8-a2 goa2 lim.  18). Cha-bou2-gin2-a2 kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2, chhiaN2 lim; chiu7 koaN2-kin2 pang3 chui2-pan5 loh8-lai5, khoa3 ti7 chhiu2--nih, hou7 i lim.  19). Hou7 i lim beng5-pek8, koh kong2, Goa2 iah8 beh ka7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 chhiuN7 chui2, hou7 in lim kau3-giah8.  20). I chiu7 koaN2-kin2 chiong pan5-lai7 e5 chui2 piaN3 ti7 cho5--nih; koh chau2 kau3 chiN2--nih chhiuN7 chui2 chiu7 ka7 i sou2 u7 e5 lok8-to5 chhiuN7.  21). Hit e5 lang5 chu3-bak8 khoaN3--i, tiam7-tiam7 bo5 kong2-oe7, ai3 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa siuN2-su3 i sun7-su7 e5 lou7 a2-bo5.  22). Lok8-to5 lim beng5-pek8, hit-lang5 chiu7 theh8 chit8 e5 kim-khoan5, tang7 poaN3 sia3-khek-lek8, nng7 e5 kim chhiu2-khoan5, tang7 chap8 sia3-khek-lek8 hou7 hit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2;  23). kong2, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2? chhiaN2 ka7 goa2 kong2; lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, u7 sou2-chai7 thang hou7 goan2 hioh a2-bo5?  24). I chiu7 ka7 i kong2, Goa2 si7 Bit8-ka tui3 Na2-hok8 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2, Pi2-thou2-li7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  25). I koh tui3 i kong2, Goan2 u7 chhau2-liau7 bi2-niu5 chhiong-chiok; iah8 u7 sou2-chai7 thang hioh.  26). Hit-lang5 chiu7 aN3-thau5 keng3-pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2,  27). Tioh8 o-lo2 goa2 e5 chu2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; I eng7 chu5-ai3 seng5-sit8 khoan2-thai7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5, long2 bo5 theng5-chi2; lun7-kau3 goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 lou7-chiuN7 in2-chhoa7 goa2 kau3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 hiaN-ti7 e5 ke.  28). Cha-bou2-gin2-a2 chau2 to3--khi3, chiau3 chiah e5 oe7 ka7 in lau7-bu2 thong-ke e5 lang5 kong2.  29). Li7-pek-ka u7 chit8 e5 hiaN, mia5 kio3 Lah8-pan, i chhut-khi3 khi3 chiN2-piN, chiu7-kun7 hit-lang5.  30). I khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 khoan5, koh khoaN3-kiN3 chhiu2-khoan5 ti7 in sio2-be7 e5 chhiu2; iah8 thiaN-kiN3 in sio2-be7 Li7-pek-ka e5 oe7, kong2, Hit-lang5 tui3 goa2 kong2 an2-ni, an2-ni; i chiu7 khi3 hit-lang5 hia, khoaN3-kiN3 hit-lang5 iau2 khia7 ti7 lok8-to5 piN, oa2-kun7 chui2-chiN2.  31). Chiu7 ka7 i kong2, Li2 chit e5 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok--e5, chhiaN2 jip8--lai5, siaN2-su7 khia7 ti7 goa7-bin7? Goa2 i2-keng pi7-pan7 chhu3, kap lok8-to5 e5 sou2-chai7.  32). Hit-lang5 chiu7 jip8 i e5 chhu3, i chiu7 thau2 lok8-to5 sou2 chai3-e5, koh eng7 chhau2-liau7 bi2-niu5 chhi7 lok8-to5; phang5 chui2 hou7 hit-lang5 i2-kip8 kun-te3 e5 lang5 soe2 kha.  33). Chiong chiah8-mih8 pai5 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, hou7 i chiah8; chong2-si7 i kong2, Goa2 bo5 beh chiah8, theng3-hau7 goa2 kong2-beng5 goa2 e5 su3-beng7.  Lah8-pan kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 kong2.  34). I chiu7 kong2, Goa2 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 lou5-pok8.  35). Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7-toa7 su3-hok ti7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5, hou7 i heng-ong7, koh hou7 i iuN5, gu5, gun5, kim, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7, lok8-to5 kap lu5.  36). Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 bou2 Sat-lah8, ni5-lau7 e5 si5, ka7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 siN chit8 e5 kiaN2; goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 iah8 chiong it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 hou7 chit e5 kiaN2.  37). Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 kah goa2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 toe7, li2 m7-thang ka7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 in e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 bou2.  38). Li2 tioh8 khi3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, goa2 pun2-chok8 hia, ka7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 chit8 e5 bou2.  39). Goa2 tui3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 kong2, KiaN-liau2 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 m7-kheng2 te3 goa2 lai5.  40). I chiu7 ka7 goa2 kong2, Goa2 sou2 hok8-sai7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhe I e5 su3-chia2 kap li2 saN-kap khi3, hou7 li2 sun7-su7 e5 lou7, li2 chiu7 thang tui3 goa2 e5 chong-chok8, goa2 e5 pe7 e5 ke, ka7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 chhoa7 chit8 e5 bou2;  41). tok8-tok8 ai3 li2 kau3 goa2 pun2-chok8 hia, goa2 kah li2 sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7, chiu7 kap li2 bo5 kan-giap8; in na7 m7 hou7 li2, goa2 kah li2 chiu3 e5 choa7, iah8 kap li2 bo5 kan-siap8.  42). Kin-a2-jit8 goa2 kau3 chiN2-piN, kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 na7 hou7 goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7 sun7-su7;  43). goa2 taN khia7 ti7 chui2-chiN2-piN, tui3 chit8 e5 chhut-lai5 chhiuN7 chui2 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 chiong li2 pan5--nih e5 chui2 tam7-poh8 hou7 goa2 lim;  44). i na7 kong2, Choe3 li2 lim, goa2 iah8 beh ka7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 chhiuN7 chui2; goan7 hit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 tiaN7-tioh8 hou7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 kiaN2 choe3 bou2--e5.  45). Goa2 sim-lai7 e5 oe7 iau2 kong2 be7 liau2, Li7-pek-ka chiu7 chhut-lai5, keng-thau5-teng2 pe7 chui2-pan5; loh8-khi3 chiN2-piN chhiuN7 chui2; goa2 chiu7 ka7 i kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 hou7 goa2 lim.  46). I chiu7 koaN2-kin2 tui3 keng-thau5-teng2 pang3-loh8 chui2-pan5, kong2, ChhiaN2 lim, goa2 iah8 hou7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 lim; goa2 chiu7 lim, i iah8 hou7 goa2 e5 lok8-to5 lim.  47). Goa2 koh mng7 i kong2, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2? I in3 kong2, Goa2 si7 Bit8-ka tui3 Na2-hok8 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2, Pi2-thou2-li7, e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; goa2 chiu7 chiong khoan5 koa3 ti7 i e5 phiN7, chhiu2-khoan5 koa3 ti7 i e5 chhiu2.  48). Goa2 chiu7 aN3-thau5 pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, o-lo2 goa2 e5 chu2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 I chhoa7 goa2 kiaN5 tu2-ho2 e5 lou7, hou7 goa2 tit-tioh8 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 sio2-ti7 e5 cha-bou2-sun lai5 hou7 i e5 kiaN2.  49). TaN lin2 na7 beh eng7 chu5-ai3 seng5-sit8 khoan2-thai7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5, chiu7 ka7 goa2 kong2; na7 m7, iah8 ka7 goa2 kong2; hou7 goa2 ho2 thang ng3-cho2 a2-si7 ng3-iu7.  50). Lah8-pan kap Pi2-thou2-li7 in3 kong2, Tai7-chi3 chhut ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, goan2 boe7-oe7 tui3 li2 kong2 ho2 a2 phaiN2.  51). Li2 khoaN3, Li7-pek-ka ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, thang chiong i chhoa7--khi3, hou7 li2 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 kiaN2 choe3 bou2, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa sou2 kong2.  52). A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 lou5-pok8 thiaN-kiN3 in chiah e5 oe7, chiu7 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa phak ti7 toe7--nih.  53). Hit-tiap8 lou5-pok8 theh8-chhut gun5-khi3 kim-khi3 kap i-hok8 sang3 Li7-pek-ka; koh chiong po2-mih8 sang3 i e5 hiaN kap i e5 lau7-bu2.  54). Lou5-pok8 kap te3 i e5 lang5 lim-chiah8 hioh-mi5; thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, chiu7 kong2, ChhiaN2 chhe goa2 to3-khi3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 hia.  55). Li7-pek-ka e5 hiaN kap i e5 lau7-bu2 kong2, Iong5-un2 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 kap goan2 tiam3 kui2-jit8, siang7-chio2 chap8-jit8, jian5-au7 i thang khi3.  56). I tui3 in kong2, M7-thang chou2-tong3 goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng hou7 goa2 sun7-su7 e5 lou7; chhiaN2 chhe goa2 khi3, hou7 goa2 to3-khi3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 hia.  57). In kong2, Goan2 kio3 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 lai5, tham3 i e5 oe7-i3.  58). Chiu7 kio3 Li7-pek-ka lai5, mng7 i kong2, Li2 beh kap chit-lang5 khi3 mah? i kong2, Goa2 beh khi3.  59). In chiu7 chhe sio2-be7 Li7-pek-ka, kap i e5 leng-bu2, kap A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 lou5-pok8, i2-kip8 te3 i e5 lang5 khi3.  60). In chiu7 ka7 Li7-pek-ka chiok-hok, tui3 i kong2, Goan2 sio2-be7 ah, goan7 li2 choe3 chheng-ban7 lang5 e5 lau7-bu2, goan7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 tit-tioh8 tui3-tek8 e5 koan-ai3.  61). Li7-pek-ka kap i e5 lu2-pi7 khi2-lai5 khia5 lok8-to5, te3 hit e5 lang5; lou5-pok8 chiu7 chhoa7 Li7-pek-ka khi3.
	62). I2-sat khia7-khi2 ti7 Lam5-toe7, hit-si5 tui3 Pi2-jiN2-lah8-hai2-lai5 e5 lou7 lai5.  63). Jit8 beh am3, I2-sat chhut-lai5 ti7 chhan5--nih, cheng7-cheng7 teh siuN7, kiah8-bak8 chit8-e7 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 lok8-to5 lai5.  64). Li7-pek-ka khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sat, chiu7 tui3 lok8-to5 loh8-lai5.  65). Mng7 hit e5 lou5-pok8 kong2, Ti7 chhan5--nih kiaN5-lai5 ngia5-chih lan2--e5 si7 chi7-chui7? Lou5-pok8 kong2, Si7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5.  Li7-pek-ka chiu7 theh8 phe3 ka-ki7 ta3.  66). Lou5-pok8 chiong sou2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, ka7 I2-sat kong2.  67). I2-sat chiu7 khan Li7-pek-ka jip8 i e5 lau7-bu2 Sat-lah8 e5 pou3-piN5, chhoa7 i choe3 bou2; koh chin thiaN3 i.  I2-sat tui3 lau7-bu2 si2-au7, kau3 chit-tiap8 chiah tit-tioh8 an-ui3.

[25]	A-pek-lah8-han2 koh chhoa7 chit8 e5 bou2, mia5 kio3 Ki-thou2-lah8.  2). Ki-thou2-lah8 ka7 i siN Sim-lan5, Iok-san, Bi2-tan3, Bi2-tian5, I-si-pa, Su-a.  3). Iok-san siN Si7-pa kap Ti2-tan3.  Ti2-tan3 e5 kiaN2-sun si7 A-su-li7 chok8, Li7-tou-si7 chok8, kap Li7-ou-bi2 chok8.  4). Bi2-tian5 e5 kiaN2 si7 I2-hoat, I2-hut, Hap-lok8, A-pi2-tai7, I2-lek8-tai7; chiah-e5 long2 si7 Ki-thou2-lah8 e5 kiaN2.  5). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 hou7 I2-sat.  6). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong chai5-but2 pun hou7 i chiah e5 soe3-i5 e5 kiaN2; than3 i pun2-sin iau2 oah8 e5 si5, chhe in li7-khui i e5 kiaN2 I2-sat khi3 tang--si3, kau3 tang-peng5 e5 toe7.  7). A-pek-lah8-han2 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 si7 chit8-pah chhit-chap8 gou7 he3.  8). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiah8 tng5 he3-siu7, chiaN5-choe3 lau7-lang5, ni5-he3 moa2-chiok, tng7-khui3 si2, to3-chou2.  9). I e5 kiaN2 I2-sat, I2-sit8-ma2-li7, chiong i bai5-chong3 ti7 Bek8-pi2-lah8 e5 hiat8; chit e5 hiat8 ti7 Ban7-li7 e5 thau5-cheng5, Hek-lang5 So2-hat e5 kiaN2 I2-hut-lun5 e5 chhan5-tiong,  10). chiu7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Hek-lang5 sou2 boe2 hit khu chhan5.  A-pek-lah8-han2 kap i e5 bou2 Sat-lah8 long2 bai5-chong3 ti7-hia.  11). A-pek-lah8-han2 si2 liau2-au7, Siong7-te3 su3-hok hou7 i e5 kiaN2 I2-sat; I2-sat oa2-kun7 Pi2-jiN2-lah8-hai2-lai5 khia7-khi2.
	12). A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 se3-he7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2:  I2-sit8-ma2-li7 chiu7-si7 Sat-lah8 e5 lu2-pi7 Ai-kip8 lang5 Ha7-kah tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 siN--e5.  13). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5, chiau3 i e5 mia5-ji7 se3-he7, chhin-chhiuN7 e7-toe2:  I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 toa7-kiaN2 Ni5-pai5-iok; koh u7 Ki-tat8, A-tek-piat8, Bi2-pi2-sam;  14). Bi2-si-ma2, Tou7-ma2, Ma2-sat;  15). Hap-tai7, The5-ma2, I-tut8, Na2-hui-si, Ki-ti2-ma2;  16). chiah-e5 chiu7-si7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5; chiau3 in e5 hiuN-chhng iaN5-che7, choe3 chap8-ji7 chok8 e5 chok8-tiuN2.  17). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 it-seng e5 he3-siu7, chit8-pah saN-chap8 chhit; khui3-tng7 si2 chiu7 to3-chou2.  18). I e5 kiaN2-sun toa3 ti7 Hap-hui-lah8 kau3 Ai-kip8 thau5-cheng5 e5 Su-jiN2, beh khi3 A-sut8 e5 lou7; khia7-khi2 ti7 i cheng3 hiaN-ti7 e5 thau5-cheng5.
	19). A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sat e5 se3-he7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2:  A-pek-lah8-han2 siN I2-sat;  20). I2-sat chhoa7 Li7-pek-ka choe3 bou2 e5 si5, tu2-a2 si3-chap8 he3.  I si7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 toe7 e5 A-lan5 lang5 Pi2-thou2-li7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, A-lan5 lang5 Lah8-pan e5 sio2-be7.  21). I2-sat in-ui7 i e5 bou2 bo5 siN-kiaN2, thoe3 i ki5-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa; Ia5-ho5-hoa un2-chun2 i sou2 kiu5; i e5 bou2 Li7-pek-ka chiu7 hoai5-in7.  22). Gin2-a2 ti7 i e5 pak-lai7 saN-khoeh; i chiu7 kong2, Na7 si7 chit-khoan2, goa2 mih8-sai2 an2-ni? Chiu7 khi3 mng7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.  23). Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 i kong2, Nng7-kok ti7 li2 pak-lai7, nng7-chok8 beh tui3 li2 e5 sin-khu chhut; chit-chok8 beh khah-kiong5 hit-chok8; si7-toa7-e5 beh hok8-sai7 si7-soe3-e5.  24). Seng-san2 e5 jit8-ki5 kau3, ko2-jian5 pak-lai7 si7 siang-siN--e5.  25). Thau5-chit8-e5 chhut-lai5--e5, sin-the2 ang5-ang5, thong sin-khu chhin-chhiuN7 phe5-a2-saN; chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 choe3 I2-so3.  26). Te3-au7 i e5 sio2-ti7 koh chhut-lai5, i e5 chhiu2 khiN5 I2-so3 e5 kha-au7-tiN; chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 Nga2-kok.  Nng7 e5 kiaN2 chhut-si3 e5 si5, I2-sat tu2-a2 lak8-chap8 he3.
	27). Nng7 e5 gin2-a2 chiam7-chiam7 toa7; I2-so3 gau5 phah-lah8, siong5-siong5 ti7 soaN-ia2; Nga2-kok choe3-lang5 thiam5-cheng7, siong5-siong5 toa3 pou3-piN5-lai7.  28). I2-sat thiaN3 I2-so3, in-ui7 siong5-siong5 chiah8 i e5 ia2-bi7. Li7-pek-ka thiaN3 Nga2-kok.  29). U7 chit8 jit8 Nga2-kok chu2-thng, I2-so3 tui3 soaN-ia2 to3-lai5, ia3-sian7 kau3-kek8.  30). I2-so3 tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Goa2 chin ia3-sian7, kiu5 li2 eng7 chit e5 ang5 e5 thng hou7 goa2 chiah8; in-ui7 an2-ni I2-so3 iah8 mia5 kio3 I2-tong.  31). Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 kin-a2-jit8 eng7 toa7-kiaN2 e5 beng5-hun7 boe7 hou7 goa2.  32). I2-so3 kong2, Goa2 to beh si2 lah; chit e5 toa7-kiaN2 e5 beng5-hun7, tui3 ti7 goa2 u7 siaN2 li7-ek?  33). Nga2-kok kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 li2 tioh8 tui3 goa2 chiu3-choa7.  I chiu7 tui3 i chiu3-choa7, chiong toa7-kiaN2 e5 beng5-hun7 boe7 hou7 Nga2-kok.  34). Nga2-kok chiu7 chiong piaN2 kap ang5-tau7-thng hou7 I2-so3; i chiu7 lim-chiah8, khi2-lai5 choe3 i khi3; che chiu7-si7 I2-so3 khoaN3-khin toa7-kiaN2 e5 beng5-hun7.

[26]	A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 si5, thau5-chit8-pai2 ki-hng i2-au7, hit sou2-chai7 koh u7 ki-hng.  I2-sat chiu7 khi3 Ki-lah8-jiN2, kau3 Hui-li7-su7 e5 ong5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 hia.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i chhut-hian7 kong2, Li2 m7-thang loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8, tioh8 toa3 ti7 Goa2 sou2 chi2-si7 li2 e5 toe7.  3). Li2 kia3-ku ti7 chit e5 toe7, Goa2 beh kap li2 ti7-teh, su3-hok li2; in-ui7 Goa2 beh chiong chiah e5 toe7 long2 hou7 li2, kap li2 e5 hou7-e3; Goa2 beh kian-kou3 Goa2 tui3 li2 e5 pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7.  4). Goa2 beh ke-thiN li2 e5 hou7-e3, chhin-chhiuN7 thiN--nih e5 chhiN hiah-choe7; koh beh chiong chiah e5 toe7 long2 hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3; koh toe7-chiuN7 ban7-kok beh in-ui7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  5). Si7 in-ui7 A-pek-lah8-han2 thiaN Goa2 e5 oe7, siu2 Goa2 e5 hoan-hu3, Goa2 e5 beng7-leng7, Goa2 e5 lut8-le7, goa2 e5 hoat-tou7.  6). I2-sat khia7-khi2 Ki-lah8-jiN2 .  7). Hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 mng7 kau3 i e5 bou2; i chiu7 kong2, I si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7; m7-kaN2 kong2, Si7 goa2 e5 bou2; sim-lai7 siuN7, KiaN-liau2 hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 ui7-tioh8 Li7-pek-ka e5 ian5-kou3 thai5 goa2; in-ui7 i bin7-mau7 chin sui2.  8). I ti7-hia i2-keng ku2, Hui-li7-su7 ong5, A-pi2-bi2-lek8, tui3 thang-a2 khoaN3; khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sat kap i e5 bou2 Li7-pek-ka teh kun2-chhio3.  9). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kio3 I2-sat lai5, ka7 i kong2, I sit8-chai7 si7 li2 e5 bou2; li2 siaN2-su7 kong2, I si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7? I2-sat kong2, Goa2 sim-lai7 siuN7, kiaN-liau2 goa2 ui7-tioh8 i lai5 si2.  10). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kong2, Li2 tui3 goan2 sou2-choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, hiam2-hiam2 u7 lang5 kap li2 e5 bou2 saN-kap khun3; li2 chiu7 hou7 goan2 ham7-loh8 choe7.  11). Tui3 hit-tiap8 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chiu7 hoan-hu3 cheng3 peh-siN3 kong2, Hoan7-na7 khap8-tioh8 chit-lang5 kap i e5 bou2--e5, tiaN7-tioh8 beh hou7 i si2.
	12). I2-sat ti7 hit sou2-chai7 cheng3-choh, hit-ni5 tit-tioh8 pah-pe7; Ia5-ho5-hoa su3 i hok-khi3.  13). I chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 toa7, na2-ku2 na2-toa7, kau3 chiaN5-choe3 toa7 hu3-hou7.  14). I u7 iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5, iah8 u7 choe7-choe7 lou5-pok8; Hui-li7-su7 lang5 chiu7 oan3-tou3 i.  15). Tng i e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7-teh e5 jit8, i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 lou5-pok8 sou2 khui e5 chiN2, Hui-li7-su7 lang5 long2 ka7 i that--khi3, eng7 thou5 thun7-moa2.  16). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 ka7 I2-sat kong2, Li2 tioh8 li7-khui goan2 khi3, in-ui7 li2 pi2 goan2 cham2-jian5 khah kiong5-seng7.  17). I2-sat chiu7 li7-khui hia, ti7 Ki-lah8-jiN2 e5 soaN-kok tah pou3-piN5, tiam3 hia khia7-khi2.  18). Tng i e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7-teh e5 jit8, sou2 khui hiah e5 chui2-chiN2, kau3 A-pek-lah8-han2 si2-au7, hou7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 thun7--khi3; I2-sat teng5-chai3 ka7 i khui; iu5-goan5 chiau3 in lau7-pe7 sou2 ho7 e5 mia5 lai5 mia5 hiah e5 chiN2.  19). I2-sat e5 lou5-pok8 ti7 soaN-kok teh kut8, tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 oah8-chui2 e5 chiN2.  20). Ki-lah8-jiN2 e5 bok8-chia2 kap I2-sat e5 bok8-chia2 saN-chiN, kong2, Chit e5 chui2 si7 goan2-e5.  I2-sat chiu7 ho7 hit e5 chiN2 e5 mia5 kio3 Ai-sek; in-ui7 in kap i saN-chiN.  21). In koh khui chit8 e5 chiN2, ui7 chit e5 chiN2 koh saN-chiN; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 Se-the5-na2.  22). Li7-khui hia koh khui chit8 e5 chiN2; in bo5 ui7 chit e5 chiN2 koh saN-chiN; chiu7 ka7 i ho7 mia5 Li7-ho5-pek; si7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa taN hou7 goan2 khui-khoah e5 toe7; goan2 beh ti7 chit e5 toe7 heng-ong7.
	23). I2-sat tui3 hia chiuN7-khi3 Piat8-si7-pa.  24). Hit-mi5 Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i chhut-hian7 kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, m7-bian2 kiaN; in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, beh su3-hok li2, hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 heng-ong7, long2 si7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 lou5-pok8 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 ian5-kou3.  25). I chiu7 ti7-hia khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, ti7-hia tah i e5 pou3-piN5.  I2-sat e5 lou5-pok8 chiu7 ti7-hia khui chit8 e5 chiN2.
	26). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kap i e5 peng5-iu2 A-hou7-sat i2-kip8 i e5 kun-tiuN2 Hui-kok, tui3 Ki-lah8-jiN2 lai5 kiN3--i.  27). I2-sat tui3 in kong2, Lin2 ki3-jian5 oan3-hun7 goa2, kah goa2 li7-khui lin2; taN siaN2-su7 lai5 goa2 chia?  28). In kong2, Goan2 beng5-beng5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap li2 ti7-teh, m7-tat8--tioh8 lan2 tiong-kan li2 goan2 chiu3-choa7, hou7 goan2 kap li2 lip8-iok;  29). li2 bo5 hai7 goan2, chhin-chhiuN7 goan2 be7-bat khap8-tioh8 li2, tok8-tok8 ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2, sang3 li2 an-jian5 to3-khi3; taN li2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok--e5.  30). I2-sat chiu7 ui7 in siat ian5-siah8, in chiu7 chiah8 chiu7 lim.  31). Thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, tai7-ke chiu3-choa7; I2-sat sang3 in khi2-sin, in chiu7 an-jian5 li7-khui i khi3.  32). Siang5 hit-jit8, I2-sat e5 lou5-pok8 lai5, chiong in khui-chiN2 e5 su7 thong-ti i; kong2, Goan2 tit-tioh8 chui2 lah.  33). I chiu7 kio3 hit e5 chiN2 e5 mia5 kio3 Si7-pa; sou2-i2 kau3 kin-a2-jit8 hit e5 siaN5 e5 mia5 kio3-choe3 Piat8-si7-pa.
	34). I2-so3 si3-chap8 he3 e5 si5, chhoa7 Hek-lang5 Pi2-li7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Iu5-tek, kap Hek-lang5 I2-lun5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Pa-sit8-boat choe3 bou2.  35). Chi2 nng7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 siong5-siong5 hou7 I2-sat kap Li7-pek-ka sim-lai7 toa7 iu-hun7.

[27]	I2-sat ni5-lau7, bak8-chiu hoe boe7 khoaN3-kiN3, chiu7 kio3 i e5 toa7-kiaN2 I2-so3 lai5, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2 ah; i in3 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia.  2). Kong2, Goa2 taN lau7 lah, m7-chai tah-loh8 chit8-jit8 beh si2.  3). TaN kiah8 li2 e5 ke-si, chiu7-si7 chiN3-te7 kap keng, khi3 soaN--nih, ka7 goa2 phah-lah8,  4). chiau3 goa2 sou2 kah-i3 e5, chu2 hou7 i ho2 chu-bi7, phang5-lai5 hou7 goa2, goa2 thang chiah8; hou7 goa2 ti7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng ka7 li2 chiok-hok.  5). I2-sat ka7 i e5 kiaN2 I2-so3 kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Li7-pek-ka thiaN-kiN3.  I2-so3 khi3 soaN--nih beh phah-lah8, thang toa3 to3--lai5.  6). Li7-pek-ka chiu7 tui3 i e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 khoaN3, goa2 thiaN-kiN3 lin2 lau7-pe7 ka7 li2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 kong2,  7). Li2 chiong ia2-siu3 ka7 goa2 toa3--lai5, ka7 goa2 chu2 hou7 i ho2 chu-bi7, hou7 goa2 chiah8; goa2 beh ti7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 li2 chiok-hok.  8). TaN goa2 e5 kiaN2, li2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7, chiau3 goa2 sou2 hoan-hu3 li2--e5.  9). Li2 khi3 iuN5-kun5 hia, ka7 goa2 liah8 nng7 chiah pui5 e5 soaN-iuN5-a2 lai5; goa2 beh ka7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 chu2 ho2 e5 bi7-sou3, chiau3 i sou2 kah-i3--e5.  10). Li2 phang5--khi3 lin2 lau7-pe7 hia, hou7 i chiah8; hou7 i ti7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng ka7 li2 chiok-hok.  11). Nga2-kok tui3 i e5 lau7-bu2 Li7-pek-ka kong2, M7-ku2 goa2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 sin-khu u7 mng5, goa2 si7 kng-kut8.  12). Siat-su2 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 bong-tioh8 goa2, beh khoaN3 goa2 choe3 khi-phian3 lang5--e5, goa2 chiu7 chio chiu3-chou2; bo5 tit-tioh8 chiok-hok.  13). I e5 lau7-bu2 kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2 ah, li2 chio e5 chiu3-chou2 kui ti7 goa2; choe3 li2 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7, khi3 liah8 lai5 hou7 goa2.  14). I chiu7 khi3 liah8 lai5 hou7 i e5 lau7-bu2; lau7-bu2 chiu7 chu2 ho2 e5 chu-bi7, chiau3 lau7-pe7 sou2 kah-i3--e5.  15). Li7-pek-ka koh hiahN toa7-kiaN2 I2-so3 siu ti7 i ke-lai7 e5 sui2-saN, ka7 i e5 soe3-kiaN2 Nga2-kok chheng7.  16). Koh eng7 soaN-iuN5-a2 phe5 pau Nga2-kok e5 chhiu2, kap i am7-kun2 kng-kut8 e5 ui7.  17). Chiu7 chiong sou2 chu2 e5 ho2 chu-bi7 kap piaN2, he7 ti7 i e5 kiaN2 Nga2-kok e5 chhiu2.  18). Nga2-kok kau3 in lau7-pe7 hia, kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah; i kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia; goa2 e5 kiaN2, li2 si7 chi7-chui7?  19). Nga2-kok tui3 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 toa7-kiaN2 I2-so3; goa2 i2-keng chiau3 li2 sou2 hoan-hu3 goa2--e5 khi3 kiaN5; chhiaN2 li2 khi2-lai5 che7, chiah8 goa2 sou2 phah-tioh8--e5, ho2 thang ka7 goa2 chiok-hok.  20). I2-sat tui3 i e5 kiaN2 kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2, li2 chaiN2-iuN7 chiah khoai3 tit-tioh8? I kong2, In-ui7 li2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 goa2 ho2 cho-gu7 lai5 tit-tioh8.  21). I2-sat ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2 ah, li2 kun7-oa2--lai5, goa2 beh bong li2, khoaN3 li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 I2-so3, a2 m7-si7.  22). Nga2-kok chiu7 oa2-kun7 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat; i chiu7 bong i kong2, SiaN, si7 Nga2-kok e5 siaN; chhiu2, si7 I2-so3 e5 chhiu2.  23). I2-sat hun-piat boe7 beng5, in-ui7 i e5 chhiu2 u7 mng5, chhin-chhiuN7 i e5 hiaN I2-so3 e5 chhiu2; chiu7 ka7 i chiok-hok.  24). Koh kong2, Li2 chin-chiaN3 si7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 I2-so3 mah? I kong2, Goa2 si7.  25). I2-sat kong2, Phang5-lai5 hou7 goa2, goa2 beh chiah8 goa2 e5 kiaN2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 ia2-bi7, ho2 thang ka7 li2 chiok-hok.  Chiu7 phang5 hou7 i, i chiu7 chiah8; iah8 phang5 chiu2 hou7 i, i chiu7 lim.  26). I e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat tui3 i kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2, chin3-cheng5 lai5 chim goa2.  27). I chiu7 chin3-cheng5, chim i e5 lau7-pe7; i e5 lau7-pe7 phiN7-tioh8 i e5 saN e5 phang-bi7, chiu7 ka7 i chiok-hok kong2:
	Goa2 e5 kiaN2 e5 phang-bi7,
	Chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok e5 chhan5 e5 phang-bi7;
28).	Goan7 Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 li2 thiN-teng2 e5 kam-lou7;
	Se3-chiuN7 e5 pui5-toe7,
	Gou7-kak kap sin e5 chiu2 chin-choe7;
29).	Cheng3 peh-siN3 hok8-sai7 li2,
	Liat8-kok kui7-pai3 li2,
	Li2 choe3 li2 hiaN-ti7 e5 chu2,
	Li2 e5 lau7-bu2 e5 kiaN2 kui7-pai3 li2;
	Chiu3-chou2 li2--e5 siu7 chiu3-chou2,
	Chiok-hok li2--e5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.
	30). I2-sat ka7 Nga2-kok chiok-hok beng5-pek8, Nga2-kok tu2-tu2 tui3 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat hia chhut-lai5, i e5 hiaN I2-so3 phah-lah8 to3--lai5.  31). I iah8 chu2 ho2 e5 bi7-sou3, phang5-lai5 hou7 i e5 lau7-pe7, kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, chhiaN2 khi2-lai5 chiah8 kiaN2 sou2 phah--tioh8-e5, ho2 thang ka7 goa2 chiok-hok.  32). I e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat ka7 i kong2, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7? I kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 toa7-kiaN2, I2-so3.  33). I2-sat toa7-kiaN, ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, kong2, He si7 chi7-chui7, li2 be7 lai5 e5 tai7-seng, phang5 i sou2 phah--tioh8-e5 lai5 hou7 goa2; goa2 chiah8 i, ka7 i chiok-hok? i tek-khak beh tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  34). I2-so3 thiaN-kiN3 lau7-pe7 e5 oe7, khui-siaN kio3-khou2 toa7-khau3; tui3 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, goa2, li2 iah8 tioh8 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok.  35). I2-sat kong2, Li2 e5 sio2-ti7 eng7 khui2-ke3 lai5, chhiuN2 li2 e5 hok-hun7.  36). I2-so3 kong2, I mia5-choe3 Nga2-kok, kiam2 bo5 chin hap8 mah? i khi-phian3 goa2 nng7-pai2; cheng5 chhiuN2 goa2 toa7-kiaN2 e5 beng5-hun7; li2 khoaN3, taN i koh chhiuN2 goa2 e5 hok-hun7.  Koh kong2, Kiam2 bo5 lau5 chit8-e5 thang ka7 goa2 chiok-hok mah?  37). I2-sat in3 I2-so3 kong2, Goa2 i2-keng lip8 i choe3 li2 e5 chu2, iah8 chiong i e5 cheng3 hiaN-ti7 hou7 i choe3 lou5-pok8; iah8 eng7 gou7-kak sin-chiu2 iuN2-chhi7 i; goa2 e5 kiaN2 ah, taN goa2 iau2 oe7 ka7 li2 choe3 sim2-mih8?  38). I2-so3 ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Pe7 ah, li2 e5 chiok-hok kiam2 chi2-u7 chit8-pai2 mah? Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, goa2, li2 iah8 tioh8 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok.  39). I2-so3 khui-siaN thi5-khau3.  I e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat in3 i, kong2:
	Li2 sou2 khia7-khi2--e5, beh u7 se3-chiuN7 e5 pui5-toe7,
	Iah8 u7 thiN-teng2 e5 kam-lou7;
40).	Li2 beh oa2-kho3 to-kiam3 tou7-oah8, koh beh hok8-sai7 li2 e5 sio2-ti7;
	Kau3 li2 hun3-heng e5 si5,
	Beh tui3 li2 e5 am7-kun2 kun3-khui i e5 gu5-taN.
41). I2-so3 in-ui7 i e5 lau7-pe7 ka7 Nga2-kok chiok hok-khi3, chiu7 oan3-hun7 Nga2-kok; sim-lai7 kong2, Ui7 lau7-pe7 teng-iu e5 si5 kun7--lah; kau3 hit-si5, goa2 beh thai5-si2 goa2 e5 sio2-ti7 Nga2-kok.  42). U7 lang5 chiong i e5 toa7-kiaN2 I2-so3 e5 oe7 ka7 Li7-pek-ka kong2; i chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 kio3 i e5 soe3-kiaN2 Nga2-kok lai5, ka7 i kong2, Li2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 beh thai5 li2, lai5 siau i e5 hun7-khi3.  43). TaN goa2 e5 kiaN2, li2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7; khi2-lai5, chau2 khi3 Hap-lan5, goa2 e5 hiaN Lah8-pan hia;  44). kap i tiam3 kui2-jit8, theng3-hau7 li2 e5 hiaN siu7-khi3 siau.  45). Kau3 li2 e5 hiaN siu7-khi3 soah, boe7 ki3-tit li2 tui3 i sou2 choe3 e5 su7, hit-si5 goa2 chiu7 chhe lang5 chhoa7 li2 tui3 hia to3--lai5.  Goa2 siaN2-su3 chit8-jit8 sit-loh8 lin2 nng7-lang5?
	46). Li2-pek-ka ka7 I2-sat kong2, Goa2 in-ui7 chiah e5 Hek-lang5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, lian5 siN3-mia7 to m7-ai3.  Siat-su2 Nga2-kok ia7 chhoa7 chit sou2-chai7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3 bou2, chhin-chhiuN7 Hek-lang5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 hit-khoan2, goa2 oah8 u7 siaN2 lou7-eng7?

[28]	I2-sat kio3 Nga2-kok lai5, ka7 i chiok-hok, iah8 hoan-hu3 i kong2, Li2 m7-thang chhoa7 Ka-lam5 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 choe3 bou2.  2). Li2 khi2-lai5, khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5, kau3 li2 e5 goa7-kong Pi2-thou2-li7 e5 ke; ti7 li2 e5 bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan cha-bou2-kiaN2 e5 tiong-kan, chhoa7 chit8-e5 choe3 bou2.  3). Goan7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 su3-hok li2, hou7 li2 siN-thoaN3 chin-choe7, chiaN5-choe3 choe7-choe7 chok8.  4). Koh chiong sou2 eng3-un2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 hok-khi3 hou7 li2, kap li2 e5 hou7-e3; hou7 li2 seng5-chiap li2 sou2-kia3-ku e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 sou2 hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2--e5.  5). I2-sat chhe Nga2-kok khi3; i chiu7 khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5; kau3 A-lan5 lang5 Pi2-thou2-li7 e5 kiaN2 Lah8-pan hia; i si7 Nga2-kok I2-so3 e5 bu2-ku7.  6). I2-so3 khoaN3-kiN3 I2-sat ka7 Nga2-kok chiok-hok, koh chhe i khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5, beh tui3 hia chhoa7-bou2; iah8 khoaN3-kiN3 chiok-hok i e5 si5, hoan-hu3 i kong2, M7-thang chhoa7 Ka-lam5 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 choe3 bou2;  7). koh khoaN3-kiN3 Nga2-kok thiaN pe7-bu2 e5 oe7, khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5;  8). I2-so3 chiu7 chai Ka-lam5 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2, i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat m7-teng3-i3;  9). I2-so3 chiu7 khi3 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 hia, ti7 i hiah e5 bou2 i2-goa7, koh chhoa7 Ma2-hap-lah8 choe3-bou2; i si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kiaN2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Ni5-pai5-iok e5 sio2-be7.
	10). Nga2-kok li7-khui Piat8-si7-pa, ng3 Hap-lan5 khi3.  11). Kau3 chit8 sou2-chai7, in-ui7 jit8 loh8, chiu7 ti7-hia hioh-mi5; tui3 hiah e5 chioh8-thau5 e5 tiong-kan, theh8 chit8-te3 choe3 chim2-thau5, ti7-hia khun3.  12). Bang7-kiN3 u7 thui khia7 ti7 toe7--nih, thui-teng2 tu2-thiN; u7 Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 ti7 thui--nih teh chiuN7-loh8.  13). Ia5-ho5-hoa khia7 ti7 thui-teng2, kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5 chou2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, iah8 si7 I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3.  Goa2 beh chiong li2 hian7-chai7 sou2 khun3 e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2, kap li2 e5 hou7-e3.  14). Li2 e5 hou7-e3 beh chhin-chhiuN7 toe7-chiuN7 e5 thou5-soa; li2 beh tui3 tang, sai, lam5, pak lai5 hoat-tian2; toe7-chiuN7 ban7-chok8 beh in-ui7 li2 kap li2 e5 hou7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.  15). Goa2 iah8 kap li2 ti7-teh, li2 bo5-lun7 khi3 tah-loh8, Goa2 beh po2-hou7 li2; iah8 beh chhoa7 li2 to3-lai5 chit sou2-chai7, long2 bo5 pang3-sak li2, kau3 Goa2 chiaN5 tui3 li2 sou2 kong2--e5.  16). Nga2-kok khun3-chhiN2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chin-chiaN3 ti7-chia, goa2 keng2-jian5 m7-chai.  17). Chiu7 kiaN kong2, Chit sou2-chai7 kau3 chiah thang kiaN!  m7-si7 pat8-hang7, che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3, che si7 thiN e5 mng5.  18). Nga2-kok cha2-cha2 khi2--lai5, chiong i choe3 chim2-thau5 e5 chioh8 khia7 choe3 thiau7; to3 iu5 ti7 teng2-bin7.  19). Chiu7 mia5 hit sou2-chai7 kio3 Pek-tek8-li7, chit e5 siaN5 pun2 mia5 Lou7-su.  20). Nga2-kok he7-goan7 kong2, Siong7-te3 na7 kap goa2 ti7-teh, ti7 goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7 po2-hou7 goa2, koh hou7 goa2 u7 mih8 thang chiah8, u7 saN thang chheng7,  21). hou7 goa2 an-jian5 to3-lai5 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 chhu3, chiu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak choe3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3.  22). Goa2 sou2 khia7 choe3 thiau7 e5 chioh8 beh choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3; kiN3-na7 Li2 sou2 siuN2-su3 goa2 e5, goa2 beh chiong chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 hian3 hou7 Li2.

[29]	Nga2-kok khi2-sin, kau3 tang-hng e5 lang5 e5 toe7;  2). khoaN3-kiN3 chhan5--nih u7 chit8 khau2 chiN2, u7 saN tin7 iuN5 to2 ti7 chiN2-piN, in-ui7 lang5 hou7 iuN5-kun5 lim, long2 si7 eng7 hit e5 chiN2 e5 chui2; chiN2-chhui3 eng7 toa7 chioh8 kham3.  3). Peng5-si5 iuN5-kun5 chu7-chip8 ti7-hia, lang5 chiu7 chiong chioh8-thau5 soa2 li7 chiN2-chhui3, hou7 iuN5 lim chui2; chiah koh chiong chioh8-thau5 soa2 kau3 goan5-ui7.  4). Nga2-kok tui3 in kong2, HiaN-ti7 ah, tui3 tah-loh8 lai5? in kong2, Goan2 tui3 Hap-lan5 lai5.  5). Mng7 in kong2, Na2-hok8 e5 sun Lah7-pan, lin2 bat i mah?  6). kong2, Bat--i.  Koh tui3 in kong2, I peng5-an mah? kong2, Peng5-an.  Li2 khoaN3, i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Lah8-kiat chhoa7 i e5 iuN5-kun5 teh lai5.  7). Kong2, Jit8 iau2 koaiN5, cheng-siN chu7-chip8 e5 si5 be7 kau3, m7-tat8--tioh8 hou7 iuN5 lim chui2, koh khi3 chhi7.  8). In kong2, Goan2 boe7-oe7, tioh8 theng3-hau7 choe7-choe7 tin7 long2 chu7-chip8, lang5 soa2 chioh8 li7-khui chiN2-chhui3, chiah thang hou7 iuN5 lim.  9). Nga2-kok teh kap in kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Lah8-kiat chhoa7 in lau7-pe7 e5 iuN5 lai5; in-ui7 si7 i teh kou3.  10). Nga2-kok khoaN3-kiN3 bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Lah8-kiat, kap bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan e5 iuN5-kun5, chiu7 chin3-cheng5 chiong chioh8 soa2 li7 chiN2-chhui3, hou7 in bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan e5 iuN5-kun5 lim.  11). Nga2-kok ka7 Lah8-kiat chim-chhui3, khui-siaN khau3.  12). Nga2-kok koh ka7 Lah8-kiat kong2 i si7 in lau7-pe7 e5 goe7-seng, si7 Li7-pek-ka e5 kiaN2; Lah8-kiat chiu7 chau2-khi3 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2.  13). Lah8-pan thiaN-kiN3 goe7-seng Nga2-kok e5 siau-sit, chiu7 chau2-khi3 ngia5-chih--i, pho7--i, kap i chim-chhui3; chhoa7 i kau3 in tau; Nga2-kok chiong it-chhe3 e5 su7-cheng5 ka7 Lah8-pan kong2.  14). Lah8-pan ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 sit8-chai7 si7 goa2 e5 kut-jiok8.  I chiu7 kap i toa3 chit8-geh8-jit8.  15). Lah8-pan ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 sui-jian5 si7 goa2 e5 chhin-chhek, kiam2 thang peh8-peh8 choe3 goa2 e5 kang; chhiaN2 ka7 goa2 kong2, li2 beh sim2-mih8 kang-chiN5.  16). Lah8-pan u7 nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, toa7--e5 mia5-kio3 Li7-a, soe3--e5 mia5-kio3 Lah8-kiat.  17). Li7-a bak8-chiu khah-su, Lah8-kiat siN-choe3 ho2-khoaN3.  18). Nga2-kok thiaN3 Lah8-kiat, chiu7 kong2, Goa2 goan7 ui7-tioh8 li2 soe3 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Lah8-kiat, ka7 li2 choe3-kang chhit-ni5.  19). Lah8-pan kong2, Chiong i ke3 hou7 li2, khah-ho2 hou7 pat8-lang5; li2 kap goa2 toa3.  20). Nga2-kok chiu7 ui7-tioh8 Lah8-kiat ka7 i choe3 kang chhit-ni5; in-ui7 chhim-thiaN3 i, khoaN3-choe3 kui2-na7 jit8.  21). Nga2-kok tui3 Lah8-pan kong2, Jit8-ki5 i2-keng moa2, kiu5 li2 chiong goa2 e5 bou2 hou7 goa2, goa2 thang kap i tang5-pang5.  22). Lah8-pan chu7-chip8 hit sou2-chai7 e5 cheng3-lang5, pan7 ian5-siah8 chhiaN2 in.  23). Kau3 jit8 am3, Lah8-pan chiong i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Li7-a, sang3 lai5 hou7 i; Nga2-kok chiu7 kap i tang5-pang5.  24). Lah8-pan chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-phaN3 hou7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Li7-a choe3 lu2-pi7.  25). Kau3 thiN-kng, chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 si7 Li7-a, chiu7 tui3 Lah8-pan kong2, Li2 ka7 goa2 choe3--e5, si7 sim2-mih8? Goa2 ka7 li2 choe3-kang, kiam2-m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 Lah8-kiat mah? li2 siaN2-su7 phian3 goa2?  26). Lah8-pan kong2, Be7 ke3 toa7--e5 tai7-seng ke3 soe3--e5, ti7 goan2 chia bo5 lang5 an2-ni choe3.  27). Li2 kap chit-e5 tioh8 moa2 chhit-jit8; goan2 chiu7 chiong hit-e5 iah8 ke3 hou7 li2; li2 ui7-tioh8 i koh ka7 goa2 choe3 kang chhit-ni5.  28). Nga2-kok chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5; kap chit-e5 moa2 chhit-jit8; i chiu7 chiong i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Lah8-kiat, hou7 i choe3-bou2.  29). Lah8-pan chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8, hou7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Lah8-kiat choe3 lu2-pi7.  30). Nga2-kok iah8 kap Lah8-kiat tang5-pang5, koh thiaN3 Lah8-kiat iaN5-ke3 Li7-a; chiu7 koh ka7 Lah8-pan choe3-kang chhit-ni5.
	31). Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3 Li7-a bo5 tek-thiong2, chiu7 hou7 i hoai5-in7; tok8-tok8 Lah8-kiat bo5.  32). Li7-a hoai5-in7 siN-kiaN2, chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 Liu5-pian7; in-ui7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 khou2-cheng5; taN goa2 e5 tiong7-hu beh thiaN3 goa2.  33). I koh hoai5-in7 siN kiaN2; kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa thiaN-kiN3 goa2 bo5 tek-thiong2, sou2-i2 koh hou7 goa2 chit e5 kiaN2; chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 Se-bian7.  34). Koh hoai5-in7 siN kiaN2, kong2, Goa2 ka7 tiong7-hu siN saN e5 kiaN2, i beh kap goa2 kiat-lian5; mia5 kio3 Li7-bi7.  35). Koh hoai5-in7 siN kiaN2; kong2, Chit-e7 goa2 beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; sou2-i2 kio3 i e5 mia5 Iu5-tai7; chiu7 theng5 bo5 koh siN.

[30]	Lah8-kiat khoaN3 pun2-sin bo5 ka7 Nga2-kok siN kiaN2, chiu7 oan3-tou3 i e5 toa7-chi2; tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 tioh8 kiaN2 hou7 goa2; na7 bo5, goa2 beh si2.  2). Nga2-kok siu7-khi3 Lah8-kiat; kong2, Hou7 li2 bo5 siN--e5, si7 Siong7-te3; goa2 kiam2 si7 thoe3 I mah?  3). Lah8-kiat kong2, Li2 khoaN3 goa2 e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 ti7-chia; li2 khi3 kap i tang5-pang5, hou7 i siN kiaN2 pho7 ti7 goa2 e5 kha-thau5-u; goa2 ia7 chiu7 thang tui3 i tit-tioh8 kiaN2.  4). Lah8-kiat chiu7 chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 hou7 i choe3-bou2; Nga2-kok chiu7 kap i tang5-pang5.  5). Phek-lah8 hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok siN chit8 e5 kiaN2.  6). Lah8-kiat kong2, Siong7-te3 ka7 goa2 phoaN3-toan3, iah8 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN, hou7 goa2 u7 kiaN2; sou2-i2 kio3 i e5 mia5 choe3 Tan3.  7). Lah8-kiat e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 koh hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok siN te7-ji7 e5 kiaN2;  8). Lah8-kiat kong2, Goa2 kap goa2 e5 toa7-chi2 hui-siong5 e5 saN-chiN, iah8 tit-tioh8 khah-iaN5; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 choe3 Na2-hut-tha-li7.  9). Li7-a khoaN3 pun2-sin theng5-hioh bo5 siN, chiu7 chiong i e5 lu2-pi7, Sek-phaN3, hou7 Nga2-kok choe3 bou2.  10). Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-phaN3 ka7 Nga2-kok siN kiaN2.  11). Li7-a kong2, Kai-chai3! chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 choe3 Ka-tek.  12). Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7, Sek-phaN3, koh ka7 Nga2-kok siN te7-ji7 e5 kiaN2.  13). Li7-a kong2, Goa2 u7 hok-khi3!  chiah e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 long2 beh chheng goa2 u7 hok-khi3; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 choe3 A-siat.  14). Koah-beh8 e5 si5, Liu5-pian7 khi3 chhan5--nih, tit-tioh8 hong-ka, theh8-lai5 hou7 i e5 lau7-bu2 Li7-a.  Lah8-kiat tui3 Li7-a kong2, ChhiaN2 chiong li2 e5 kiaN2 e5 hong-ka hou7 goa2.  15). Li7-a tui3 i kong2, Li2 chhiuN2-toat8 goa2 e5 tiong7-hu, kiam2-si7 sio2-khoa2 su7; li2 koh chhiuN2-toat8 goa2 e5 kiaN2 e5 hong-ka mah? Lah8-kiat kong2, Ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 kiaN2 e5 hong-ka, sou2-i2 kin-mi5 i thang kap li2 saN-kap khun3.  16). Kau3 am3, Nga2-kok tui3 chhan5--nih to3-lai5; Li7-a chhut-khi3 ngia5-chih i, kong2, Li2 tioh8 kap goa2 saN-kap khun3; in-ui7 goa2 sit8-chai7 eng7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 e5 hong-ka chhiaN3 li2.  Hit-mi5 i chiu7 kap i saN-kap khun3.  17). Siong7-te3 un2-chun2 Li7-a, i chiu7 hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok siN te7-gou7 e5 kiaN2.  18). Li7-a kong2, Siong7-te3 hou7 goa2 kang-chiN5, in-ui7 goa2 chiong lu2-pi7 hou7 goa2 e5 tiong7-hu; tui3 an2-ni ka7 i ho7-mia5 I2-sat-ka.  19). Li2-a koh hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok siN te7-lak8 e5 kiaN2.  20). Li7-a kong2, Siong7-te3 siuN2-su3 goa2 ho2 e5 siuN2-su3; goa2 e5 tiong7-hu beh kap goa2 toa3, in-ui7 goa2 ka7 i siN lak8 e5 kiaN2; tui3 an2-ni ka7 i ho7-mia5 Se-pou3-lun5.  21). Au7-lai5 siN chit8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 Ti2-na2.  22). Siong7-te3 siau3-liam7 Lah8-kiat, Siong7-te3 un2-chun2 i, hou7 i oe7 siN kiaN2.  23). I chiu7 hoai5-in7 siN kiaN2; kong2, Siong7-te3 tu5--khi3 goa2 e5 kian3-siau3;  24). chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 Iok-sek, kong2, Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa koh ke-thiN goa2 chit8 e5 kiaN2.
	25). Lah8-kiat siN Iok-sek liau2-au7, Nga2-kok tui3 Lah8-pan kong2, ChhiaN2 chhe goa2 khi3, hou7 goa2 to3-khi3 goa2 e5 pun2 sou2-chai7, pun2-toe7;  26). chhiaN2 li2 chiong goa2 hok8-sai7 li2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 bou2-kiaN2 hou7 goa2, iong5-un2 goa2 khi3; goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 hok8-sai7 li2, li2 long2 chai.  27). Lah8-pan ka7 i kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, chhiaN2 li2 kap goa2 toa3; in-ui7 goa2 chhim-chai Ia5-ho5-hoa su3 goa2 hok-khi3, si7 ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 ian5-kou3.  28). Koh ka7 i kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 tiaN7-tioh8 li2 e5 kang-chiN5, goa2 chiu7 hou7 li2.  29). Nga2-kok ka7 i kong2, Goa2 hok8-sai7 li2 chaiN2-iuN7, li2 e5 cheng-siN ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2-thau5 chaiN2-iuN7, si7 li2 sou2 chai.  30). Goa2 be7 lai5 e5 tai7-seng, li2 sou2-u7--e5 chin-chio2, taN chiu7 toa7 hoat-tat8; Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7 hok-khi3 te3 goa2 e5 kha lai5 hou7 li2; taN goa2 beh sim2-mih8 si5 ui7 goa2 e5 ke kian3-ti3 san2-giap8?  31). Lah8-pan kong2, Goa2 tioh8 hou7 li2 sim2-mih8? Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 iah8 m7-bian2 hou7 goa2 sim2-mih8; u7 chit8-hang7 su7, li2 na7 eng3-seng5, chiu7 goa2 iu5-goan5 chhi7 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5 lai5 kou3-siu2.  32). Kin-a2-jit8 goa2 beh pian3-sun5 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5, chiong mi5-iuN5-tiong kiN3-u7 tiam2--e5, u7 pan--e5, kap ou-sek--e5, i2-kip8 soaN-iuN5-tiong kiN3-u7 pan--e5, u7 tiam2--e5, long2 poah-chhut; chiong-lai5 chit-khoan2--e5 choe3 goa2 e5 kang-chiN5.  33). I2-au7 li2 lai5 khoaN3 goa2 e5 kang-chiN5, hit tiong-kan na7 soaN-iuN5 bo5 tiam2 bo5 pan--e5, mi5-iuN5 bo5 ou-sek--e5, chiu7 sng3 si7 goa2 thau--e5; eng7 an2-ni lai5 cheng3-beng5 goa2 e5 kong-to7.  34). Lah8-pan kong2, Ho2, goa2 goan7 chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 kiaN5.  35). Tng hit-jit8, chiu7 chiong u7 hun5 u7 pan e5 soaN-iuN5-kang2, u7 tiam2 u7 pan, kaiN3 peh8 e5 soaN-iuN5-bu2, i2-kip8 ou-sek e5 mi5-iuN5, long2 poah-chhut lai5 kau hou7 i hiah e5 kiaN2.  36). I hou7 ka-ki7 kap Nga2-kok saN-li7 u7 saN-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7; Nga2-kok chiu7 kou3 Lah8-pan ki5-u5 e5 iuN5.  37). Nga2-kok theh8 chhiN e5 iong5-chhiu7, heng7-chhiu7, png-chhiu7, nng2 e5 ki, chiong phe5 pak chiaN5 peh8-hun5, hou7 ki-lai7 peh8--e5 lou7-chhut.  38). Chiong pah-phe5 e5 ki, chhah ti7 iuN5 lim-chui2 e5 chui2-kau kap chui2-cho5, hou7 i kap iuN5 saN-tui3; iuN5 lai5 lim e5 si5, kang-bu2 kau-hap8;  39). iuN5 ti7 ki e5 tui3-bin7 kau-hap8, chiu7 siN u7-hun5--e5, u7-tiam2--e5, u7-pan--e5.  40). Nga2-kok chiong iuN5-a2 poah-chhut, hou7 Lah8-pan e5 iuN5 kap chiah e5 u7-hun5 kap ou-sek e5 iuN5 saN-tui3; chiong ka-ki7 e5 iuN5 leng7-goa7 pang3 ti7 chit8 sou2-chai7, bo5 hou7 i kap Lah8-pan e5 iuN5 chham-chhap.  41). Tu2-tioh8 iuN5-kun5-tiong iong2-chong3-e5 kau-hap8 e5 si5, Nga2-kok chiu7 eng7 chhiu7-ki chhah ti7 chui2-kau-lai7; hou7 iuN5 ti7 chhiu7-ki e5 tui3-bin7 kau-hap8.  42). Tu2-tioh8 iuN5-kun5 e5 san2--e5, chiu7 bo5 chhah chhiu7-ki; tui3 an2-ni san2--e5 kui Lah8-pan, iong2-chong3--e5 kui Nga2-kok.  43). Tui3 an2-ni i toa7 hoat-tat8, tit-tioh8 choe7-choe7 iuN5-kun5, lu2-pi7, lou5-pok8, lok8-to5, kap lu5.

[31]	Nga2-kok thiaN-kiN3 Lah8-pan cheng3-kiaN2 u7 oe7 kong2, Lan2 lau7-pe7 sou2-u7--e5, Nga2-kok long2 chhiuN2-khi3, koh tui3 lan2 e5 lau7-pe7 tit-tioh8 chit-e5 it-chhe3 e5 eng5-kng.  2). Nga2-kok khoaN3-kiN3 Lah8-pan kiN3-tioh8 i, bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 chiong5-cheng5 e5 bin7-sek.  3). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 tioh8 to3--khi3 li2 e5 pe7-kong e5 toe7, kau3 li2 e5 chhin-chok8 hia; Goa2 beh kap li2 ti7-teh.  4). Nga2-kok chhe lang5 kio3 Lah8-kiat kap Li7-a kau3 soaN-ia2, kau3 iuN5-kun5 hia;  5). tui3 in kong2, Goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 lin2 lau7-pe7 kiN3-tioh8 goa2, bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 chiong5-cheng5 e5 bin7-sek; chong2-si7 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 si5-siong5 kap goa2 ti7-teh.  6). Lin2 iah8 chai goa2 chin7 goa2 e5 lat8 choe3 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 kang.  7). Lin2 lau7-pe7 phian3 goa2, chap8-pai2 koe2-oaN7 goa2 e5 kang-chiN5; chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 bo5 iong5-un2 i hai7 goa2.  8). I na7 kong2, U7-tiam2--e5 kui li2 choe3 kang-chiN5, chiu7 iuN5-kun5 sou2 siN--e5 long2 u7-tiam2; i na7 kong2, U7-hun5--e5 kui li2 choe3 kang-chiN5, chiu7 iuN5-kun5 sou2 siN--e5 long2 u7-hun5.  9). An2-ni Siong7-te3 chiong lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 cheng-siN chhiuN2-lai5 hou7 goa2.  10). IuN5 kau-hap8 e5 si5, goa2 bang7-tiong kiah8-bak8 chit8-e7 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 phah iuN5-bu2 e5 iuN5-kang2, long2 si7 u7-hun5--e5, u7-tiam2--e5, u7 hoe-pan--e5;  11). Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 ti7 hit bang7-tiong kio3 goa2 kong2, Nga2-kok; goa2 kong2, Goa2 ti7 chia.  12). I kong2, Li2 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3, phah iuN5-bu2 e5 iuN5-kang2, long2 si7 u7-hun5--e5, u7-tiam2--e5, u7 hoe-pan--e5; hoan7-na7 Lah8-pan tui3 li2 sou2 choe3--e5, Goa2 long2 khoaN3-kiN3.  13). Goa2 si7 Pek-tek8-li7 e5 Siong7-te3, li2 ti7-hia bat eng7 iu5 boah thiau7, tui3 Goa2 he7-goan7.  TaN li2 tioh8 khi2-lai5, li2-khui chit sou2-chai7, to3-khi3 pun2-toe7.  14). Lah8-kiat kap Li7-a in3 i kong2, Ti7 goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, kiam2 iau2 u7 goan2 thang tit e5 ke-he2 kap san2-giap8 mah?  15). Goan2 kiam2-m7-si7 hou7 i khoaN3-choe3 goa7-lang5 mah? in-ui7 i boe7 goan2, thun-chiah8 goan2 e5 ke3-chiN5;  16). Siong7-te3 tui3 goan2 lau7-pe7 chhiuN2-chhut it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8, hiah-e5 chiu7-si7 goan2 kap goan2 kiaN2 e5.  TaN kiN3-na7 Siong7-te3 sou2 tui3 li2 kong2--e5, choe3 li2 khi3 kiaN5.  17). Nga2-kok chiu7 khi2-lai5, hou7 i e5 kiaN2 kap bou2 long2 khia5 lok8-to5.  18). Koh toa3 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, kap sou2 chek-chu7 e5 chai5-but8, sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 cheng-siN, si7 ti7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 sou2 tit-tioh8-e5; beh khi3 Ka-lam5 toe7, khi3 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat hia.  19). Hit-si5 Lah8-pan khi3 chian2 iuN5-mng5; Lah8-kiat thau-theh8 in lau7-pe7 ke-lai7 e5 ngou2-siong7.  20). Nga2-kok poe7 A-lan5 lang5 Lah8-pan, thau-chau2 khi3, bo5 ka7 i kong2.  21). Chiu7 toa3 it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 to5-chau2; i khi2-sin ke3 hit e5 Ho5, ng3 Ki-liat8 soaN khi3.
	22). Kau3 te7-saN jit8, u7 lang5 ka7 Lah8-pan kong2, Nga2-kok chau2-khi3 lah.  23). I chiu7 chhoa7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 saN-kap khi3 tui-jip; lek8-ke3 chhit-jit8 e5 lou7-cham7, kau3 Ki-liat8 soaN chiah jip-tioh8.  24). Mi5--si5 bin5-bang7-tiong, Siong7-te3 kau3 A-lan5 lang5 Lah8-pan hia; ka7 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 sio2-sim, m7-thang kap Nga2-kok kong2-ho2 kong2-phaiN2.  25). Lah8-pan tui-tioh8 Nga2-kok, Nga2-kok ti7 hit e5 soaN i2-keng tah pou3-piN5; Lah8-pan kap i e5 cheng3 hiaN-ti7, iah8 ti7 Ki-liat8 soaN tah pou3-piN5.  26). Lah8-pan ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 sou2 choe3 si7 sim2-mih8 su7, li2 siaN2-su7 poe7 goa2, chiong goa2 chiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chhoa7--khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 eng7 to-kiam3 chhiuN2-liah8 chit8-iuN7?  27). Li2 siaN2-su7 am3-chiN7 chau2, thau-chau2 iah8 bo5 ka7 goa2 kong2; hou7 goa2 thang eng7 hoaN-hi2, chhiuN3-koa, phah-kou2, toaN5-khim5, sang3 li2 to3-khi3?  28). Koh bo5 iong5-un2 goa2 kap goa7-sun, cha-bou2-kiaN2 chim-chhui3? li2 taN sou2 kiaN5 si7 chin gong7.  29). Goa2 e5 chhiu2 pun2 u7 lat8 thang hai7 lin2; tok8-tok8 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 cha7-mi5 ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 sio2-sim, m7-thang kap Nga2-kok kong2-ho2 kong2-phaiN2.  30). TaN li2 sui-jian5 loan5-bou7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, put-tek-put tioh8 khi3, siaN2-su7 thau-theh8 goa2 e5 sin5-beng5?  31). Nga2-kok in3 Lah8-pan kong2, In-ui7 goa2 kiaN, sim-lai7 siuN7, kong2, KiaN-liau2 li2 chiong li2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 tui3 goa2 chhiuN2--khi3.  32). Lun7-kau3 li2 e5 sin5-beng5, li2 tui3 sim2-mih8 lang5 chhiau-tioh8, i chiu7 tioh8 si2; tng lan2 cheng3 hiaN-ti7 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 jin7-khoaN3, ti7 goa2 chia u7 sim2-mih8 mih8 si7 li2-e5, thang theh8--khi3.  In-ui7 Nga2-kok m7-chai Lah8-kiat u7 thau-theh8--in.  33). Lah8-pan chiu7 jip8 Nga2-kok e5 pou3-piN5, Li2-a e5 pou3-piN5, kap nng7 e5 lu2-pi7 e5 pou3-piN5, long2 chhiau-bo5; chiu7 tui3 Li7-a e5 pou3-piN5 chhut-lai5, jip8 Lah8-kiat e5 pou3-piN5.  34). Lah8-kiat i2-keng chiong ngou2-siong7 khng3 ti7 lok8-to5 e5 oaN-e7, lai5 che7 ti7 hit teng2-bin7.  Lah8-pan ti7 i e5 pou3-piN5-lai7 si3-koe3 bong, long2 chhiau-bo5.  35). Lah8-kiat tui3 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Keng-ki5 tu2-a2 kau3, boe7-oe7 khi2-lai5 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; kiu5 goa2 e5 chu2 boh8-tit siu7-khi3.  Lah8-pan si3-koe3 chhe7 ngou2-siong7, chhiau long2 bo5.  36). Nga2-kok chiu7 siu7-khi3, kap Lah8-pan ke3-kau3; tui3 Lah8-pan kong2, Goa2 u7 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih8 ke3-sit, u7 sim2-mih8 choe7-ok, li2 keng2-jian5 jip goa2 chiah-kin2?  37). Li2 pian3-bong goa2 it-chhe3 e5 ke-si, u7 chhiau-tioh8 lin2 tau sim2-mih8 ke-si chhut lai5? thang he7 ti7 li2 goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 bin7-cheng5; ho7 in ti7 lan2 nng7-lang5 e5 tiong-kan phoaN3-toan3.  38). Goa2 kap li2 toa3 chi2 ji7-chap8 ni5, li2 e5 mi5-iuN5-bu2, soaN-iuN5-bu2 m7-bat u7 lau3-the; li2 iuN5-kun5-tiong e5 iuN5-kang2, goa2 be7-bat chiah8--i.  39). Hou7 ia2-siu3 siong-hai7--e5, goa2 bo5 toa3-lai5 hou7 li2; goa2 pun2-sin che7-giah8; bo5 lun7 jit8--si5 siu7-thau, mi5-si5 siu7-thau, li2 long2 tui3 goa2 tho2-pe5.  40). Goa2 jit8--si5 hou7 jit8 phak8, mi5--si5 hou7 sng tang3, long2 boe7-kou3-tit khun3, goa2 siong5-siong5 si7 an2-ni.  41). Goa2 chi2 ji7-chap8-ni5 ti7 li2 e5 ke, ui7-tioh8 li2 nng7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, ka7 li2 choe3-kang chap8-si3 ni5; ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 iuN5-kun5 lak8 ni5; li2 chap8-pai2 koe2-oaN7 goa2 e5 kang-chiN5.  42). Na7 m7-si7 u7 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, koh si7 I2-sat sou2 kiaN-ui3--e5, kap goa2 ti7-teh; li2 taN un2-tang3 hou7 goa2 khang-chhiu2 khi3.  Siong7-te3 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 e5 khou2-cheng5, kap goa2 e5 lo5-lok8, chiah ti7 cha7-mi5 chek-pi7 li2.  43). Lah8-pan in3 Nga2-kok kong2, Chiah e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 si7 goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; chiah e5 gin2-a2 si7 goa2 e5 gin2-a2; chiah e5 iuN5-kun5 iah8 si7 goa2 e5 iuN5-kun5; hoan7-na7 li2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3--e5, long2 si7 goa2 e5; goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, kap in sou2 siN e5 gin2-a2; kin-a2-jit8 goa2 oe7 ka7 in choe3 sim2-mih8?  44). TaN lai5, lan2 nng7-lang5 thang lai5 lip8-iok, ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan choe3 cheng3-ku3.
	45). Nga2-kok chhu2 chioh8, khia7 choe3 thiau7.  46). Nga2-kok tui3 chiah e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khioh chioh8-thau5; in chiu7 chiong chioh8-thau5 khioh lai5 thiap8 kui-tui; tai7-ke chiu7 ti7 hit tui e5 piN-a2 chiah8.  47). Lah8-pan mia5 i kio3 I-ka-ni2-sat-khap-tou7-tha; Nga2-kok mia5 i kio3 Ka-lui7-tek.  48). Lah8-pan kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 chit e5 chioh8-tui choe3 li2 goa2 tiong-kan e5 cheng3-ku3.  In-ui7 an2-ni, mia5 i kio3 Ka-lui7-tek;  49). ia7 kio3-choe3 Bi2-su-pa; chiu7-si7 kong2, Lan2 tai7-ke li7-piat8 i2-au7, goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan kam3-chhat.  50). Li2 na7 khou2-chhou2 goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, koh ti7 goa2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 i2-goa7 leng7-goa7 chhoa7-bou2, sui-jian5 bo5 lang5 kap lan2 ti7-teh, u7 Siong7-te3 ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan choe3 kan-cheng3.  51). Lah8-pan koh tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 khoaN3 chit tui chioh8, li2 khoaN3 chit ki thiau7; chiu7-si7 goa2 sou2 he7 ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan--e5.  52). Chit tui chioh8 choe3 kan-cheng3, chit ki thiau7 choe3 kan-cheng3; goa2 bo5 beh ke3 chit tui chioh8 khi3 hai7 li2, li2 ia7 m7-thang ke3 chit tui chioh8 kap thiau7, lai5 hai7 goa2.  53). Goan7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, Na2-hok8 e5 Siong7-te3, in lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan phoaN3-toan3.  Nga2-kok chiu7 ki2 in lau7-pe7 I2-sat sou2 kiaN-ui3 e5 Siong7-te3 lai5 chiu3-choa7.  54). Nga2-kok ti7 soaN--nih hian3-che3, chhiaN2 i hiah e5 hiaN-ti7 lai5 chiah8; in chiah8-liau2, chiu7 ti7 soaN--nih hioh-mi5.  55). Lah8-pan thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, kap i e5 goa7-sun, kap i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 chim-chhui3, ka7 in chiok-hok; chiu7 khi2-sin to3--khi3 ka-ki7 e5 sou2-chai7.

[32]	Nga2-kok koh kiaN5 i e5 lou7, Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 tu2-tioh8 i.  2). Nga2-kok khoaN3-kiN3 in, chiu7 kong2, Che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 kun-tui7; sou2-i2 mia5 hit sou2-chai7 kio3 Ma2-khap-liam7.
	3). Nga2-kok chhe lang5 tai7-seng khi3 Se-jiN2 e5 toe7, I2-tong e5 chhan5, kiN3 i e5 hiaN I2-so3.  4). Hoan-hu3 in kong2, Lin2 ka7 goa2 e5 chu2 I2-so3 kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ti7 Lah8-pan hia kia3-ku, toa3 kau3 kin-a2-jit8.  5). goa2 u7 gu5, lu5, iuN5-kun5, lou5-pok8, lu2-pi7; taN chhe lang5 lai5 po3 goa2 e5 chu2, ai3 tit ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2.  6). Sou2 chhe e5 lang5 to3--lai5 Nga2-kok hia kong2, Goan2 kau3 li2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 hia, i tu2-tu2 teh lai5 beh ngia5-chih li2; koh u7 si3-pah lang5 kap i lai5.  7). Nga2-kok toa7 kiaN koh peh-pak; chiong hiah-e5 kap i saN-kap ti7-teh e5 lang5, kap iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, lok8-to5, pun choe3 nng7 tui7;  8). kong2, I2-so3 na7 lai5 kong-kek chit-tui7, chhun-e5 hit-tui7 iau2 thang to5-chau2.  9). Nga2-kok koh kong2, Goa2 e5 chou2, A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 pe7 I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat tui3 goa2 kong2, To3-khi3 li2 e5 pun2-toe7 pun2-chok8, Goa2 beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2.  10). Li2 tui3 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 sou2 si it-chhe3 e5 chu5-ai3 kap it-chhe3 e5 seng5-sit8, chiu7 chi3-bi5-soe3 e5, goa2 ia7 boe7 kham-tit tit-tioh8; goa2 cheng5 kiah8 goa2 e5 koaiN2-a2, ke3 chit e5 Iok-tan3 ho5; taN goa2 i2-keng chiaN5-choe3 nng7-tui7.  11). Kiu5 Li2 kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 e5 chhiu2; in-ui7 goa2 kiaN i, kiaN-liau2 i lai5 thai5-si2 goa2 kap in bu2-kiaN2.  12). Li2 ia7 bat kong2, Goa2 tek-khak beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2; hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-piN e5 soa, choe7 kau3 boe7-sng3-tit.  13). Hit-mi5 Nga2-kok hioh ti7-hia; chiu7 ti7 i sou2 u7 e5 mih8 e5 lai7-bin7, keng2-chhut le2-mih8, beh sang3 i e5 hiaN I2-so3;  14). soaN-iuN5-bu2 nng7-pah chiah, soaN-iuN5-kang ji7-chap8 chiah, mi5-iuN5-bu2 nng7-pah chiah, mi5-iuN5-kang ji7-chap8 chiah;  15). lok8-to5-bu2 kap chiah8-ni e5 kiaN2 saN-chap8 chiah, gu5-bu2 si3-chap8 chiah, gu5-kang2 chap8 chiah, lu5-bu2 ji7-chap8 chiah, lu5-kiaN2 chap8-chiah.  16). Kok-iuN7 leng7-goa7 chit8-kun5, kau-tai3 lou5-pok8; ka7 lou5-pok8 kong2, Lin2 tai7-seng goa2 khi3, hou7 tak8-kun5 u7 saN-li7.  17). Koh hoan-hu3 choe3-thau5--e5, kong2, Goa2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 tu2-tioh8 li2 e5 si5, na7 mng7 li2 kong2, Li2 si7 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5? beh khi3 tah-loh8? li2 thau5-cheng5 hiah-e5 chi7-chui7 e5?  18). li2 tioh8 kong2, Si7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok e5; si7 beh sang3 goa2 e5 chu2 I2-so3 e5 le2-mih8; hian7-chai7 i pun2-sin iah8 ti7 goan2 e5 au7-bin7.  19). Koh hoan-hu3 te7-ji7 te7-saN, kap it-chhe3 koaN2 kui-kun5 cheng-siN e5 lang5, kong2, Lin2 tu2-tioh8 I2-so3 e5 si5, iah8 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni ka7 i kong2.  20). Koh lin2 iah8 tioh8 kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 Nga2-kok ti7 goan2 e5 au7-bin7.  In-ui7 Nga2-kok ka-ki7 phah-sng3 kong2, Goa2 eng7 ti7 goa2 thau5-cheng5 khi3 e5 le2-mih8 lai5 koe2 i e5 hun7; jian5-au7 goa2 kiN3-tioh8 i e5 bin7, kiam2-chhai2 i chiap-lap8 goa2.  21). Tui3 an2-ni, le2-mih8 seng kiaN5; hit-mi5 Nga2-kok hioh ti7 tui7-tiong.
	22). I mi5--si5 khi2-lai5, chhoa7 i nng7 e5 bou2, nng7 e5 lu2-pi7, kap chap8-it e5 kiaN2, long2 ke3 Nga2-pok8 e5 tou7-thau5.  23). Tai7-seng hou7 in ke3-khoe; hoan7 sou2-u7--e5 iah8 hou7 in ke3.  24). Chi2-u7 chhun Nga2-kok ka-ki7 ti7-teh; u7 chit8-lang5 lai5 kap i saN-ian2, kau3 ti7 thiN-phu2-kng.  25). Hit-lang5 khoaN3 boe7 iaN5--i; chiu7 sian3 Nga2-kok e5 toa7-thui2-khu7; saN-ian2 e5 si5, Nga2-kok e5 toa7-thui2-khu7 choah8-tioh8.  26). Hit-lang5 kong2, ThiN beh kng lah, tioh8 pang3 goa2 khi3.  Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 na7 bo5 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok, m7 pang3 li2 khi3.  27). Hit-lang5 kong2, Li2 mia5 choe3 sim2-mih8? i kong2, Goa2 mia5 choe3 Nga2-kok.  28). Hit-lang5 kong2, Li2 e5 mia5 bo5 beh koh kio3 Nga2-kok, beh kio3-choe3 I2-sek-liat8; in-ui7 li2 kap Siong7-te3 kap lang5 tau3 su-iaN5, long2 tit-tioh8 khah-iaN5.  29). Nga2-kok mng7 i kong2, ChhiaN2 chiong li2 e5 mia5 ka7 goa2 kong2.  Hit lang5 in3 kong2, Mih-sai2 mng7 goa2 e5 mia5? chiu7 ti7-hia ka7 i chiok-hok.  30). Nga2-kok mia5 Hit sou2-chai7 kio3 Pian7-i2-li7, in-ui7 kong2, Goa2 tng-thau5 tui3-bin7 kiN3-tioh8 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 siN3-mia7 iau2 tit-tioh8 po2-choan5.  31). Jit8 tu2-a2 chhut, Nga2-kok keng-ke3 Pian7-i2-li7; i e5 toa7-thui2 i2-keng pai2.  32). Sou2-i2 chiah e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 bo5 chiah8 toa7-thui2-thau5 e5 kun, kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8; in-ui7 hit-lang5 sian3 Nga2-kok thui2-khu7 e5 toa7-kun.

[33]	Nga2-kok kiah8-bak8 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 I2-so3 lai5; koh u7 si3-pah lang5 kap i lai5.  I chiu7 chiong hiah e5 gin2-a2 pun-khui, kau hou7 Li7-a, kau hou7 Lah8-kiat, kau hou7 nng7 e5 lu2-pi7.  2). Chiong lu2-pi7 kap in e5 kiaN2 pai5 ti7 thau5-cheng5, Li2-a kap i e5 kiaN2 pai5 ti7 au7-bin7, Lah8-kiat kap Iok-sek pai5 ti7 lou7-be2.  3). I pun2-sin ti7 in e5 thau5-cheng5 ke3--khi3, lian5-lian5 chhit-pai2 phak ti7 toe7--nih, chiah oa2-kun7 i e5 hiaN.  4). I2-so3 chau2-lai5 ngia5-chih i, chiong i pho7--teh, koh lam2 i e5 am7-kun2, chim i; nng7-lang5 chiu7 thi5-khau3.  5). I2-so3 kiah8-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap gin2-a2, chiu7 kong2, Chiah-e5 kap li2 tang5-kiaN5--e5 si7 chi7-chui7? Nga2-kok kong2, Chiah e5 gin2-a2 si7 Siong7-te3 si-un hou7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8--e5.  6). Tui3 hit-tiap8 nng7 e5 lu2-pi7, kap in e5 gin2-a2, chin3-cheng5 lai5 pai3.  7). Li7-a kap i e5 gin2-a2 iah8 chin3-cheng5 lai5 pai3; lou7-be2 Iok-sek kap Lah8-kiat iah8 chin3-cheng5 lai5 pai3.  8). I2-so3 kong2, Goa2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 kui-kun5 e5 cheng-siN, li2 si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3? Nga2-kok kong2, Si7 beh ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2.  9). I2-so3 kong2, Sio2-ti7 ah, goa2-e5 i2-keng kau3-giah8, li2-e5 iu5-goan5 kui li2.  10). Nga2-kok kong2, Boh8 an2-ni, goa2 na7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, kiu5 li2 tui3 goa2 e5 chhiu2 siu goa2 e5 le2-mih8; in-ui7 goa2 kiN3-tioh8 li2 e5 bin7, chhin-chhiuN7 kiN3-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7, li2 iah8 chiap-lap8 goa2;  11). kiu5 li2 siu goa2 toa3--lai5 hou7 li2 e5 le2-mih8; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 un-tian2 goa2, hou7 goa2 chhiong-chiok; pek--i, jian5-au7 siu.  12). I2-so3 kong2, Lan2 khi2-sin lai5 khi3, goa2 choe3-thau5 kiaN5.  13). Nga2-kok tui3 i kong2, goa2 e5 chu2 chai chiah e5 gin2-a2 nng2-chiaN2, gu5-iuN5 iah8 tu2-a2 siN; na7 choe3 chit8-jit8 koaN2, kui-kun5 long2 beh si2.  14). Kiu5 goa2 e5 chu2 ti7 lou5-pok8 e5 thau5-cheng5 kiaN5, goa2 beh chiau3 ti7 goa2 bin7-cheng5 kui-kun5 cheng-siN e5 lek8-liong7, iah8 chiau3 gin2-a2 e5 lek8-liong7, ban7-ban7 chin3-cheng5, kiaN5 kau3 Se-jiN2, kau3 goa2 e5 chu2 hia.  15). I2-so3 kong2, Iong5-un2 goa2 chiong te3 goa2 e5 lang5 lau5 kui2-e5 kap li2 choe3-tin7.  Nga2-kok kong2, Mih-sai2 an2-ni? ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 chiu7 ho2.  16). Hit-jit8 I2-so3 khi2-sin, chiau3 goan5-lou7 to3--khi3 Se-jiN2.  17). Nga2-kok kiaN5 kau3 Sou3-kat, ti7-hia ui7 pun2-sin khi2-chhu3, ui7 cheng-siN tah chhau2-liau5; sou2-i2 mia5 hit sou2-chai7 choe3 Sou3-kat.
	18). Nga2-kok tui3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 to3--lai5 e5 si5, peng5-an kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Si7-kiam3 siaN5; ti7 siaN5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tah pou3-piN5.  19). Eng7 chit8-pah te3 gun5, tui3 Si7-kiam3 e5 lau7-pe7 Hap-boat e5 kiaN2-sun, boe2 i tah pou3-piN5 hit te3 toe7;  20). ti7-hia khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, ka7 i ho7 mia5 kio3 I-li7 I-lo5-i I2-sek-liat8.

[34]	Li7-a ka7 Nga2-kok sou2 siN e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Ti2-na2, chhut-khi3 beh kiN3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2.  2). Hit sou2-chai7 e5 bok8-pek Hi-bi7 lang5 Hap-boat e5 kiaN2 Si7-kiam3 khoaN3-kiN3 i; chiu7 khiu2--i, kap i saN-kap khun3, leng5-jiok8 i.  3). I e5 sim loan5-bou7 Nga2-kok e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Ti2-na2; thiaN3 chit e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, eng7 ho2-oe7 an-ui3 i.  4). Si7-kiam3 ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 Hap-boat, kong2, Kiu5 li2 ka7 goa2 pheng3 chit e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 choe3-bou2.  5). Nga2-kok thiaN-kiN3 i phah la5-sam5 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Ti2-na2; hit-si5 i hiah e5 kiaN2 kap i e5 cheng-siN ti7 soaN--nih; Nga2-kok cheng7-cheng7 bo5 choe3 siaN, theng3-hau7 in to3-lai5.  6). Si7-kiam3 e5 lau7-pe7, Hap-boat, chhut-lai5 kiN3 Nga2-kok, beh kap i kong2-oe7.  7). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kiaN2 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 tui3 soaN-nih to3--lai5, tak8-e5 m7 kam-goan7, chap8-hun siu7-khi3; in-ui7 Si7-kiam3 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 choe3 chhut kian3-siau3 e5 tai7-chi3, kap Nga2-kok e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 saN-kap khun3; che pun2 si7 m7 eng-kai choe3 e5 su7.  8). Hap-boat kap in chham-siong5 kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2 Si7-kiam3 e5 sim him-bou7 lin2 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2; kiu5 lin2 chiong i hou7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 choe3-bou2.  9). Lin2 kap goan2 tai7-ke kiat-chhin; lin2 thang chiong lin2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 hou7 goan2, lin2 iah8 thang chhoa7 goan2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.  10). Lin2 kap goan2 saN-kap khia7-khi3; toe7 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5, lin2 toa3 chia khia7, choe3 seng-li2, kian3-ti3 san2-giap8.  11). Si7-kiam3 tui3 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap i e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Goan7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2; lin2 sou2 tui3 goa2 kong2--e5 goa2 beh hou7 lin2.  12). Chhut-chai7 lin2 beh tui3 goa2 tho2 joa7-choe7 pheng3-kim, kap le2-mih8, goa2 tek-khak chiau3 lin2 sou2 kong2--e5 hou7 lin2; chi2-u7 ai3 lin2 eng7 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 hou7 goa2 choe3-bou2.  13). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kiaN2, in-ui7 Si7-kiam3 phah la5-sam5 in e5 sio2-be7 Ti2-na2, chiu7 eng7 kan-cha3 e5 oe7 lai5 in3 Si7-kiam3, kap i e5 lau7-pe7, Hap-boat, tui3 in kong2,  14). Chiong goan2 e5 sio2-be7 hou7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 choe3-bou2, che e5 tai7-chi3 goan2 boe7-choe3-tit; in-ui7 he si7 goan2 e5 kian3-siau3.  15). Lin2 sou2 u7 e5 ta-pou-lang5, na7 long2 siu7 kat-le2 chhin-chhiuN7 goan2 chit8-iuN7, u7 chi2 chit8-hang7 chiah thang eng3-un2 lin2;  16). goan2 chiu7 chiong goan2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 hou7 lin2, goan2 iah8 chhoa7 lin2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; goan2 chiu7 kap lin2 saN-kap toa3, chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 peh-siN3.  17). Siat-su2 lin2 m7-thiaN goan2 e5 oe7 lai5 siu7 kat-le2, goan2 chiu7 toa3 goan2 e5 sio2-be7 lai5 khi3.  18). Hap-boat kap i e5 kiaN2 Si7-kiam3, hoaN-hi2 in e5 oe7.  19). Hit e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 choe3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, long2 bo5 ian5-chhian5; in-ui7 i thiaN3 Nga2-kok e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; koh i ti7 in lau7-pe7 e5 ke te7-it chun-kui3.  20). Hap-boat, kap i e5 kiaN2 Si7-kiam3, lai5 kau3 pun2-siaN5 e5 mng5-khau2, ka7 pun2-siaN5 e5 lang5 kong2,  21). Chiah e5 lang5 kap lan2 ho5-ho2; m7-tat8--tioh8 chun2 in ti7 chit e5 toe7 khia7-khi2, choe3 seng-li2; koh chit e5 toe7 iah8 khui-khoah, oe7 iong5-un2--tit in; lan2 thang chhoa7 in e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 choe3-bou2, iah8 thang chiong lan2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 ke3 hou7 in.  22). Tok8-tok8 tioh8 u7 chit8-hang7, hiah-e5 chiah beh un2 lan2, kap lan2 khia7-khi2, chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 peh-siN3; chiu7-si7 lan2 tiong-kan sou2 u7 e5 ta-pou-lang5 long2 tioh8 siu7 kat-le2, chhin-chhiuN7 in siu7 kat-le2 chit8-iuN7.  23). I e5 gu5, iuN5, chai5-san2, kap it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, kiam2 bo5 long2 kui ti7 lan2 mah? chi2-u7 tioh8 un2--in, in chiu7 beh kap lan2 toa3.  24). KiN3-na7 tui3 siaN5-mng5 chhut-lai5 e5 lang5 long2 thiaN-than3 Hap-boat kap i e5 kiaN2 Si7-kiam3 e5 oe7; tui3 an2-ni kiN3-na7 tui3 siaN5-mng5 chhut-lai5 e5 ta-pou-lang5 long2 siu7 kat-le2.  25). Kau3 te7-saN jit8, cheng3-lang5 tng teh thang3-thiaN3 e5 si5, Nga2-kok nng7 e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Ti2-na2 e5 hiaN Se-bian7 kap Li7-bi7, long2 kiah8-to, than3 lang5 bo5 tiuN-ti5, lai5 kau3 siaN5-lai7, thai5-si2 long2-chong2 e5 ta-pou-lang5.  26). Ia7 eng7 to thai5-si2 Hap-boat kap i e5 kiaN2 Si7-kiam3; chhoa7 Ti2-na2 tui3 Si7-kiam3 e5 chhu3 chhut-lai5, chiu7 khi3.  27). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kiaN2, ui7-tioh8 in sio2-be7 siu7 phah la5-sam5, chiu7 lai5 kau3 siu7-thai5 e5 lang5 hia, chhiuN2-kiap in e5 siaN5.  28). ChhiuN2 in e5 iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap lu5; i2-kip8 siaN5-lai7 kap chhan5--nih sou2 u7 e5.  29). Koh chiong in it-chhe3 e5 he3-mih8 chiN5-chai5, it-chhe3 e5 gin2-a2 kap hu7-jin5-lang5, i2-kip8 tak8 te3 chhu3 sou2-u7--e5, long2 chhiuN2, liah8 chiu7 khi3.  30). Nga2-kok ka7 Se-bian7 kap Li7-bi7 kong2, Lin2 lian5-lui7 goa2, hou7 goa2 ti7 chit sou2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan, chiu7-si7 ti7 Ka-lam5 lang5 kap Pi2-li7-se2 lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 chhau3-mia5.  Koh goa2 e5 lang5-giah8 chio2; in tek-khak chu7-chip8 lai5 kong-kek goa2, phah goa2; goa2 kap choan5-ke e5 lang5 long2 oe7 biat8-bo5.  31). In kong2, I kiam2 thang khoan2-thai7 goan2 sio2-be7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiong-ki mah?

[35]	Siong7-te3 ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Khi2--ah, chiuN7-khi3 Pek-tek8-li7, toa3 ti7-hia.  Koh tioh8 ti7-hia ka7 Siong7-te3 khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, chiu7-si7 li2 siam2-pi7 li2 e5 hiaN I2-so3 e5 bin7 e5 si5, tui3 li2 chhut-hian7--e5, hit-e5.  2). Nga2-kok chiu7 ka7 choan5-ke i2-kip8 it-chhe3 kap i ti7-teh e5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 tu5-khi3 lin2 tiong-kan goa7-pang e5 siong7-te3; iah8 tioh8 ka-ki7 chheng-khi3, oaN7 lin2 e5 i-chiuN5.  3). Lan2 tioh8 khi2-lai5, chiuN7-khi3 Pek-tek8-li7; ti7-hia goa2 beh ka7 Siong7-te3 khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, chiu7-si7 ti7 goa2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, un2-chun2 goa2 e5 ki5-to2, ti7 goa2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7 kap goa2 ti7-teh, hit-e5.  4). In chiu7 chiong in chhiu2-lai7 sou2 u7 iN7-pang e5 sin5-beng5, kap in e5 hi7-kau, long2 hou7 Nga2-kok; Nga2-kok chiong hiah-e5 tai5 ti7 Si7-kiam3 hit-ui7 e5 siong7-chhiu7-kha.  5). In chiu7 khi2-sin, Siong7-te3 hou7 si3-chiu-ui5 e5 siaN5 e5 lang5 long2 chin kiaN; in chiu7 bo5 tui-jip Nga2-kok e5 cheng3-kiaN2.  6). Nga2-kok, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 kap i choe3-tin7 e5 lang5, kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Lou7-su, chiu7-si7 Pek-tek8-li7.  7). I ti7-hia khi2 chit8 cho7 toaN5, chiu7 ka7 hit sou2-chai7 ho7-mia5, kio3 I-lek8-pek-tek8-li7; in-ui7 i siam2-pi7 i e5 hiaN e5 si5, Siong7-te3 ti7-hia tui3 i chhut-hian7.  8). Li7-pek-ka e5 ni-bu2 Ti2-pho3-lat si2; chiu7 bai5-chong3 ti7 Pek-tek8-li7 e5 e7-bin7, siong7-chhiu7-kha; sou2-i2 kio3 i e5 mia5 A-lun5-pa-kou2.
	9). Nga2-kok tui3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 to3--lai5, Siong7-te3 koh tui3 i chhut-hian7, su3-hok hou7 i.  10). Siong7-te3 koh ka7 i kong2, Li2 mia5 si7 Nga2-kok; taN i2-au7 li2 e5 mia5 bo5 koh kio3 Nga2-kok, beh mia5 kio3 I2-sek-liat8; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 I2-sek-liat8.  11). Siong7-te3 koh ka7 i kong2, Goa2 si7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3; li2 tioh8 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7; chiong-lai5 u7 chit8-kok, koh u7 choe7-choe7 kok, tui3 li2 lai5 siN, koh u7 kun-ong5 tui3 li2 siN-chhut.  12). Goa2 sou2 hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kap I2-sat e5 toe7, Goa2 beh hou7 li2, iah8 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 hou7 li2 e5 hou7-e3.  13). Siong7-te3 chiu7 tui3 kap i kong2-oe7 e5 sou2-chai7 chiuN7-khi3.  14). Nga2-kok chiu7 ti7 Siong7-te3 kap i kong2-oe7 e5 sou2-chai7, khia7 chit8 ki thiau7, chiu7-si7 chioh8-thiau7; ti7 hit teng2-bin7 koan3-tian7 to3-iu5.  15). Nga2-kok chiu7 chheng Siong7-te3 kap i kong2-oe7 e5 sou2-chai7, mia5 choe3 Pek-tek8-li7.  16). In tui3 Pek-tek8-li7 khi2-sin; li7-khui I2-hoat-tha iau2 u7 chit8 cham7 e5 lou7; Lah8-kiat tit-beh siN, lim5-san2 kan-lan5.  17). Tng i kan-khou2 siN e5 si5, khioh-chia2 tui3 i kong2, M7-bian2 kiaN, li2 taN beh koh tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 kiaN2.  18). I khui3 beh tng7, lim5-chiong e5 si5, chiu7 kio3 i e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5 Pian7-go5-ni5; i e5 lau7-pe7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 Pian7-nga2-bin2.  19). Lah8-kiat si2, bai5-chong3 ti7 khi3 I2-hoat-tha e5 lou7; I2-hoat-tha chiu7-si7 Pek-li7-heng5.  20). Nga2-kok khia7 thiau7 ti7 i e5 bong7-teng2; chit e5 thiau7 chiu7-si7 Lah8-kiat e5 bong7-pai5; kau3 kin-a2-jit8 iau2 ti7-teh.  21). I2-sek-liat8 koh khi2-sin khi3, ti7 I2-tek-tai5 tah pou3-piN5.  22). I2-sek-liat8 toa3 ti7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 si5, Liu5-pian7 khi3 kap i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 soe3-i5, Phek-lah8, saN-kap khun3; I2-sek-liat8 iah8 thiaN.
	23). Nga2-kok kiong7 u7 chap8-ji7 e5 kiaN2.  Li7-a e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Nga2-kok e5 toa7-kiaN2 Liu5-pian7, i2-kip8 Se-bian7, Li7-bi7, Iu5-tai7, I2-sat-ka, Se-pou3-lun5;  24). Lah8-kiat e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Iok-sek, Pian7-nga2-bin2;  25). Lah8-kiat e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 Tan3 kap Na2-hut-tha-li7;  26). Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-phaN3 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2 Ka-tek, A-siat; che si7 Nga2-kok ti7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2.  27). Nga2-kok lai5 kiN3 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat ti7 Ban7-li7, kau3 Ki-liat8-a-pa, chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lun5, A-pek-lah8-han2 kap I2-sat bat kia3-ku e5 sou2-chai7.
	28). I2-sat hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah poeh-chap8 he3;  29). I2-sat ni5-he3 lau7, jit8-chi2 moa2-chiok, khui3 tng7 lai5 si2, to3--khi3 i e5 liat8-chou2 hia; i nng7 e5 kiaN2 I2-so3, Nga2-kok, ka7 i bai5-chong3.

[36]	I2-so3 chiu7-si7 I2-tong, i e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  2). I2-so3 chhoa7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 cha-bou2-gin2-a2 choe3-bou2; chiu7-si7 Hek-lang5 I2-lun5 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 A-tai7, kap Hi-bi7 lang5 Che3-pian7 e5 cha-bou2-sun, A-na2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2.  3). Koh chhoa7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, Ni5-pai5-iok e5 chi2-be7, Pa-sit8-boat.  4). A-tai7 ka7 I2-so3 siN I2-li7-hoat; Pa-sit8-boat siN Liu5-jiN2;  5). A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 siN Ia5-ou-si, Nga2-lan5, Kho2-lah8; che long2 si7 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2, ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 siN--e5.  6). I2-so3 toa3 i e5 bou2, kiaN2, cha-bou2-kiaN2, kap ke-lai7 long2-chong2 e5 lang5, i2-kip8 gu5, iuN5, kap it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8, chiu7-si7 i ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5, khi3 pat8 sou2-chai7, li7-khui i e5 sio2-ti7 Nga2-kok.  7). In-ui7 nng7-lang5 sou2-u7--e5 chin-choe7, boe7 thang saN-kap khia7; koh in-ui7 in e5 gu5 iuN5 choe7, sou2 kia3-kha e5 sou2-chai7 boe7 iong5-un2--tit.  8). Tui3 an2-ni I2-so3 toa3 ti7 Se-jiN2 soaN.  I2-so3 chiu7-si7 I2-tong.
	9). I2-so3 e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2:  I2-so3 chiu7-si7 Se-jiN2 soaN I2-tong lang5 e5 chou2;  10). I2-so3 chiah e5 kiaN2 e5 mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2, I2-so3 e5 bou2 A-tai7 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-hoat, I2-so3 e5 bou2 Pa-sit8-boat e5 kiaN2 Liu5-jiN2.  11). I2-li7-hoat e5 kiaN2; The5-ban7, O-boat, Se2-pho, Ka-than2, Ki-lap8-su;  12). Teng5-lap8 si7 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2 I2-li7-hoat e5 soe3-i5, i ka7 I2-li7-hoat siN A-ma2-lek8; che si7 I2-so3 e5 bou2 A-tai7 e5 kiaN2-sun.  13). Liu5-jiN2 e5 kiaN2 si7 Na2-hap, Sia7-lah8, Sa-ma2, Bi2-sat; chiah-e5 si7 I2-so3 e5 bou2 Pa-sit8-boat e5 kiaN2-sun.  14). I2-so3 e5 bou2 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 si7 Che3-pian7 e5 cha-bou2-sun, A-na2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; i ka7 I2-so3 siN Ia5-ou-si, Nga2-lan5, Kho2-lah8.
	15). I2-so3 e5 kiaN2 sou2 siN choe3 chok8-tiuN2--e5, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; I2-so3 e5 toa7-kiaN2 I2-li7-hoat e5 kiaN2, u7 The5-ban7 chok8-tiuN2, O-boat chok8-tiuN2, Se2-pho chok8-tiuN2, Ki-lap8-su chok8-tiuN2,  16). Kho2-lah8 chok8-tiuN2, Ka-than2 chok8-tiuN2, A-ma2-lek8 chok8-tiuN2; chiah-e5 si7 ti7 I2-tong toe7, I2-li7-hoat sou2 siN e5 chok8-tiuN2, si7 A-tai7 e5 kiaN2-sun.  17). I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun Liu5-jiN2 e5 kiaN2, u7 Na2-hap chok8-tiuN2, Sia7-lah8 chok8-tiuN2, Sa-ma2 chok8-tiuN2, Bi2-sat chok8-tiuN2; che si7 ti7 I2-tong toe7, tui3 Liu5-jiN2 sou2 chhut e5 chok8-tiuN2, long2 si7 I2-so3 e5 bou2 Pa-sit8-boat e5 kiaN2-sun.  18). I2-so3 e5 bou2 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 e5 kiaN2, u7 Ia5-ou-si chok8-tiuN2, Nga2-lan5 chok8-tiuN2, Kho2-lah8 chok8-tiuN2; che si7 tui3 I2-so3 e5 bou2, A-na2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2, sou2 chhut e5 chok8-tiuN2.  19). Chiah-e5 si7 I2-so3 e5 kiaN2-sun, koh chiah-e5 si7 in e5 chok8-tiuN2; I2-so3 chiu7-si7 I2-tong.
	20). Hit sou2-chai7 e5 pun2-toe7 lang5, chiu7-si7 Ho5-li7 lang5 Se-jiN2 e5 kiaN2-sun, ki3 e7-toe2; chiu7-si7 Lo5-tan, Sok-pa, Che3-pian7, A-na2, Ti2-sun7, I2-chhat, Ti2-san;  21). chiah-e5 si7 tui3 I2-tong toe7 e5 Ho5-li7 lang5, Se-jiN2 kiaN2-sun-tiong sou2 chhut e5 chok8-tiuN2.  22). Lo5-tan e5 kiaN2 si7 Ho5-li7, Hi-ban7; Lo5-tan e5 chi2-be7 si7 Teng5-lap8.  23). Sok-pa e5 kiaN2 si7 A-lek8-bun5, Ma2-na2-hat, I2-pa-liok8, Si7-pho, O-lam5.  24). Che3-pian7 e5 kiaN2; A-nga2, A-na2; tng-si5 teh chhi7 in lau7-pe7 Che3-pian7 e5 lu5, ti7 khong3-ia2 chhe7-tioh8 un-choaN5--e5, chiu7-si7 chit e5 A-na2.  25). A-na2 e5 kiaN2 si7 Ti2-sun7; A-na2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 si7 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2.  26). Ti2-sun7 e5 kiaN2 si7 Him-tan3, I-si7-pan, Ek-lan5, Ki-lan5.  27). I2-chhat e5 kiaN2 si7 Phek-han2, Sat-hoan, A-kan.  28). Ti2-san e5 kiaN2 si7 OU-su, A-lan5.  29). Tui3 Ho5-li7 lang5 sou2 chhut e5 chok8-tiuN2, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; chiu7-si7 Lo5-tan chok8-tiuN2, Sok-pa chok8-tiuN2, Che3-pian7 chok8-tiuN2, A-na2 chok8-tiuN2,  30). Ti2-sun7 chok8-tiuN2, I2-chhat chok8-tiuN2, Ti2-san chok8-tiuN2.  Chiah-e5 si7 tui3 Ho5-li7 lang5 sou2 chhut e5 chok8-tiuN2, long2 ti7 Se-jiN2 toe7 choe3 chok8-tiuN2.
	31). Tng I2-sek-liat8 lang5 be7 u7 kun-ong5 ti7-li2 e5 tai7-seng, ti7 I2-tong toe7 choe3 ong5 lai5 ti7-li2--e5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  32). Pi2-jiN2 e5 kiaN2, Pi2-lah8, ti7 I2-tong choe3 ong5; i e5 kiaN-siaN5 mia5 kio3 Teng5-hap-pa.  33). Pi2-lah8 si2-liau2, Pho-su-lah8 lang5 Sia7-lah8 e5 kiaN2, Iok-pa, soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5.  34). Iok-pa si2, The5-ban7 toe7 e5 lang5 Hou7-san soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5.  35). Hou7-san si2, Pi2-tat8 e5 kiaN2, Hap-tat8, soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5; i chiu7-si7 ti7 Mou5-ap toe7 thai5-iaN5 Bi2-tian5 lang5--e5.  I e5 kiaN-siaN5 mia5 kio3 A-bi7-tek.  36). Hap-tat8 si2, Ma2-su7-li7-ka lang5 Song-lah8 soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5.  37). Song-lah8 si2-liau2, Ho5-piN e5 Li7-ho5-pek lang5 So3-lo5 soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5.  38). So3-lo5 si2, A-kek-pho e5 kiaN2, Pa-lek8-hap-lam5, soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5.  39). A-kek-pho e5 kiaN2 Pa-lek8-hap-lam5 si2, Hap-tat8 soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5; i e5 kiaN-siaN5 mia5-kio3 Pa-ou; i e5 bou2 mia5-kio3 Bi2-hi-tha-piat, si7 Bi2-sat-hap8 e5 cha-bou2-sun, Ma2-tek-liat8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2.
	40). Tui3 I2-so3 sou2 chhut e5 chok8-tiuN2, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8, sou2-chai7, mia5-ji7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; chiu7-si7 Teng5-lap8 chok8-tiuN2, A-lek8-oa2 chok8-tiuN2, Ia5-thiap chok8-tiuN2;  41). A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 chok8-tiuN2, I2-lah8 chok8-tiuN2, Pi2-lun3 chok8-tiuN2;  42). Ki-lap8-su chok8-tiuN2, The5-ban7 chok8-tiuN2, Bi2-pi2-sat chok8-tiuN2;  43). Ma2-ki-tiap8 chok8-tiuN2, I2-lan5 chok8-tiuN2; chiah-e5 si7 I2-tong e5 chok8-tiuN2, chiau3 in khia7-khi2 e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 sou2 tit-tioh8 choe3-giap8 e5 toe7.  Chit-e5 si7 I2-tong lang5 e5 chou2, chiu7-si7 I2-so3.

[37]	Nga2-kok khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 toe7, chiu7-si7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kia3-kha e5 sou2-chai7.  2). Nga2-kok e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Iok-sek chap8-chhit he3 kap i hiah e5 hiaN saN-kap kou3 iuN5; i si7 chit8 e5 gin2-a2 kap i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 soe3-i5 Phek-lah8 e5 kiaN2, Sek-phaN3 e5 kiaN2, siong5-siong5 choe3-tin7; Iok-sek chiong i hiah e5 hiaN e5 phaiN2 phin2-heng7 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2.  3). TaN I2-sek-liat8 thiaN3 Iok-sek khah iaN5-ke3 ti7 thiaN3 i e5 cheng3-kiaN2, in-ui7 Iok-sek si7 i ni5-lau7 siN--e5; i ka7 i choe3 chit8 nia2 chhai2-sek e5 saN.  4). Iok-sek hiah e5 hiaN khoaN3-kiN3 lau7-pe7 thiaN3 Iok-sek, ke3-thau5 ti7 thiaN3 in; chiu7 oan3-hun7 Iok-sek, boe7-oe7 kap i kong2 ho5-bok8 e5 oe7.
	5). Iok-sek bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 bang7, ka7 i hiah e5 hiaN kong2; in chiu7 koh-khah oan3-hun7 i.  6). Iok-sek tui3 in kong2, ChhiaN2 lin2 thiaN goa2 sou2 bang7-kiN3 e5 bang7.  7). Lan2 ti7 hng5--nih ha5 gou7-kak; goa2 sou2-ha5--e5 khi2-lai5 khia7, lin2 sou2-ha5--e5 ui5-lui5 lai5 pai3 goa2 sou2 ha5--e5.  8). I e5 hiaN in3 kong2, Chong2-bo5 li2 chin-chiaN3 beh choe3 goan2 e5 ong5 mah? chin-chiaN3 beh koan2-hat goan2 mah? In chiu7 ui7-tioh8 i e5 bang7, kap i e5 oe7, koh-khah oan3-hun7 i.  9). Au7-lai5 i koh bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 bang7, iah8 ka7 i e5 hiaN kong2, Li2 khoaN3, goa2 iu7-koh bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 bang7; u7 jit8, geh8, kap chap8-it liap8 chhiN teh pai3 goa2.  10). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kap i e5 hiaN kong2; in lau7-pe7 chiu7 chek-pi7 i, kong2, Li2 sou2 bang7-kiN3 chit e5 bang7 si7 chaiN2-iuN7? chong2-bo5 goa2 kap lin2 lau7-bu2 lin2 hiaN-ti7, long2 beh phak-teh pai3 li2 mah?  11). I e5 hiaN long2 oan3-tou3 i; i e5 lau7-pe7 eng7 chiah e5 oe7 ki3 ti7 sim-lai7.
	12). Iok-sek e5 hiaN khi3 Si7-kiam3, chhi7 lau7-pe7 e5 iuN5.  13). I2-sek-liat8 tui3 Iok-sek kong2, Lin2 hiaN kiam2 m7-si7 ti7 Si7-kiam3 chhi7 iuN5 mah? Li2 lai5, goa2 beh chhe li2 khi3 in hia.  14). I in3 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia.  I ka7 i kong2, Li2 khi3 khoaN3 lin2 hiaN u7 peng5-an a2-bo5, iuN5-kun5 u7 peng5-an a2-bo5; to3--lai5 ka7 goa2 kong2.  Chiu7 chhe i chhut Hi-pek-lun5 e5 soaN-kok; i chiu7 khi3 kau3 Si7-kiam3.  15). U7 lang5 tng7--tioh8 i ti7 soaN--nih be5-lou7; chiu7 mng7 i kong2, Li2 teh chhe7 sim2-mih8?  16). I kong2, Goa2 teh chhe7 goa2 e5 hiaN; chhiaN2 ka7 goa2 kong2, in ti7 tah-loh8 teh chhi7 iuN5.  17). Hit-lang5 kong2, In i2-keng li7-khui chia; in-ui7 goa2 thiaN-kiN3 in teh kong2, Lan2 lai5-khi3 To-tan.  Iok-sek chiu7 khi3 jip i e5 hiaN, tu2-tioh8 in ti7 To-tan.  18). In hng7-hng7 khoaN3-kiN3 i, i iau2-be7 kiaN5 kau3 in hia, in chiu7 saN-kap ke3-bou5 beh hai7-si2 i.  19). Tai7-ke saN-kap kong2, Li2 khoaN3, choe3-bang7--e5 lai5--lah.  20). Hou3--lai5, taN lan2 ka7 i thai5-si2, hiat ti7 chit8 e5 ta-chiN2; chiah lai5 kong2 u7 phaiN2-siu3 chiah8--i; lan2 chiah khoaN3 i e5 bang7 chiong-lai5 chaiN2-iuN7.  21). Liu5-pian7 thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 kiu3 i thoat-li7 in e5 chhiu2; kong2, Lan2 m7-thang hai7 i e5 siN3-mia7.  22). Liu5-pian7 koh tui3 in kong2, M7-thang hou7 i lau5-huih; thang ka7 i hiat ti7 chit e5 khong3-ia2 e5 ta-chiN2, m7-thang he7 chhiu2 hai7 i; i3-su3 si7 beh kiu3 i thoat-li7 in e5 chhiu2, hou7 i to3--khi3 i e5 lau7-pe7 hia.  23). Iok-sek kau3 i e5 hiaN hia, hit-tiap8 in chiu7 thng3 Iok-sek e5 goa7-saN, chiu7-si7 i seng-khu hit-nia2 chhai2-sek e5 saN;  24). chiu7 liah8 i, hiat-loh8 chiN2, hit e5 chiN2 si7 ta--e5, lai7-bin7 bo5 chui2.
	25). In che7-teh chiah8-piaN2; kiah8-bak8 khoaN3, khoaN3-kiN3 chit8-tin7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5 tui3 Ki-liat8 lai5; eng7 lok8-to5 pe7 hiuN-liau7, ju2-hiuN, but8-ioh8, beh toa3 loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8.  26). Iu5-tai7 tui3 chiah e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Lan2 thai5-si2 lan2 e5 sio2-ti7, khng3-bat8 i e5 huih, u7 sim2-mih8 li7-ek?  27). Lan2 lai5 ka7 i boe7 hou7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5; m7-thang he7-chhiu2 hai7 i; in-ui7 i si7 lan2 e5 sio2-ti7, lan2 e5 kut-jiok8.  HiaN-ti7 thiaN--i.  28). U7 hiah e5 Bi2-tian5 e5 seng-li2 lang5 tui3 hia ke3, i e5 hiaN chiu7 ka7 Iok-sek tui3 chiN2-lai7 puih8--khi2-lai5, chiong i boe7 hou7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5, tit-tioh8 ji7-chap8 e5 gun5.  Hiah e5 lang5 chiu7 toa3 Iok-sek khi3 Ai-kip8.  29). Liu5-pian7 to3-tng2--lai5 chiN2-piN, khoaN3-kiN3 Iok-sek bo5 ti7 chiN2-lai7, chiu7 thiah-lih8 ka-ki7 e5 saN.  30). To3--khi3 sio2-ti7 hia, kong2, Gin2-a2 bo5--khi3 lah; ia7 goa2 nih, goa2 beh tah-loh8 khi3?  31). In chiu7 thai5 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-kang2, chiong Iok-sek hit nia2 saN un3-huih;  32). chiu7 chhe lang5 theh8 hit nia2 chhai2-sek e5 saN khi3 in lau7-pe7 hia, kong2, Goan2 chhe7-tioh8 chit-nia2, chhiaN2 li2 jin7-khoaN3 si7 li2 e5 kiaN2 e5 goa7-saN a2 m7-si7.  33). I jin7-tit, chiu7 kong2, Che si7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 e5 goa7-saN, u7 phaiN2-siu3 ka7-chiah8--i; Iok-sek tek-khak hou7 i thiah-chhui3.  34). Nga2-kok chiu7 thiah-lih8 saN, io ha5 moa5-pou3, ui7 i e5 kiaN2 ai-siong choe7-choe7 jit8.  35). I e5 kiaN2 kap i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 long2 khi2-lai5 an-ui3 i; i m7-kheng2 siu7 an-ui3; kong2, Goa2 tek-khak ai-siong loh8 im-hu2, kau3 goa2 e5 kiaN2 hia.  I e5 lau7-pe7 ui7-tioh8 i thi5-khau3.  36). Bi2-tian5 lang5 toa3 Iok-sek kau3 Ai-kip8, chiong i boe7 hou7 Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5, si7-oe7-tiuN2, Pho-the5-hoat.

[38]	Hit-si5 Iu5-tai7 li7-khui i e5 hiaN-ti7, loh8--khi3 kau3 chit8 e5 A-tou7-lan5 lang5, mia5 choe3 Hi-lah8 e5 ke;  2). Iu5-tai7 ti7-hia khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 Ka-lam5 lang5, mia5-kio3 Su-a e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2; chiu7 chhoa7 i, kap i tang5-pang5.  3). I chiu7 hoai5-in7 siN-kiaN2; Iu5-tai7 chiu7 ka7 i ho7 mia5 choe3 JiN2.  4). I koh hoai5-in7 siN-kiaN2; lau7-bu2 ka7 i ho7 mia5 Go5-lam5.  5). I iu7-koh siN-kiaN2, ka7 i ho7-mia5 Si7-lah8; i siN Si7-lah8 e5 si5, Iu5-tai7 tu2-a2 ti7 Ki-sek.  6). Iu5-tai7 ka7 i e5 toa7-kiaN2 JiN2 chhoa7-bou2, mia5-kio3 Tha-ma2.  7). Iu5-tai7 e5 toa7-kiaN2 JiN2 kiaN5-phaiN2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 hou7 i si2.  8). Iu5-tai7 ka7 Go5-lam5 kong2, Li2 tioh8 kap li2 e5 hiaN-so2 tang5-pang5, tui3 i lai5 chin7 li2 choe3 sio2-ti7 e5 pun2-hun7, ka7 li2 e5 hiaN lip8 hou7-su5.  9). Go5-lam5 chai sou2 siN e5 kiaN2 bo5 kui ti7 i ka-ki7; sou2-i2 tang5-pang5 e5 si5, ui5-siat ti7 toe7--nih, bian2-tit hou7 i e5 hiaN u7 hou7-su5.  10). I e5 sou2-choe3, Ia5-ho5-hoa khoaN3 choe3 phaiN2; hou7 i ia7 si2.  11). Iu5-tai7 sim-lai7 kong2, KiaN-liau2 Si7-lah8 iah8 si2, chhin-chhiuN7 i nng7 e5 hiaN chit8-iuN7; chiu7 tui3 i e5 sim-pu7 Tha-ma2 kong2, Li2 khi3 toa3 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 ke chiu2-koaN2, theng3-hau7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lah8 tiong2-seng5.  Tha-ma2 chiu7 to3--khi3, toa3 ti7 in lau7-pe7 e5 ke.
	12). Ke3 ku2-ku2, Iu5-tai7 e5 bou2 Su-a e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 si2; Iu5-tai7 siu7 an-ui3; chiu7 kap i e5 peng5-iu2 A-tou7-lan5 lang5 Hi-lah8 chiuN7-khi3 Teng5-na2, kau3 i chian2 iuN5-mng5 e5 lang5 hia.  13). U7 lang5 ka7 Tha-ma2 kong2, Lin2 ta-koaN chiuN7-khi3 Teng5-na2, chian2 i e5 iuN5 e5 mng5.  14). Tha-ma2 khoaN3-kiN3 Si7-lah8 i2-keng tiong2-seng5, iau2 bo5 chhoa7 i choe3-bou2; chiu7 thng3 i chiu2-koaN2 e5 saN, eng7 phe3 ta3-bin7, koh moa sin-the2; che7 ti7 Teng5-na2 e5 lou7, I-na2-in3 mng5-khau2.  15). Iu5-tai7 khoaN3-kiN3 i, liah8-choe3 si7 chhiong-ki, in-ui7 i u7 ta3-bin7.  16). Chiu7 oat-khi3 lou7-piN chiu7-kun7 i; kong2, Lai5, hou7 goa2 kap li2 saN-kap khun3; in-ui7 m7-chai si7 i e5 sim-pu7; in3 kong2, Li2 beh kap goa2 khun3, beh eng7 sim2-mih8 hou7 goa2?  17). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goa2 tui3 iuN5-kun5-lai7 liah8 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-a2, kia3--lai5 hou7 li2.  Kong2, Li2 beh eng7 mih8 hou7 goa2 choe3 chun2-tng3, theng3-hau7 li2 kia3--lai5 mah?  18). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goa2 tioh8 sim2-mih8 hou7 li2 choe3 chun2-tng3? I chiu7 kong2, Li2 e5 in3, li2 e5 toa3, kap li2 chhiu2--nih e5 koaiN2-a2; chiu7 hou7 i, kap i khun3; i chiu7 tui3 Iu5-tai7 hoai5-in7.  19). Tha-ma2 khi2-lai5 khi3; thng3 i e5 phe3, iu5-goan5 chheng7 i chiu2-koaN2 e5 saN.  20). Iu5-tai7 thok i e5 peng5-iu2 A-tou7-lan5 lang5 sang3 chit8 chiah soaN-iuN5-a2, beh tui3 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 chhiu2 theh8 chun2-tng3; chhe7 i boe7 tioh8.  21). Chiu7 mng7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 lang5 kong2, I-na2-in3 lou7-piN e5 chhiong-ki ti7 tah-loh8? in kong2, chit-ui7 bo5 chhiong-ki.  22). I to3--khi3 kiN3 Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goa2 chhe7 i bo5; hit-ui7 e5 lang5 iah8 kong2, Chit-ui7 bo5 chhiong-ki.  23). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Ku3-chai7 i theh8-khi3, bian2-tit lan2 kian3-siau3; li2 khoaN3, goa2 i2-keng chiong chit chiah soaN-iuN5-a2 sang3 i, li2 keng2-jian5 chhe7 i bo5.  24). Iok-liok8 ke3 saN-geh8-jit8, u7 lang5 ka7 Iu5-tai7 kong2, Li2 e5 sim-pu7 Tha-ma2 choe3 chhiong-ki; koh in-ui7 kiaN5-im5, soa3 u7 sin-in7.  Iu5-tai7 kong2, Ka7 i thoa--chhut-lai5 sio.  25). Tha-ma2 hou7 lang5 thoa--chhut-lai5 e5 si5, chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 kiN3 i e5 ta-koaN kong2, Chiah e5 mih8 si7 chi7-chui7 e5, goa2 chiu7-si7 tui3 i lai5 hoai5-in7.  26). Koh kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 jin7, khoaN3 chit e5 in3 kap toa3 kap koaiN2-a2 si7 chi7-chui7 e5.  Iu5-tai7 jin7-tit, chiu7 kong2, I pi2 goa2 khah u7-gi7; in-ui7 goa2 bo5 chiong i ke3 hou7 goa2 e5 kiaN2 Si7-lah8; tui3 hit-tiap8 Iu5-tai7 bo5 koh chhin-kun7 i.  27). Tha-ma2 tit-beh siN e5 si5, chai i pak-tou2-lai7 si7 siang-e5.  28). Teh siN e5 si5, chit8 e5 gin2-a2 chhun chit8 ki chhiu2 chhut-lai5; khioh-chia2 theh8 ang5-soaN3 pak8 ti7 i e5 chhiu2 kong2, Chit-e5 si7 tai7-seng chhut-e5.  29). Au7-lai5 i e5 chhiu2 kiu--jip8-khi3; te7-ji7--e5 chhut-si3; khioh-chia2 kong2, Li2 siaN2-su7 chong5--chhut-lai5? chit e5 piak-phoa3 si7 ui7-tioh8 li2; sou2-i2 ka7 i ho7-mia5 choe3 Hoat-lek8-su.  30). Au7-lai5 hit-e5, chhiu2 pak8 ang5-soaN3--e5, iah8 siN--chhut-lai5; chiu7 ho7 i e5 mia5 choe3 Sia7-lah8.

[39]	Iok-sek hou7 lang5 toa3 loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8; u7 chit8 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5, si7 Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5 si7-oe7-tiuN2 Pho-the5-hoat, tui3 hiah-e5 toa3 i lai5 e5 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 boe2--khi3.  2). Ia5-ho5-hoa kap i saN-kap ti7-teh, hou7 i tak8-hang7 heng-thong; toa3 ti7 i e5 chu2-lang5 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 ke.  3). I e5 chu2-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap i saN-kap ti7-teh; koh Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 i e5 chhiu2 sou2 choe3--e5 long2 heng-thong.  4). Iok-sek chiu7 ti7 chu2-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, lai5 hok8-sai7 i; chu2-lang5 siat-lip8 i koan2-li2 i e5 ke, chiong it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 kau i e5 chhiu2.  5). Tui3 chu2-lang5 siat-lip8 i koan2-li2 ke-su7, kap i it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 Iok-sek e5 ian5-kou3, su3-hok ti7 hit e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 ke; kiN3-na7 ke-lai7 kap chhan5--nih it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, long2 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok.  6). I chiong it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, long2 kau Iok-sek e5 chhiu2; tu5-khi3 i sou2 chiah8 e5 mih8 i2-goa7, pat8-hang7 sou2-u7--e5, long2 m7-chai.  Iok-sek sui2 koh ho2-siN-choe3.
