	7). Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7, Iok-sek e5 chu2-bu2 chu3-sin5 khoaN3--i, kong2, Lai5 kap goa2 khun3.  8). Iok-sek m7-than3, tui3 i e5 chu2-bu2 kong2, Li2 khoaN3, ke-lai7 u7 sim2-mih8 ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2, goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 long2 m7-chai; i i2-keng chiong sou2-u7--e5 kau ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2; ti7 chi2 ke-lai7 bo5 chit8-e5 pi2 goa2 khah-toa7;  9). li2 i2-goa7, i bo5 chit8-hang7 bo5 kau goa2, in-ui7 li2 si7 i e5 bou2; goa2 chaiN2-iuN7 thang kiaN5 chit e5 toa7-phaiN2, lai5 tek-choe7 Siong7-te3?  10). Au7-lai5 i tak8-jit8 kap Iok-sek kong2-oe7; Iok-sek bo5 thiaN i e5 oe7; bo5 kap i khun3, iah8 bo5 kap i choe3-tui.  11). U7 chit8-jit8, Iok-sek jip8 chhu3 pan7 i e5 tai7-chi3; ke-lai7 e5 lang5 bo5 chit8-e5 ti7 chhu3-lai7.  12). Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 khiu2 i e5 saN kong2, Li2 lai5 kap goa2 khun3; Iok-sek chiong saN pang3 ti7 i e5 chhiu2, chau2 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7.  13). Hu7-jin5-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 Iok-sek chiong saN pang3 ti7 i chhiu2--nih, koh chau2-chhut goa7-bin7;  14). chiu7 kio3 ke-lai7 e5 lang5 lai5, tui3 in kong2, Lin2 khoaN3--teh, i toa3 chit8 e5 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 jip8-lai5 lan2 e5 ke beh hi3-lang7 lan2; i lai5 goa2 chia, beh kap goa2 khun3, goa2 chiu7 toa7-siaN hoah;  15). i thiaN-kiN3 goa2 chhut-siaN hoah, chiu7 chiong i e5 saN pang3 ti7 goa2 chia, chau2-chhut goa7-bin7.  16). Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiong Iok-sek e5 saN siu ti7 i hia, theng3-hau7 i e5 chu2-lang5 to3--lai5.  17). Chiu7 tui3 i kong2-khi2 chiah e5 su7; kong2, Li2 sou2 toa3-lai5 lan2 chia, hit e5 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 lou5-pok8, kau3 goa2 chia, beh hi3-lang7 goa2;  18). goa2 chhut-siaN hoah, i chiong i e5 saN pang3 ti7 goa2 chia, chau2-chhut goa7-bin7.  19). Chu2-lang5 thiaN-kiN3 i e5 bou2 tui3 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goa2, i chiu7 siu7-khi3.  20). Iok-sek e5 chu2-lang5 chiong i koaiN-loh8 kaN, chiu7-si7 ong5 e5 choe7-hoan7 siu7 koaiN e5 sou2-chai7; tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek ti7 hit e5 kaN-lai7.
	21). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap Iok-sek ti7-teh, si-un hou7 i; hou7 i ti7 koan2-kaN e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2.  22). Koan2-kaN--e5 chiu7 chiong kaN-lai7 sou2 u7 e5 hoan7-lang5 long2 kau Iok-sek e5 chhiu2; in ti7-hia sou2 choe3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 si7 i teh choe3.  23). KiN3-na7 Iok-sek chhiu2-e7 e5 tai7-chi3, koan2-kaN--e5 it-khai3 bo5 chhap; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap Iok-sek ti7-teh, koh i sou2 choe3--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa long2 hou7 i heng-thong.

[40]	Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7, Ai-kip8 ong5 e5 chiu2-cheng3 kap tu5-pang5 tek-choe7 in e5 chu2 Ai-kip8 ong5.  2). Hoat-lo2 siu7-khi3 i nng7 e5 jin5-sin5, chiu7-si7 chiu2-cheng3-tiuN2 kap tu5-pang5-tiuN2,  3). chiong in koaiN ti7 si7-oe7-tiuN2 hu2-lai7 e5 kaN, chiu7-si7 Iok-sek siu7 koaiN e5 sou2-chai7.  4).  Si7 -oe7-tiuN2 chiong in kau-tai3 Iok-sek, i chiu7 su-hau7 in; in chiu7 ti7 kaN-lai7 u7 hiah-ku2.  5). Siu7-koaiN ti7 kaN--e5, Ai-kip8 ong5 e5 chiu2-cheng3 kap tu5-pang5, nng7-lang5 tang5 chit8-mi5 kok bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 bang7, long2 chiau3 tak8 e5 bang7 e5 i3-gi7 lai5 bang7.  6). Kau3 thiN-kng, Iok-sek jip8--khi3 in hia, khoaN3-kiN3 in u7 iu-bun7 e5 khoan2-sit.  7). I chiu7 mng7 Hoat-lo2 nng7 e5 jin5-sin5, chiu7-si7 kap i piN5-piN5 koaiN ti7 chu2-lang5 hu2-lai7--e5, kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 lin2 siaN2-su7 bin7 tai3-iu-iong5?  8). In ka7 i kong2, Goan2 tak8-lang5 bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 bang7, bo5 lang5 thang oan5.  Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, Oan5-bang7 kiam2-m7-si7 chai7 ti7 Siong7-te3 mah? chhiaN2 lin2 ka7 goa2 kong2.  9). Chiu2-cheng3 chiu7 tui3 Iok-sek pai5-liat8 i e5 bang7, kong2, Goa2 bang7-tiong khoaN3-kiN3 u7 chit8 chang5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5;  10). chhiu7-teng2 u7 saN-ki, chhin-chhiuN7 u7 hoat-ge5 khui-hoe; i e5 pha kiat-chiaN5 sek8 e5 phu5-to5.  11). Hoat-lo2 e5 poe ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2-lai7, goa2 chiu7 theh8 phu5-to5, nih8 i ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 poe-lai7, chiong poe phang5 kau Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2.  12). Iok-sek ka7 i kong2, Li2 e5 bang7 si7 an2-ni oan5; saN-ki chiu7-si7 saN-jit8;  13). koh saN-jit8, Hoat-lo2 beh ku2-khi2 li2 e5 thau5, hok8-to3 li2 e5 koaN-chit; Hoat-lo2 e5 chiu2-poe beh iu5-goan5 he7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 choe3 i e5 chiu2-cheng3 chit8-iuN7.  14). Li2 na7 tek-chi3 e5 si5, tioh8 ki3-liam7 goa2, si-un hou7 goa2; ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 thoe3 goa2 kong2 chit8 siaN; kiu3 goa2 chhut chit e5 kaN.  15). Goa2 sit8-chai7 si7 tui3 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 toe7 siu7-boe7--lai5-e5; goa2 ti7-chia iah8 bo5 choe3-chhut sim2-mih8, hou7 in ka7 goa2 koaiN-loh8 kaN.  16). Tu5-pang5 khoaN3-kiN3 bang7 oan5-liau2 ho2, chiu7 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 iah8 ti7 goa2 e5 bang7-tiong khoaN3, ti7 goa2 e5 thau5-khak-teng2 u7 saN-kheng pek e5 piaN2;  17). teng2-bin7 hit-kheng u7 toe2 Hoat-lo2 sou2 chiah8 tak8-ho7 pek e5 mih8; u7 chiau2 lai5 teh goa2 thau5-khak-teng2 kheng-lai7 e5 mih8.  18). Iok-sek in3 i kong2, Li2 e5 bang7 si7 an2-ni oan5; saN khia kheng si7 saN-jit8;  19). koh saN-jit8, Hoat-lo2 beh ku2-khi2 li2 e5 thau5-khak li7-khui li2, tiau3 li2 ti7 chha5--nih; beh u7 pe-chiau2 lai5 teh li2 sin-khu e5 bah.  20). Kau3 te7-saN jit8, si7 Hoat-lo2 e5 siN-jit8, i ui7 cheng3 jin5-sin5 pai5-siat ian5-siah8; ti7 chiah e5 jin5-sin5 e5 tiong-kan, thai-ku2 chiu2-cheng3 kap tu5-pang5;  21). hou7 chiu2-cheng3-tiuN2 hok8-to3 koaN-chit; i iu5-goan5 phang5-poe ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2;  22). chong2-si7 chiong tu5-pang5-thau5 tiau3--khi2-lai5; tu2-tu2 chiau3 Iok-sek sou2 ka7 in oan5--e5.  23). Na7-si7 chiu2-cheng3-tiuN2 bo5 liam7-tioh8 Iok-sek, keng2-jian5 boe7-ki3-tit i.

[41]	 Ke3 nng7-ni5 ka-nng5, Hoat-lo2 bin5-bang7; bang7-kiN3 i khia7 ti7 ho5-piN,  2). khoaN3-kiN3 chhit chiah gu5-bu2 tui3 ho5--nih khi2-lai5, sui2 koh pui5; ti7 lou5-tek-a2-lai7 teh chiah8.  3). Te3-au7 koh u7 chhit chiah gu5-bu2 tui3 ho5--nih khi2--lai5, khiap-si3 koh san2; kap cheng5 hiah e5 gu5 tang5-khia7 ti7 ho5-piN.  4). Chiah e5 khiap-si3 koh san2 e5 gu5-bu2 it-chin7 chiah8 hi2 chhit-chiah sui2 koh pui5 e5 gu5.  Hoat-lo2 chiu7 chhiN2.  5). I koh khun3, te7-ji7 pai2 bin5-bang7; bang7-kiN3 chit8 chang5 beh8 chhut chhit-sui7, phauh koh ho2.  6). Au7-lai5 khoaN3-kiN3 koh chhut chhit-sui7, phaN3-phaN3, koh hou7 tang-hong sau3-phaiN2.  7). Chiah e5 phaN3 e5 sui7 thun hi2 chhit-sui7 phauh koh pa2-moa2--e5.  Hoat-lo2 chhiN2, chiah chai si7 bang7--kiN3.  8). Kau3 thiN-kng, Hoat-lo2 sim bo5 peng5-an; chiu7 chhe lang5 tiau3 Ai-kip8 sou2 u7 e5 sut8-su7, phok-su7 lai5; Hoat-lo2 chiu7 chiong i sou2 bang7-kiN3--e5 ka7 in kong2; in bo5 lang5 oe7 ka7 Hoat-lo2 oan5.
	9). Hit-si5 chiu2-cheng3-tiuN2 ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 ki3-tit goa2 e5 choe7.  10). Cheng5 Hoat-lo2 siu7-khi3 jin5-sin5, chiong goa2 kap tu5-pang5-thau5 koaiN ti7 si7-oe7-tiuN2 hu2-lai7 e5 kaN.  11). Goa2 kap i, nng7-lang5 siang5 hit-mi5 u7 bang7-kiN3, kok chiau3 i e5 bang7 e5 i3-gi7 lai5 bang7.  12). Ti7-hia, kap goan2 ti7-teh, u7 chit8 e5 Hi-pek-lai5 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, si7 si7-oe7-tiuN2 e5 lou5-pok8, goan2 ka7 i kong2, i chiu7 ka7 goan2 oan5 goan2 e5 bang7; si7 chiau3 goan2 tak8-lang5 e5 bang7 lai5 oan5.  13). Au7-lai7 tu2-tu2 chiau3 i sou2 ka7 goan2 oan5--e5 lai5 chiaN5; i hou7 goa2 hok8-chit, hit-lang5 siu7 tiau3 lai5 si2.
	14). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 tiau3 Iok-sek, in chiu7 kin2-kin2 chhoa7 i chhut-kaN; i chiu7 chian2-hoat, oaN7 i e5 saN, lai5 kiN3 Hoat-lo2.  15). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 bang7-kiN3 chit8 e5 bang7, bo5 lang5 oe7 oan5--i; goa2 thiaN-kiN3 lang5 kong2 kau3 li2 thiaN-kiN3 bang7 chiu7 oe7 oan5.  16). Iok-sek in3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Che m7-si7 chai7-ti7 goa2; Siong7-te3 beh chiong peng5-an chi2-si7 Hoat-lo2.  17). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 bang7-kiN3 goa2 khia7 ti7 ho5-piN,  18). u7 chhit chiah gu5-bu2 tui3 ho5--nih khi2--lai5, pui5 koh sui2; ti7 lou5-tek-a2-lai7 teh chiah8;  19). te3-au7 koh u7 chhit chiah gu5-bu2 khi2--lai5, nng7-chiaN2, chin khiap-si3, koh chin san2; pian3 Ai-kip8 toe7, goa2 m7-bat khoaN3-kiN3 kau3 chiah phaiN2.  20). Chiah e5 san2 koh khiap-si3 e5 gu5-bu2 it-chin7 chiah8 tai7-seng hi2 chhit chiah pui5 e5 gu5-bu2;  21). thun loh8 pak, iau2-boe7 khoaN3-chhut u7 thun--loh8 khi3; hit e5 khiap-si3 e5 khoan2 iu5-goan5 kap tai7-seng bo5 koh-iuN7; goa2 chiu7 chhiN2.  22). Goa2 ti7 bang7-tiong koh khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 chang5 beh8, chhut chhit-sui7, pa2-moa2 koh ho2;  23). au7-lai5 koh chhut chhit-sui7, kou-ta5, phaN3-phaN3, koh hou7 tang-hong sau3-phaiN2;  24). chiah e5 phaN3-phaN3 e5 sui7 thun hi2 chhit sui7 ho2--e5.  Goa2 kong2 hou7 sut8-su7 thiaN, ia7 bo5 lang5 oe7 ka7 goa2 koe2-beng5.
	25). Iok-sek ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Hoat-lo2 e5 bang7 chiu7-si7 chit8-e5; Siong7-te3 sou2 beh kiaN5 e5 su7, u7 chi2-si7 Hoat-lo2.  26). Chhit-chiah ho2 e5 gu5-bu2 si7 chhit-ni5; chhit-sui7 ho2--e5, iah8 si7 chhit-ni5; bang7 si7 chit8-e5.  27). Hiah e5 te3-au7 khi2--lai5 e5 chhit chiah san2 koh khiap-si3 e5 gu5-bu2, si7 chhit-ni5; hiah e5 chhit sui7 khang-phaN3, koh hou7 tang-hong sau3-phaiN2--e5, iah8 si7 chhit ni5; beh choe3 chhit ni5 e5 ki-hng.  28). Siong7-te3 sou2 beh choe3 e5 su7, u7 hian2-beng5 ti7 Hoat-lo2; che si7 goa2 tui3 Hoat-lo2 sou2 kong2--e5.  29). Li2 khoaN3, Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 beh tu2-tioh8 toa7 ho2-ni5-tang chhit-ni5;  30). te3-au7, koh beh tu2-tioh8 ki-hng chhit-ni5; sim7-chi3 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 long2 boe7 ki3-tit i2-cheng5 e5 ho2-siu; choan5-toe7 beh hou7 ki-hng sou2 biat8;  31). in-ui7 i2-au7 e5 ki-hng thai3 siong-tiong7, chiu7 m7-chai i2-cheng5 toe7-hng e5 ho2-siu.  32). Lun7-kau3 Hoat-lo2 nng7 pai2 e5 bin5-bang7, si7 in-ui7 Siong7-te3 chu3-tiaN7 chit e5 tai7-chi3, koh Siong7-te3 beh kin2-kin2 chiaN5-i.  33). Sou2-i2 Hoat-lo2 tioh8 keng2 chit8 e5 u7 chhang-mia5, u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, phai3 i ti7-li2 Ai-kip8 toe7.  34). Hoat-lo2 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5, koh lip8 koaN-oan5 koan2-li2 chit e5 toe7; tng chhit-ni5 ho2-ni5-tang e5 si5, Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2-siu--e5, gou7-hun7 thiu chit8-hun7;  35). hou7 in ti7 chiong-lai5 e5 ho2-ni5-tang, chek-chu7 it-chhe3 e5 bi2-niu5; chu7-chip8 ngou2-kok, siu-khng3 chiau3-kou3; ti7 tak8 e5 siaN5 choe3 chiah8-mih8, kui ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2-thau5.  36). Sou2 chek-chu7 e5 bi2-niu5, thang choe3 Ai-kip8 toe7 chiong-lai5 chhit-ni5 ki-hng e5 lou7-eng7; bian2-tit chit e5 toe7 hou7 ki-hng sou2 biat8.
	37). Hoat-lo2 kap i it-chhe3 e5 jin5-sin5 long2 liah8 chit e5 tai7-chi3 choe3-ho2.  38). Hoat-lo2 tui3 i e5 jin5-sin5 kong2, Lan2 kiam2 oe7 chhe7-tioh8 chit8-e5 chhin-chhiuN7 i chit e5 lang5, u7 Siong7-te3 e5 sin5 ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7 mah?  39). Hoat-lo2 tui3 Iok-sek kong2, Siong7-te3 i2-keng chiong chit e5 tai7-chi3 long2 chi2-si7 li2, kho2-kian3 bo5 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 li2 u7 chit-ho7 e5 chhang-mia5 ti3-hui7.  40). Li2 thang koan2-li2 goa2 e5 ke; goa2 e5 peh-siN3 long2 tioh8 thiaN li2 e5 oe7, hou7 li2 koan2-li2; tok8-tok8 ti7 po2-cho7, goa2 pi2 li2 khah toa7.  41). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 ku2-khi2 li2 koan2-hat Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7.  42). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 pak i chhiu2--nih choe3 in3 e5 chhiu2-chi2, koa3 ti7 Iok-sek e5 chng2-thau5-a2; ka7 i chheng7 iu3-toe7-saN; chiong kim-lian7 koa3 ti7 i e5 am7-kun2.  43). Koh hou7 Iok-sek che7 i e5 te7-ji7 pan7 chhia; khui-to7--e5 kio3 kong2, Kui7; an2-ni Hoat-lo2 siat-lip8 i ti7-li2 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7.  44). Hoat-lo2 tui3 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 si7 Hoat-lo2, na7 bo5 li2 u7 siaN, ti7 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7, m7-chun2 lang5 tang7 kha-chhiu2.  45). Hoat-lo2 khim-su3 Iok-sek e5 mia5 kio3 Sat-hoat-na2-thek Pa-loe7-a; koh chiong An-siaN5 e5 che3-si Pho-the5-hui-lah8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 A-se-lap8 hou7 i choe3-bou2.  Iok-sek chiu7 chhut-sun5 Ai-kip8 toe7.
	46). Iok-sek kiN3 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 e5 si5, hit-ni5 saN-chap8 he3.  Iok-sek tui3 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-khi3, pian3 kiaN5 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7.  47). Chhit-e5 ho2 ni5-tang e5 lai7-bin7, toe7 e5 chhut-san2 kek8-ki5 hong-seng7.  48). Iok-sek chu7-chip8 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhit e5 ho2 ni5-tang it-chhe3 e5 bi2-niu5; chiong bi2-niu5 chek-chu7 ti7 tak8 e5 siaN5; chiu-ui5 chhan5-toe7 e5 bi2-niu5, long2 chek-chu7 ti7 i e5 pun2-siaN5.  49). Iok-sek chek-chu7 gou7-kak kek8-choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-piN e5 soa, kau3 i theng5-chi2 bo5 sng3; in-ui7 sng3-boe7-liau2.  50). Ki-hng e5 ni5 be7-kau3 i2-cheng5, An-siaN5 e5 che3-si Pho-the5-hui-lah8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 A-se-lap8 ka7 Iok-sek siN nng7 e5 kiaN2.  51). Iok-sek ka7 toa7 kiaN2 ho7 mia5 kio3 Ma2-na2-se; in-ui7 i kong2, Siong7-te3 hou7 goa2 boe7-ki3-tit goa2 it-chhe3 e5 khun3-khou2, kap goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 choan5-ke.  52). I ka7 te7-ji7 kiaN2 ho7 mia5 I2-hoat-lian5; in-ui7 i kong2, Siong7-te3 hou7 goa2 ti7 goa2 siu7-khou2 e5 toe7-hng heng-ong7.  53). Ai-kip8 toe7 chhit-ni5 ho2 ni5-tang i2-keng oan5,  54). chhit-ni5 ki-hng chiu7 lai5, tu2-tu2 chiau3 Iok-sek sou2 kong2--e5; tak8-kok long2 u7 ki-hng; tok8-tok8 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 u7 bi2-niu5.
	55). Kau3 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 u7 ki-hng, cheng3 peh-siN3 tui3 Hoat-lo2 ai-kiu5 bi2-niu5; Hoat-lo2 tui3 Ai-kip8 e5 cheng3-lang5 kong2, Lin2 khi3 chhe7 Iok-sek, hoan7-na7 i sou2 kong2--e5, lin2 long2 tioh8 choe3.  56). Tng-si5 ki-hng pian3-moa2 thiN-e7; Iok-sek khui tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 chhek-chhng, thio3 bi2-niu5 hou7 Ai-kip8 lang5; ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ki-hng chin siong-tiong7.  57). Tak8-kok e5 lang5 long2 khi3 Ai-kip8, kau3 Iok-sek hia tiah8 bi2-niu5; in-ui7 thiN-e7 ki-hng chin siong-tiong7.

[42]	Nga2-kok khoaN3-kiN3 Ai-kip8 u7 gou7-kak, Nga2-kok chiu7 ka7 i hiah e5 kiaN2 kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 teh saN-khoaN3.  2). Koh kong2, Goa2 thiaN-kiN3 Ai-kip8 u7 gou7-kak, lin2 thang loh8-khi3 hia, ui7 lan2 tiah8 tam7-poh8, hou7 lan2 thang tou7-oah8, bian2 si2.  3). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek chap8 e5 hiaN long2 loh8 Ai-kip8, khi3 tiah8 bi2-niu5.  4). Chong2-si7 Iok-sek e5 sio2-ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2, Nga2-kok bo5 chhe i kap in hiaN saN-kap khi3; in-ui7 i kong2, KiaN-liau2 i tu2-tioh8 hai7.  5). Lai5 tiah8 bi2-niu5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, I2-sek-liat8 hiah e5 kiaN2 iah8 u7 lai5, in-ui7 Ka-lam5 toe7 iah8 u7 ki-hng.  6). Tng-si5 ti7-li2 Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 si7 Iok-sek; thio3 bi2-niu5 hou7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3--e5, iah8 si7 i; Iok-sek hiah e5 hiaN lai5, phak-loh8 toe7 pai3 i.  7).  Iok-sek khoaN3-kiN3 i hiah e5 hiaN, oe7 jin7--tit, ke2-choe3 siN-hun7-lang5, tui3 in kong2 khah-giam5 e5 oe7, mng7 in kong2, Lin2 tui3 tah-loh8 lai5? in kong2, Tui3 Ka-lam5 toe7 lai5 tiah8 bi2-niu5.  8). Iok-sek oe7 jin7-tit in hiaN, in boe7 jin7--tit i.  9). Iok-sek ki3-tit cheng5 sou2 bang7 lun7-kau3 in-e5 hiah e5 bang7, chiu7 tui3 in kong2, Lin2 si7 cheng-tham3, lai5 tham3-thiaN chit sou2-chai7 e5 hu-sit8.  10). In tui3 i kong2, Goan2 e5 chu2 ah, m7-si7, li2 e5 lou5-pok8 lai5 beh tiah8 bi2-niu5.  11). Goan2 long2 si7 chit8-lang5 e5 kiaN2, goan2 si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, li2 e5 lou5-pok8 m7-si7 cheng-tham3.  12). Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, M7-si7 an2-ni, lin2 lai5 si7 beh tham3-thiaN chit sou2-chai7 e5 hu-sit8.  13). In kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 chap8-ji7 e5 hiaN-ti7, si7 Ka-lam5 toe7 chit8 e5 lang5 e5 kiaN2; te7-it-soe3--e5, hian7-kim ti7 goan2 lau7-pe7 hia; u7 chit8-e5 bo5--khi3 lah.  14). Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, Goa2 tu2-a2 kong2 lin2 si7 cheng-tham3, chit e5 oe7 sit8-chai7 bo5 chho3.  15). Goa2 ki2 Hoat-lo2 e5 siN3-mia7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, na7 lin2 soah-be2 e5 sio2-ti7 bo5 kau3 chia, lin2 boe7-tit-thang chhut chit sou2-chai7; eng7 an2-ni lai5 chhi3-giam7 lin2 e5 hu-sit8.  16). Tioh8 chhe lin2 tiong-kan chit8-lang5 khi3 chhoa7 lin2 e5 sio2-ti7 lai5, lin2 chiah-e5 long2 tioh8 koaiN ti7-chia, cheng3-beng5 lin2 e5 oe7, chai lin2 seng5-sit8 a2-bo5; na7 bo5, goa2 ki2 Hoat-lo2 e5 siN3-mia7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, lin2 it-teng7 si7 cheng-tham3.  17). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek chiong in long2 koaiN ti7 KaN--nih saN-jit8.
	18). Kau3 te7-saN jit8 Iok-sek tui3 in kong2, Goa2 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3; lin2 chiau3 goa2 e5 oe7 kiaN5, chiu7 oe7 oah8.  19). Lin2 na7 ko2-jian5 si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, lin2 hiaN-ti7-tiong thang lau5 chit8-e5 pak8 ti7 lin2 hi2 kaN-lai7; chong2-si7 lin2 thang toa3 bi2-niu5 to3--khi3, kiu3 lin2 ke-lai7 e5 ki-hng,  20). chiong lin2 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 chhoa7 lai5 goa2 chia; an2-ni lin2 e5 oe7 chiu7 u7 pin5-ku3, lin2 ia7 m7-bian2 si2.  In chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kiaN5.  21). In saN-kap kong2, Lan2 tui3 ti7 lan2 e5 sio2-ti7 sit8-chai7 u7 choe7, i ai-kiu5 lan2 e5 si5, lan2 khoaN3-kiN3 i sim-lai7 e5 kan-khou2, ia7 m7-kheng2 thiaN i; sou2-i2 chit-tiuN5 e5 khou2-lan7 kau3 ti7 lan2.  22). Liu5-pian7 in3 in kong2, Goa2 kiam2 m7-si7 tui3 lin2 kong2, m7-thang hai7 hit e5 gin2-a2 lai5 chhu2-choe7, tok8-tok8 lin2 m7-thiaN? sou2-i2 lau5 i e5 huih e5 choe7, tui3 lan2 chiah-e5 tho2.  23). In m7-chai Iok-sek thiaN oe7 hiau2--tit; in-ui7 ti7 in tiong-kan u7 eng7 hoan-ek8-koaN.  24). Iok-sek oat8-tng2-sin lau5 bak8-sai2; koh oat8-lai5 kap in kong2-oe7; chiu7 ti7 in tiong-kan chhu2 Se-bian7 chhut--lai5, ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 i pak8--teh.  25). Iok-sek hoan-hu3 lang5 chiong gou7-kak jip8 ti7 in e5 khi3-ku7 kau3 moa2-moa2, ia7 chiong in tak8-lang5 e5 gun5 he7 ti7 in e5 pou3-te7-lai7, lai5 heng5 in, koh eng7 lou7--nih e5 chiah8-mih8 hou7 in; lang5 chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 ka7 in choe3.
	26). In chiu7 chiong gou7-kak hou7 in e5 lu5 chai3, chiu7 li7-khui hia khi3.  27). Kau3 hioh-mi5 e5 sou2-chai7, in tiong-kan u7 chit8-lang5 thau2-khui i e5 pou3-te7, beh theh8 hou7 lu5 chiah8, chiah khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 gun5 iu5-goan5 ti7--teh, he7 ti7 pou3-te7-khau2.  28). Chiu7 ka7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Goa2 e5 gun5 heng5 to3-tng2, li2 khoaN3, iu5-goan5 ti7 goa2 e5 pou3-te7-lai7; in chiu7 kiaN kau3 bo5 sim-koaN, ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, saN-kap kong2, Siong7-te3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 lan2 si7 sim2-mih8?  29). In kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7, kau3 in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok hia, chiong sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7 long2 ka7 i kong2, kong2, Hit-lang5, chiu7-si7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 chu2, tui3 goan2 kong2 chin giam5 e5 oe7, liah8 goan2 choe3 hit sou2-chai7 e5 cheng-tham3.  31). Goan2 ka7 i kong2, Goan2 si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, goan2 m7-si7 cheng-tham3,  32). goan2 si7 chap8-ji7 e5 hiaN-ti7, si7 goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 kiaN2; u7 chit8-e5 bo5--khi3, te7-it-soe3-e5 hian7-kim kap goan2 lau7-pe7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7.  33). Hit-lang5, chiu7-si7 hit sou2-chai7 e5 chu2, ka7 goan2 kong2, Na7 ai3 ho7 goa2 chai lin2 si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, lin2 hiaN-ti7-tiong thang lau5 chit8-e5 ti7 goa2 chia, lin2 chiah-e5 thang toa3 gou7-kak to3--khi3, kiu3 lin2 ke-lai7 e5 ki-hng;  34). chhoa7 lin2 soah-be2 e5 sio2-ti7 lai5 goa2 chia, goa2 chiu7 chai lin2 m7-si7 cheng-tham3, si7 lau2-sit8 lang5; an2-ni goa2 chiu7 chiong lin2 e5 hiaN-ti7 kau hou7 lin2, lin2 ia7 thang ti7 chit sou2-chai7 boe2-boe7.
	35). Au7-lai5 in piaN3 in e5 pou3-te7, bo5 phah-sng3, in tak8-lang5 e5 gun5-pau long2 ti7 in e5 pou3-te7-lai7; in kap in lau7-pe7 khoaN3-kiN3 gun5-pau chiu7 long2 kiaN-hiaN5.  36). In e5 lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok ka7 in kong2, Lin2 hou7 goa2 sit-loh8 goa2 e5 kiaN2; Iok-sek bo5--khi3, Se-bian7 ia7 bo5--khi3, lin2 koh beh chhoa7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 khi3; chiah e5 tai7-chi3 long2 si7 hai7-tioh8 goa2.  37). Liu5-pian7 ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 na7 bo5 chhoa7 i to3-lai5 kau li2, li2 thang thai5 goa2 nng7 e5 kiaN2; choe3 li2 thang chiong i kau-tai3 goa2, goa2 tek-khak chhoa7 i to3--lai5 kau li2.  38). Nga2-kok kong2, Goa2 e5 kiaN2 goa2 bo5 beh hou7 i kap lin2 khi3; i e5 hiaN i2-keng si2, chi2-u7 chhun i; i na7 ti7 lin2 sou2 kiaN5 e5 lou7 tu2-tioh8 ham7-hai7, he! chiu7-si7 lin2 hou7 goa2 peh8-thau5-mng5 chhiN-chham2 loh8 im-hu2.

[43]	Hit sou2-chai7 ki-hng chin-toa7.  2). In tui3 Ai-kip8 toa3-lai5 e5 gou7-kak i2-keng chiah8-liau2, in lau7-pe7 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 koh khi3 ka7 lan2 tiah8 tam7-poh8 bi2-niu5 lai5.  3). Iu5-tai7 in3 i kong2, Hit-lang5 chhiat-chhiat hoan-hu3 goan2 kong2, Lin2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap lin2 saN-kap lai5, lin2 chiu7 boe7 tit-tioh8 kiN3 goa2 e5 bin7.  4). Lin2 na7 chhe goan2 sio2-ti7 kap goan2 saN-kap khi3, goan2 chiu7 loh8--khi3, ka7 li2 tiah8 bi2-niu5.  5). Li2 na7 m7 chhe i khi3, goan2 chiu7 m7 loh8--khi3; in-ui7 hit-lang5 ka7 goan2 kong2, Lin2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap lin2 saN-kap lai5, lin2 chiu7 boe7 tit-tioh8 kiN3 goa2 e5 bin7.  6). I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 an2-ni hai7 goa2, ka7 hit-lang5 kong2 lin2 iau2 u7 sio2-ti7 ah?  7). In in3 kong2, Hit-lang5 ti3-i3 mng7 goan2 kap goan2 chhin-chok8 e5 tai7-chi3 kong2, Lin2 lau7-pe7 iau2 ti7-teh bo5? lin2 iau2 u7 hiaN-ti7 bo5? goan2 chiau3 i sou2 mng7--e5 ka7 i kong2; goan2 thai2-tho2 oe7 chai i beh kong2, Tioh8 toa3 lin2 sio2-ti7 loh8--lai5?  8). Iu5-tai7 koh ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Li2 chhe gin2-a2 kap goa2 khi3, goan2 chiu7 khi2-sin khi3, thang hou7 goan2 kap li2, i2-kip8 goan2 e5 gin2-a2, tit-tioh8 oah8, bian2 si2.  9). Goa2 ka7 i po2, li2 thang tui3 goa2 tho2; goa2 na7 bo5 chhoa7 i to3-lai5, khia7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, goa2 goan7 it-seng tam-tng choe7.  10). Lan2 na7 m7-si7 u7 ian5-chhian5, i2-keng te7-ji7-pai2 to3--lai5 lah.  11). In lau7-pe7 I2-sek-liat8 tui3 in kong2, Na7 si7 an2-ni, lin2 chiu7 tioh8 an2-ni choe3; thang chhu2 chit sou2-chai7 te7-it ho2 e5 thou2-san2, ju2-hiuN tam7-poh8, phang-bit8 tam7-poh8, i2-kip8 hiuN-liau7, but8-ioh8, hui2-chi2, heng7-jin5, long2 siu ti7 khi2-ku7 lai7; toa3--khi3 sang3 hit-lang5.  12). Koh tioh8 toa3 gun5 teng5-pe7, iah8 tioh8 chiong lin2 pou3-te7-khau2, i heng5 lin2 e5 gun5, toa3 to3-tng2 khi3 hou7--i; hit-e5 kiam2-chhai2 si7 sit-chho3;  13). iah8 chhoa7 lin2 sio2-ti7 khi2-sin, khi3 koh kiN3 hit-lang5.  14). Tok8-tok8 goan7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 hou7 lin2 ti7 hit-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 lin5-bin2; chiong lin2 hit e5 hiaN-ti7 kap Pian7-nga2-bin2 kau lin2; goa2 na7 sit-loh8 goa2 e5 kiaN2, iah8 tioh8 hou7 i sit-loh8 chiu7-si7.  15). Tui3 hit-tiap8 in toa3 hiah e5 le2-mih8, iah8 toa3 gun5 teng5-pe7, koh chhoa7 Pian7-nga2-bin2, khi2-sin loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8; khia7 ti7 Iok-sek e5 bin7-cheng5.
	16). Iok-sek khoaN3-kiN3 Pian7-nga2-bin2 kap in saN-kap lai5, chiu7 tui3 koan2-ke--e5 kong2, Chhoa7 chiah e5 lang5 khi3 chhu3-lai7, thai5 cheng-siN, pi7-pan7 ian5-siah8; in-ui7 jit8-tau3, chiah e5 lang5 beh kap goa2 saN-kap chiah8.  17). Hit-lang5 chiu7 chiau3 Iok-sek e5 oe7 khi3 kiaN5; chhoa7 in hiah e5 lang5 jip8 Iok-sek e5 chhu3.  18). Hiah e5 lang5, in-ui7 hou7 i chhoa7 kau3 Iok-sek e5 chhu3, chiu7 kiaN-hiaN5; kong2, Chhoa7 lan2 kau3 chia, tek-khak si7 in-ui7 thau5-chit8-pai2 heng5 lan2 ti7 pou3-te7-lai7 e5 gun5, beh chhe7 lan2 e5 khang-phang7, he7 chhiu2 hai7 lan2, kiong5-kiong5 liah8 lan2 choe3 lou5-pok8, chhiuN2 lan2 e5 lu5.  19). In chiu7 oa2-kun7 Iok-sek e5 koan2-ke--e5, ti7 chhu3-mng5-khau2 kap i kong2-oe7,  20). kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, goan2 thau5-pai2 loh8-lai5, sit8-chai7 si7 beh tiah8 bi2-niu5;  21). au7-lai5 kau3 hioh-mi5 e5 sou2-chai7, khui goan2 e5 pou3-te7, bo5 phah-sng3, goan2 tak8-lang5 e5 gun5 chiok-sou3 iu5-goan5 ti7 tak8-lang5 e5 pou3-te7-khau2; taN goan2 u7 koh toa3--lai5; goan2 leng7-goa7 u7 koh toa3 gun5 beh lai5 tiah8 bi2-niu5;  22). goan2 m7-chai chi7-chui7 chiong goan2 e5 gun5 he7 ti7 goan2 e5 pou3-te7-lai7.  23). Koan2-ke--e5 kong2, Choe3 lin2 an-sim, bian2 kiaN; si7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, kap lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, siuN2-su3 lin2 chai5-po2 ti7 lin2 e5 pou3-te7-lai7; lin2 e5 gun5 goa2 i2-keng siu-liau2.  Chiu7 chhoa7 Se-bian7 chhut-lai5 hou7 in.  24). Hit-lang5 chiu7 chhoa7 hiah e5 lang5 jip8 Iok-sek e5 chhu3, phang5 chui2 hou7 in, in chiu7 soe2 kha; koh theh8 chhau2-liau7 chhi7 in e5 lu5.  25). In chiu7 pi7-pan7 hiah e5 le2-mih8, theng3-hau7 Iok-sek jit8-tau3 to3--lai5; in-ui7 in thiaN-kiN3 beh ti7-hia chiah8.
	26). Iok-sek to3--lai5 kau3 chhu3, in chiu7 chiong sou2 toa3--lai5 e5 le2-mih8 theh8 jip8 chhu3 sang3--i; koh phak ti7 toe7--nih pai3 i.  27). Iok-sek mng7 in peng5-an; koh kong2, Lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 kong2 hit e5 lau7-lang5, peng5-an mah? i iau2 ti7--teh mah?  28). In in3 kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, goan2 e5 lau7-pe7, peng5-an, i iau2 ti7-teh; in chiu7 aN3-thau5 pai3 i.  29). Iok-sek kiah8-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 i tang5-bu2 e5 sio2-ti7, Pian7-nga2-bin2; chiu7 kong2, Li2 sou2 ka7 goa2 kong2 soah-be2 sio2-ti7, si7 chit-e5 mah? Koh kong2, Soe3-kiaN2, goan7 Siong7-te3 si-un hou7 li2.  30). Iok-sek thiaN3 sio2-ti7 e5 cheng5 toa7 siu7 kek-tong7; chiu7 koaN2-kin2 chhe7 chit8-ui7 thang thi5-khau3; jip8 i e5 pang5-keng thi5-khau3;  31). au7-lai5 soe2-bin7 chhut-lai5, bian2-kiong2 lun2--teh; hoan-hu3 khui-toh.  32). In chiu7 ui7 Iok-sek leng7-goa7 pai5 chit8 te3 toh, ui7 hiah e5 lang5 koh pai5 chit8 te3, iah8 ui7 kap Iok-sek saN-kap chiah8 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 leng7-goa7 pai5 chit8-te3; in-ui7 Ai-kip8 lang5 boe7 thang kap Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 saN-kap chiah8, che si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 iam3-ouN3.  33). Hiah e5 lang5 che7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, toa7-soe3 chiau3 in ni5-he3 e5 chhu3-su7; hiah e5 lang5 tai7-ke gong5-ngiah8.  34). Iok-sek chiong i bin7-cheng5 e5 chiah8-mih8, pun hou7 in; tok8-tok8 Pian7-nga2-bin2 sou2 tit-tioh8--e5, pi2 pat8-lang5 gou7-pe7 choe7; in chiu7 lim chiu2, kap Iok-sek saN-kap ian3-lok8.

[44]	Iok-sek hoan-hu3 koan2-ke--e5 kong2, chiong bi2-niu5 jip8 moa2 chiah e5 lang5 e5 pou3-te7, chin7 in sou2 oe7 toa3--e5; koh chiong tak8-lang5 e5 gun5 lok ti7 i e5 pou3-te7-khau2.  2). Iah8 chiong goa2 e5 poe, chiu7-si7 hit te3 gun5-poe, he7 ti7 siau3-lian5--e5 e5 pou3-te7-khau2; i tiah8 gou7-kak e5 gun5 iah8 soa3 he7--teh.  Koan2-ke--e5 chiu7 chiau3 Iok-sek sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 khi3 kiaN5.  3). ThiN chit8-e7 kng, chiu7 chhe hiah e5 lang5 kap in e5 lu5 khi3.  4). In chhut siaN5 kiaN5 bo5 joa7-hng7, Iok-sek ka7 koan2-ke--e5 kong2, Khi2--lai5, khi3 tui-jip hiah e5 lang5, tui-tioh8, chiu7 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 siaN2-su7 eng7 phaiN2 po3 ho2 ah?  5). Che kiam2 m7-si7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 lim-chiu2 e5 poe mah? Kiam2 m7-si7 i chiam-pok teh eng7--e5 mah? lin2 an2-ni choe3 si7 phaiN2.  6). Koan2-ke--e5 tui--tioh8 in, chiong chiah e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2.  7). In in3 kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 siaN2-su7 kong2 chit ho7 oe7? li2 e5 lou5-pok8 toan3-toan3 bo5 choe3 chit-ho7 su7.  8). Li2 khoaN3, goan2 cheng5 ti7 pou3-te7-khau2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 gun5, siong7-chhiaN2 tui3 Ka-lam5 toe7 toa3--lai5 heng5 li2; goan2 thai2-tho2 oe7 tui3 li2 chu2-lang5 e5 ke thau-theh8 kim-gun5 ah?  9). Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 tiong-kan, bo5-lun7 ti7 sim2-mih8 lang5 hia chhiau--tioh8, chiu7 hou7 i si2, goan2 iah8 beh choe3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 lou5-pok8.  10). Koan2-ke--e5 kong2, TaN chiu7 chiau3 lin2 e5 oe7 kiaN5; ti7 sim2-mih8 lang5 hia chhiau--tioh8, hit-lang5 chiu7 choe3 goa2 e5 lou5-pok8; ki5-u5--e5 long2 bo5 choe7.  11). Tui3 hit-tiap8 in tak8-lang5 koaN2-kin2 chiong pou3-te7 sia3 ti7 thou5-kha, tak8-lang5 thau2-khui in e5 pou3-te7.  12). Koan2-ke--e5 chiu7 chhiau, tui3 toa7--e5 khi2, kau3 soe3--e5 chi2; hit e5 poe keng2-jian5 ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 pou3-te7-lai7 chhiau--tioh8.  13). In chiu7 thiah-lih8 in e5 saN, tak8-lang5 chiong in e5 mih8 hou7 lu5 chai3, to3--khi3 siaN5-lai7.  14). Iu5-tai7 kap i e5 hiaN-ti7 kau3 Iok-sek e5 chhu3, Iok-sek iau2 ti7-hia, in chiu7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 phak-loh8 toe7.  15). Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, Lin2 sou2-choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? lin2 kiam2 m7-chai, chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 chit-ho7 e5 lang5 oe7 chiam-pok mah?  16). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goan2 tui3 goa2 e5 chu2 beh kong2 sim2-mih8? iau2 u7 siaN2 oe7 thang kong2? goan2 thai2 oe7 ka-ki7 sou3-beng5 ah? Siong7-te3 i2-keng cha-chhut li2 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 choe7-koa3, goan2 kap hit-e5 ti7 i e5 chhiu2 chhiau tioh8 poe--e5, long2 si7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 lou5-pok8.  17). Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 toan3-toan3 bo5 beh an2-ni choe3; Ti7 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5 chhiu2 chhiau tioh8 poe, hit-lang5 chiu7 tioh8 choe3 goa2 e5 lou5-pok8; lin2 chiah-e5 thang peng5-an chiuN7 khi3 lin2 lau7-pe7 hia.
	18). Iu5-tai7 oa2-kun7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2 chit8-ku3-oe7 hou7 goa2 e5 chu2 thiaN, boh8-tit siu7-khi3 li2 e5 lou5-pok8; in-ui7 li2 kap Hoat-lo2 chit8-iuN7.  19). Goa2 e5 chu2 bat mng7 li2 chiah e5 lou5-pok8 kong2, Lin2 u7 lau7-pe7, u7 hiaN-ti7 bo5?  20). Goan2 ka7 goa2 e5 chu2 kong2, Goan2 u7 lau7-pe7, i2-keng ni5-lau7; iau2 u7 i ni5-lau7 sou2 siN chit8 e5 soah-be2 kiaN2; i e5 hiaN i2-keng si2, i e5 lau7-bu2 kan-ta pang3 i chit8-e5, koh i e5 lau7-pe7 chin thiaN3--i.  21). Li2 ka7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2, Chhoa7 i loh8--lai5 goa2 chia, hou7 goa2 chhin-bak8 khoaN3-kiN3 i.  22). Goan2 ka7 goa2 e5 chu2 kong2, Gin2-a2 boe7-oe7 li7-khui i e5 lau7-pe7; na7 li7-khui i e5 lau7-pe7, lau7-pe7 tek-khak si2.  23). Li2 ka7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 kong2, Lin2 e5 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap lin2 saN-kap loh8--lai5, lin2 chiu7 boe7-tit koh kiN3 goa2 e5 bin7.  24). Goan2 chiuN7 kau3 li2 e5 lou5-pok8, goan2 lau7-pe7 hia, chiu7 chiong goa2 e5 chu2 e5 oe7 ka7 i kong2.  25). Goan2 e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Lin2 koh khi3 ka7 lan2 tiah8 tam7-poh8 bi2-niu5 lai5.  26). Goan2 chiu7 kong2, Goan2 boe7-oe7 loh8-khi3; goan2 e5 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 na7 kap goan2 saN-kap khi3, goan2 chiu7 beh loh8--khi3; in-ui7 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap goan2 saN-kap khi3, goan2 tek-khak boe7-tit kiN3 hit-lang5 e5 bin7.  27). Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, goa2 e5 lau7-pe7, ka7 goan2 kong2, Lin2 chai goa2 e5 bou2 ka7 goa2 siN nng7 e5 kiaN2;  28). chit8-e5 li7-khui goa2 chhut-khi3, goa2 kong2 i tek-khak si7 hou7 ia2-siu3 thiah-chhui3; kau3-taN goa2 iau2 m7-bat khoaN3-kiN3;  29). taN lin2 koh chiong chit-e5 chhoa7-khi3, li7-khui goa2; na7 i tu2-tioh8 ham7-hai7, chiu7-si7 lin2 hou7 goa2 peh8-thau5-mng5 chhiN-chham2 loh8 im-hu2.  30). Goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 siN3-mia7 kap chit e5 gin2-a2 e5 siN3-mia7 siN saN-lian5; taN goa2 to3--khi3 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 hia; na7 gin2-a2 bo5 kap goan2 saN-kap ti7-teh, goan2 e5 lau7-pe7 khoaN3 bo5 gin2-a2, i chiu7 tek-khak si2,  31). che chiu7-si7 goan2 hou7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8, goan2 e5 lau7-pe7, peh8-thau5-mng5 chhiN-chham2 loh8 im-hu2.  32). In-ui7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 bat tui3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 po2 chit e5 gin2-a2, kong2, Goa2 na7 bo5 chhoa7 i to3--lai5 kau li2, goa2 goan7 ti7 lau7-pe7 e5 bin7-cheng5 it-seng tam-tng choe7.  33). TaN kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 tiam3--teh, thoe3 chit e5 gin2-a2 choe3 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 lou5-pok8; hou7 gin2-a2 kap i hiah e5 hiaN saN-kap chiuN7--khi3.  34). Na7 gin2-a2 bo5 kap goa2 saN-kap khi3, goa2 thai2-tho2 oe7 chiuN7--khi3 kiN3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 ah? kiaN-liau2 goa2 khoaN3-kiN3 goan2 lau7-pe7 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 chai-e7.

[45]	Iok-sek ti7 hiah-e5 khia7 i sin-piN e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 lun2-boe7-tiau5; chiu7 hoah kong2, Cheng3-lang5 tioh8 li7-khui goa2 chhut-khi3.  Iok-sek chiong i pun2-sin hou7 hiaN-ti7 jin7-tit e5 si5, bo5 chit8-lang5 khia7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5.  2). I chiu7 chhut-siaN toa7-khau3; Ai-kip8 lang5 thiaN-kiN3, Hoat-lo2 e5 ke iah8 thiaN-kiN3.  3). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Goa2 si7 Iok-sek, goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 iau2 ti7-teh mah? I e5 hiaN-ti7 boe7-oe7 in3, in-ui7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 long2 kiaN-hiaN5.  4). Iok-sek koh ka7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, ChhiaN2 kiaN5-oa2--lai5.  In chiu7 oa2--lai5.  I kong2, Goa2 si7 lin2 e5 sio2-ti7 Iok-sek, chiu7-si7 lin2 sou2 boe7 kau3 Ai-kip8--e5.  5). TaN m7-bian2 in-ui7 boe7 goa2 kau3 chia lai5 iu-bun7, lai5 ka-ki7 oan3-hun7; che si7 Siong7-te3 chhe goa2 tai7-seng lin2 lai5, in-ui7 beh po2-choan5 siN3-mia7.  6). TaN ti7 chit sou2-chai7 e5 ki-hng i2-keng nng7-ni5, iau2 u7 gou7-ni5, bo5 thang cheng3-choh, bo5 thang siu-seng5.  7). Siong7-te3 chhe goa2 tai7-seng lin2 lai5, ui7-tioh8 beh ka7 lin2 lau5 chhun e5 cheng2-chok8 ti7 se3-chiuN7; koh beh kiaN5 I toa7 e5 chin2-kiu3, po2-choan5 lin2 e5 oah8-mia7.  8). An2-ni khoaN3--khi2-lai5, chhe goa2 kau3 chia e5, m7-si7 lin2, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3; I koh hou7 goa2 chhin-chhiuN7 Hoat-lo2 e5 pe7, choe3 i choan5-ke e5 chu2, kap koan2-li2 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7.  9). Lin2 tioh8 koaN2-kin2 chiuN7-khi3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 hia, ka7 i kong2, Li2 e5 kiaN2 Iok-sek an2-ni kong2, Siong7-te3 hou7 goa2 choe3 choan5 Ai-kip8 e5 chu2, chhiaN2 loh8--lai5 goa2 chia, m7-thang ian5-chhian5.  10). Li2 kap li2 e5 kiaN2 li2 e5 sun, kap gu5-kun5 iuN5-kun5, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, long2 thang lai5 tiam3 ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7, kap goa2 saN-kun7.  11). Goa2 beh ti7-hia hong7-seng5 li2; in-ui7 iau2 u7 gou7 ni5 e5 ki-hng, bian2-tit li2, kap li2 e5 ke-koan3, kap it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 loh8-poh8.  12). Ho5-hong3 lin2 e5 bak8-chiu kap goa2 e5 sio2-ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 bak8-chiu long2 khoaN3-kiN3 goa2 kap lin2 chhin-chhui3 tui3 lin2 kong2-oe7.  13). Lin2 ia7 tioh8 chiong goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8 it-chhe3 e5 eng5-kng kap lin2 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 su7, long2 ka7 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 kong2; koh tioh8 koaN2-kin2 chiong goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 poaN--lai5 goa2 chia.  14). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek phak ti7 i e5 sio2-ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 am7-kun2 thi5-khau5; Pian7-nga2-bin2 ia7 ti7 i e5 am7-kun2 thi5-khau3.  15). I koh kap cheng3 hiaN-ti7 chim-chhui3, pho7--in thi5-khau3; au7-lai5 i e5 hiaN-ti7 chiu7 kap i kong2-oe7.
	16). Chit e5 hong-siaN thoan5 kau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 keng-lai7, kong2, Iok-sek e5 hiaN-ti7 lai5 lah.  Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 long2 hoaN-hi2.  17). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 an2-ni kiaN5; chiong mih8 hou7 cheng-siN chai3; khi2-sin khi3 Ka-lam5 toe7;  18). chiong lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, kap lin2 e5 ke-koan3, long2 poaN--lai5 goa2 chia; goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 ho2-mih8 hou7 lin2, lin2 iah8 thang chiah8 chit sou2-chai7 e5 san-tin hai2-bi7.  19). TaN goa2 beng7-leng7 li2, lin2 tioh8 an2-ni choe3; tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 toa3 chhia khi3, chiong lin2 e5 gin2-a2, kap bou2, kap lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, long2 poaN--lai5.  20). M7-thang khoaN3-tang7 lin2 ke-lai7 e5 mih8, in-ui7 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 e5 ho2-mih8, long2 si7 lin2 e5.
	21). I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-kiaN2 chiu7 an2-ni kiaN5.  Iok-sek chiau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 beng7-leng7 hou7 in chhia, kap lou7-tiong tioh8 eng7 e5 chiah8-mih8;  22). koh hou7 in chit8-lang5 chit8-tho3 i-hok8; tok8-tok8 hou7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 gun5 saN-pah, i-hok8 gou7-tho3.  23). Sang3 in lau7-pe7 e5 mih8, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; lu5-kang2 chap8-chiah, chai3 Ai-kip8 e5 ho2-mih8; lu5-bu2 chap8-chiah, chai3 gou7-kak kap piaN2 kap chhai3, hou7 in lau7-pe7 lou7--nih thang eng7.  24). Iok-sek chiu7 chhe i e5 hiaN-ti7 to3--khi3, in chiu7 khi2-sin; koh ka7 in kong2, Lin2 m7-thang ti7 lou7--nih oan-ke.  25). In tui3 Ai-kip8 chiuN7--khi3, lai5 kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7, in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok hia.  26). Ka7 i kong2, Iok-sek iau2 ti7-teh, koh koan2-li2 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7.  Nga2-kok sim hun7--khi3, in-ui7 m7 sin3 in e5 oe7.  27). In chiu7 chiong Iok-sek tui3 in sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, long2 ka7 i kong2; i koh khoaN3-kiN3 Iok-sek sou2 chhe--lai5 beh chai3 i e5 chhia, in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok e5 sim oah8--khi2-lai5.  28). I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Ho2 lah; goa2 e5 kiaN2 Iok-sek iau2 ti7-teh, than3 goa2 iau2-be7 si2, goa2 beh khi3 khoaN3--i.

[46]	I2-sek-liat8 toa3 it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, khi2-sin lai5 kau3 Piat8-si7-pa; chiu7 hian3-che3 hou7 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3.  2). Mi5-si5 Siong7-te3 ti7 iN7-siong7 e5 tiong-kan ka7 I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Nga2-kok ah, Nga2-kok ah.  I kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia.  3). Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3; li2 loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8 m7-sai2 kiaN; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hou7 li2 ti7-hia chiaN5-choe3 toa7-kok.  4). Goa2 beh kap li2 saN-kap loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8, Goa2 iah8 tek-khak chhoa7 li2 khi2-lai5; Iok-sek beh chhiu2 hoaN7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu, hou7 li2 khoeh.  5). Nga2-kok chiu7 tui3 Piat8-si7-pa khi2-sin; I2-sek-liat8 hiah e5 kiaN2, hou7 in e5 lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok, kap in e5 kiaN2-ji5, in e5 bou2, long2 che7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 sou2 chhe--lai5 beh chai3 i e5 chhia.  6). Nga2-kok kap i it-chhe3 e5 kiaN2-sun, toa3 in e5 cheng-siN, i2-kip8 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 he3-chai5, long2 kau3 Ai-kip8.  7). Nga2-kok toa3 i e5 kiaN2, sun, cha-bou2-kiaN2, cha-bou2-sun, kap i it-chhe3 e5 hou7-e3, long2 kau3 Ai-kip8.
	8). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kau3 Ai-kip8--e5, Nga2-kok kap i e5 kiaN2, in e5 mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2.  Nga2-kok e5 toa7-kiaN2 Liu5-pian7.  9). Liu5-pian7 e5 kiaN2; Hap-lok8, Hoat-lou7, Hi-su-lun5, Ka-bi2.  10). Se-bian7 e5 kiaN2; Ia5-bou2-li2, Nga2-bin2, O-hat, Nga2-kun, So2-hat; iau2 u7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 kiaN2 So3-lo5.  11). Li7-bi7 e5 kiaN2; Kek-sun7, Kho-hat, Bi2-lah8-li7.  12). Iu5-tai7 e5 kiaN2; JiN2, Go5-lam5, Si7-lah8, Hoat-lek8-su, Sia7-lah8; tok8-tok8 JiN2 kap Go5-lam5 si2 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7.  Hoat-lek8-su e5 kiaN2; Hi-su-lun5, Hap-bou2-lek8.  13). I2-sat-ka e5 kiaN2; To5-lah8, Phou2-oa2, Iok-pek, Sin-lun5.  14). Se-pou3-lun5 e5 kiaN2; Se-liat8, I2-lun5, Nga2-li7.  15). Chiah-e5 si7 Li7-a ti7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 ka7 Nga2-kok sou2 siN e5 kiaN2; koh u7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Ti2-na2; kiaN2-sun lam5-lu2 kiong7 saN-chap8-saN lang5.  16). Ka-tek e5 kiaN2; Se2-hui-un5, Hap-ki, Su-ni5, I2-su-pun2, I2-li7, A-lo5-ti2, A-liat8-li7.  17). A-siat e5 kiaN2; Im-na2, Ek-si-oa2, Ek-si-ui2, Pi2-li7-a; koh in e5 sio2-be7 Se-lah8.  Pi2-li7-a e5 kiaN2; Hi-piat, Ma2-kiat.  18). Che si7 Lah8-pan hou7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-phaN3 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2-sun; chiu7-si7 i ka7 Nga2-kok siN--e5; kiong7 chap8-lak8 lang5.  19). Nga2-kok e5 bou2 Lah8-kiat e5 kiaN2; Iok-sek kap Pian7-nga2-bin2.  20). Iok-sek ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 siN Ma2-na2-se kap I2-hoat-lian5; chiu7-si7 An-siaN5 e5 che3-si, Pho-the5-hui-lah8 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, A-se-lap8, ka7 Iok-sek siN--e5.  21). Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 kiaN2; Pi2-lah8, Pi2-kiat, A-sit8-piat8, Ki-lah8, Nai2-ban7, I2-hi, Lo5-sit8, Bou2-peng5, Hou7-peng5, A-lek8;  22). che si7 Lah8-kiat ka7 Nga2-kok sou2 siN e5 kiaN2-sun, kiong7 chap8-si3 lang5.  23). Tan3 e5 kiaN2, Hou7-sin.  24). Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5 kiaN2; Nga2-siat, Kou-ni5, Ia5-sek, Si7-leng2;  25). che si7 Lah8-pan hou7 i e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Lah8-kiat e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2-sun, chiu7-si7 i ka7 Nga2-kok sou2 siN--e5; kiong7 chhit lang5.  26). Hiah-e5 kap Nga2-kok saN-kap kau3 Ai-kip8--e5, tu5 i e5 sim-pu7 i2-goa7, kiN3-na7 tui3 i sin-khu sou2 chhut--e5, kiong7 lak8-chap8-lak8 lang5.  27). Koh u7 Iok-sek ti7 Ai-kip8 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2, nng7-e5; Nga2-kok e5 ke lai5 kau3 Ai-kip8--e5 kiong7 chhit-chap8 lang5.
	28). Nga2-kok chhe Iu5-tai7 choe3-thau5 khi3 kiN3 Iok-sek, thang chhoa7 in khi3 Ko-san; in chiu7 kau3 Ko-san e5 toe7.  29). Iok-sek pi7-pan7 i e5 chhia; khi3 Ko-san, ngia5-chih i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sek-liat8; kau3 kiN3--tioh8 bin7, chiu7 phak ti7 lau7-pe7 e5 am7-kun2, ti7 am7-kun2--nih khau3 ku2-ku2.  30). I2-sek-liat8 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 kiN3--tioh8 li2 e5 bin7, chai li2 iau2 oah8--teh, goa2 taN si2 iah8 kam-sim.  31). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 hiaN-ti7 kap lau7-pe7 e5 ke kong2, Goa2 beh chiuN7-khi3 thong-ti Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 kap goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, cheng5 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7--e5, taN long2 lai5 kau3 goa2 chia.  32). In si7 bok8-chia2, in-ui7 in si7 chhi7 cheng-siN e5 lang5; in chiong iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5 long2 toa3--lai5.  33). Hoat-lo2 tiau3 lin2 e5 si5, na7 mng7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 choe3 sim2-mih8 thau5-lou7?  34). lin2 tioh8 kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8, tui3 siau3-lian5 kau3-taN, goan2 lian5 goan2 e5 chou2-kong long2 si7 teh chhi7 cheng-siN; an2-ni lin2 thang lai5 khia7 ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7; in-ui7 kiN3-na7 chhi7 cheng-siN--e5, long2 si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 sou2 iam3-chian7.

[47]	Iok-sek jip8--khi3 ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap goa2 e5 hiaN-ti7 toa3 in e5 iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap it-chhe3 sou2-u7--e5, tui3 Ka-lam5 toe7 lai5; taN ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7.  2). Iok-sek tui3 i e5 hiaN-ti7 e5 tiong-kan keng2 gou7 lang5, chhoa7 in khi3 kiN3 Hoat-lo2.  3). Hoat-lo2 mng7 Iok-sek e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Lin2 choe3 sim2-mih8 thau5-lou7? In ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Li2 e5 lou5-pok8 pun2-sin, kap goan2 e5 chou2-kong, long2 si7 kou3-iuN5 e5 lang5.  4). In koh ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Ka-lam5 toe7 ki-hng chin siong-tiong7, lou5-pok8 e5 iuN5-kun5 bo5 chhau2 thang chiah8; sou2-i2 goan2 lai5, si7 beh kia3-kha ti7-chia; taN kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 li2 e5 lou5-pok8 tiam3 ti7 Ko-san toe7.  5). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 lai5 kau3 li2 chia;  6). Ai-kip8 toe7 long2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; hou7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 toa3 ti7 kok-lai7 te7 it ho2 e5 toe7; in thang toa3 ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7; li2 na7 chai in tiong-kan khah u7 pun2-su7 e5 lang5, chiu7 phai3 in koan2-kou3 goa2 e5 cheng-siN.  7). Iok-sek chhoa7 i e5 lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok jip8--khi3 khia7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5; Nga2-kok chiu7 ka7 Hoat-lo2 chiok-hok.  8). Hoat-lo2 mng7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 si7 joa7 choe7 ah?  9). Nga2-kok ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, goa2 kia3-kha ti7 se3-kan e5 ni5-jit8 si7 chit8-pah saN-chap8 he3.  Goa2 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 iah8 chio2, iah8 kan-khou2, m7-tat8-tioh8 goa2 e5 liat8-chou2 kia3-kha ti7 se3-kan e5 ni5-jit8.  10). Nga2-kok koh ka7 Hoat-lo2 chiok-hok; chiu7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-khi3.  11). Iok-sek chiau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 beng7-leng7, chiong Ai-kip8 kok te7-it ho2 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Lan5-sek e5 toe7, hou7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kap i hiaN-ti7 khia7-khi2, choe3 san2-giap8.  12). Iok-sek eng7 bi2-niu5 hong7-seng5 i e5 lau7-pe7, kap i e5 hiaN-ti7, kap i e5 lau7-pe7 choan5-ke; long2 chiau3 in e5 lang5-giah8 lai5 kiong-kip in.
	13). Ki-hng chin siong-tiong7, choan5-toe7 long2 bo5 bi2-niu5; sim7-chi3 Ai-kip8 toe7 kap Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 lang5, in-ui7 ki-hng e5 ian5-kou3, go7 kau3 hun7--khi3.  14). Iok-sek chu7-chip8 Ai-kip8 toe7 kap Ka-lam5 toe7 sou2 u7 e5 gun5, chiu7-si7 in tiah8 bi2-niu5 e5 gun5; Iok-sek chiu7 chiong hiah e5 gun5 toa3 kau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 keng.  15). Ai-kip8 toe7 kap Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 gun5 long2 eng7-liau2; Ai-kip8 cheng3-lang5 long2 lai5 kiN3 Iok-sek kong2, Goan2 e5 gun5 long2 eng7-liau2 lah, kiu5 li2 hou7 goan2 bi2-niu5; goan2 siaN2-su7 tioh8 si2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5?  16). Iok-sek kong2, Na7 si7 gun5 eng7-liau2, lin2 e5 cheng-siN thang khan--lai5; goa2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 cheng-siN beh hou7 lin2 bi2-niu5.  17). In chiu7 chiong cheng-siN koaN2 kau3 Iok-sek hia; Iok-sek chiu7 eng7 bi2-niu5 oaN7 in e5 be2, iuN5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap lu5; hit-ni5 ui7-tioh8 oaN7 in it-chhe3 e5 cheng-siN, chiu7 eng7 bi2-niu5 iuN2-chhi7 in.  18). Hit-ni5 i2-keng ke3; te7-ji7 ni5, in koh lai5 kiN3 Iok-sek, ka7 i kong2, Goan2 boe7 moa5--tit goa2 e5 chu2, goan2 e5 gun5 long2 eng7-liau2, cheng-siN iah8 long2 kui ti7 goa2 e5 chu2, goan2 ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5, tu5 goan2 e5 sin-the2 kap goan2 e5 chhan5-toe7 i2-goa7, bo5 chhun chit8-hang7.  19). goan2 siaN2-su7 lang5 si2, toe7 pha-hng, ti7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 ah? kiu5 li2 eng7 bi2-niu5 boe2 goan2 kap goan2 e5 toe7; goan2 kap goan2 e5 toe7 choe3 Hoat-lo2 e5 lou7-eng7; koh eng7 cheng2-chi2 hou7 goan2, hou7 goan2 tit-tioh8 oah8, bian2 si2, thou2-toe7 iah8 bian2 pha-hng.
	20). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek ui7 Hoat-lo2 boe2 Ai-kip8 sou2 u7 e5 toe7; Ai-kip8 lang5 in-ui7 hou7 ki-hng sou2 pek, tak8-lang5 long2 boe7 i e5 chhan5-toe7; hiah e5 toe7 chiu7 long2 kui ti7 Hoat-lo2.  21). Iok-sek chiau3 chiah e5 siaN5-ip chhian-soa2 Ai-kip8 e5 peh-siN3 tui3 Ai-kip8 chit-peng5 kau3 ti7 hit-peng5.  22). Tok8-tok8 che3-si e5 toe7 Hoat-lo2 bo5 boe2--i; in-ui7 che3-si u7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 tit-tioh8 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 niu5; in chiah8 Hoat-lo2 sou2 hou7 in e5 niu5; sou2-i2 in bo5 boe7 in e5 toe7.  23). Iok-sek ka7 peh-siN3 kong2, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 ui7 Hoat-lo2 boe2 lin2 kap lin2 e5 toe7; khoaN3 ah, ti7-chia u7 cheng2-chi2 hou7 lin2, lin2 thang khi3 choh-chhan5;  24). kau3 siu-seng5 e5 si5, lin2 tioh8 chiong gou7-hun7-chit8 lap8 hou7 Hoat-lo2; si3-hun7 kui lin2, choe3 chhan5--nih e5 cheng2-chi2, iah8 choe3 lin2 kap lin2 ke-lai7 lang5 e5 chiah8-mih8, i2-kip8 lin2 e5 gin2-a2 e5 chiah8-mih8.  25). In kong2, Li2 u7 kiu3 goan2 e5 siN3-mia7; goan7 goan2 ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, goan2 beh choe3 Hoat-lo2 e5 lou5-pok8.  26). An2-ni Iok-sek ui7 Ai-kip8 e5 toe7, siat-lip8 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 le7, kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8; Hoat-lo2 tit-tioh8 gou7-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7; tok8-tok8 che3-si e5 toe7 bo5 kui Hoat-lo2.
	27). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khia7-khi2 Ai-kip8 kok, Ko-san e5 toe7, in ti7-hia kian3-ti3 san2-giap8, koh siN-thoaN3 kek8-ki5 choe7.  28). Nga2-kok tiam3 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 chap8-chhit ni5.  Nga2-kok it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 si7 chit8-pah si3-chap8-chhit he3.  29). I2-sek-liat8 si2 e5 jit8 kun7 lah; i chiu7 kio3 i e5 kiaN2 Iok-sek lai5, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, chhiaN2 li2 he7 chhiu2 ti7 goa2 e5 toa7-thui2-e7, eng7 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8 khoan2-thai7 goa2; m7-thang bai5-chong3 goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8.  30). Goa2 kap goa2 e5 pe7-kong tang5-khun3 e5 si5, li2 tioh8 chiong goa2 toa3 chhut Ai-kip8, bai5-chong3 ti7 in bai5-chong3 e5 toe7.  Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 beh chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 lai5 kiaN5.  31). Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 goa2 chiu3-choa7; i chiu7 tui3 i chiu3-choa7.  Tui3 an2-ni I2-sek-liat8 oa2 chhng5-thau5 keng3-pai3 Siong7-te3.

[48]	Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, u7 lang5 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Lin2 lau7-pe7 phoa3-piN7 lah; i chiu7 chhoa7 i nng7 e5 kiaN2 Ma2-na2-se, I2-hoat-lian5, saN-kap khi3.  2). U7 lang5 thong-ti Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 khoaN3, li2 e5 kiaN2 Iok-sek lai5 beh chhe7 li2; I2-sek-liat8 chiu7 bian2-kiong2 khi2-lai5, che7 ti7 bin5-chhng5.  3). Nga2-kok ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 bat ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Lou7-su tui3 goa2 chhut-hian7, su3-hok goa2;  4). ka7 goa2 kong2, Goa2 beh hou7 li2 siN-thoaN3 choe7-choe7, chiaN5-choe3 choe7-choe7 peh-siN3; iah8 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 siuN2-su3 li2 e5 hou7-e3, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 giap8.  5). Goa2 be7 kau3 Ai-kip8 li2 chia e5 tai7-seng, li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 sou2 siN nng7 e5 kiaN2, I2-hoat-lian5 Ma2-na2-se, si7 goa2-e5, chhin-chhiuN7  Liu5-pian7 Se-bian7 si7 goa2-e5 chit8-iuN7.  6). Ti7 in i2-au7, li2 sou2 siN e5 kiaN2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5; in thang kui ti7 in nng7 e5 hiaN e5 mia5-e7, tit-tioh8 giap8.  7). Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 tui3 Pa-tan3 lai5 e5 si5, Lah8-kiat si2 ti7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7, ti7 lou7--nih e5 tiong-kan, li7-khui I2-hoat-tha iau2 u7 chit8-cham7; goa2 chiu7 ka7 i bai5-chong3 ti7 I2-hoat-tha e5 lou7. (I2-hoat-tha chiu7-si7 Pek-li7-heng5).
	8). I2-sek-liat8 khoaN3-kiN3 Iok-sek nng7 e5 kiaN2, chiu7 kong2, Che si7 chi7-chui7?  9). Iok-sek ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2, Che si7 goa2 e5 kiaN2, Siong7-te3 ti7-chia siuN2-su3 goa2--e5.  Kong2, ChhiaN2 li2 chhoa7 in oa2-kun7 goa2; goa2 beh ka7 in chiok-hok.  10). I2-sek-liat8 ni5-lau7, bak8-chiu hoe boe7 khoaN3-kiN3; Iok-sek chhoa7 in kun7-oa2 i e5 bin7-cheng5, i chiu7 ka7 in chim-chhui3 pho7 in.  11). I2-sek-liat8 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 bo5 phah-sng3 oe7 kiN3-tioh8 li2 e5 bin7; taN Siong7-te3 koh hou7 goa2 khoaN3-tioh8 li2 e5 kiaN2.  12). Iok-sek chiong nng7 e5 kiaN2 tui3 i nng7 e5 kha-thau5-u-tiong chhoa7--chhut-lai5; pun2-sin chiu7 phak-loh8 toe7 pai3.  13). Au7-lai5 Iok-sek koh khan in nng7-e5, chiaN3-chhiu2 khan I2-hoat-lian5 ng3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 to3-chhiu2, to3-chhiu2 khan Ma2-na2-se ng3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chiaN3-chhiu2, chhoa7 in kun7-oa2 i.  14). I2-sek-liat8 chhun chiaN3-chhiu2 hoaN7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 thau5-khak, i si7 te7-ji7--e5, koh phah-chhe eng7 to3-chhiu2 hoaN7 Ma2-na2-se e5 thau5-khak, Ma2-na2-se pun2 si7 toa7-kiaN2.  15). I chiu7 ka7 Iok-sek chiok-hok kong2, Goan7 goa2 e5 chou2 A-pek-lah8-han2, kap goa2 e5 pe7 I2-sat, sou2 kiaN5 ti7 I bin7-cheng5 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 it-seng po2-iuN2 goa2 kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8 e5 Siong7-te3,  16). kiu3-siok8 goa2 thoat-li7 it-chhe3 e5 hoan7-lan7, hit e5 Su3-chia2, su3-hok hou7 chi2 nng7 e5 gin2-a2; goan7 in kui ti7 goa2 e5 mia5-e7, kap goa2 chou2 A-pek-lah8-han2, goa2 e5 pe7 I2-sat, e5 mia5-e7; koh goan7 in ti7 se3-kai3-tiong siN-thoaN3 chin-choe7.  17). Iok-sek khoaN3 i e5 lau7-pe7 eng7 chiaN3-chhiu2 hoaN7 ti7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 thau5-khak, bo5 hoaN-hi2; chiu7 thaN2 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 chhiu2, beh tui3 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 thau5-khak soa2 kau3 Ma2-na2-se e5 thau5-khak.  18). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, m7-si7 an2-ni; chit-e5 si7 toa7-kiaN2, kiu5 li2 eng7 chiaN3-chhiu2 hoaN7 i e5 thau5-khak.  19). I e5 lau7-pe7 m7-than3 kong2, Goa2 chai, goa2 e5 kiaN2, goa2 chai; i iah8 beh chiaN5-choe3 chit8-chok8, iah8 beh khoah-toa7; chong2-si7 i e5 sio2-ti7 chiong-lai5 pi2 i khah-toa7; i e5 sio2-ti7 e5 hou7-e3 beh chiaN5-choe3 choe7-choe7 chok8.  20). Tng hit-jit8 chiu7 ka7 in chiok-hok kong2, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 beh ki2 li2 lai5 chiok-hok lang5 kong2, Goan7 Siong7-te3 hou7 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 I2-hoat-lian5, chhin-chhiuN7 Ma2-na2-se chit8-iuN7; tui3 an2-ni lip8 I2-hoat-lian5 ti7 Ma2-na2-se e5 tai7-seng.  21). I2-sek-liat8 koh ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 beh si2 lah; chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 beh kap li2 ti7-teh, beh chhoa7 lin2 to3--khi3 lin2 liat8-chou2 e5 toe7.  22). Goa2 cheng5 eng7 goa2 e5 keng, goa2 e5 to, tui3 A-mou5-li7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 chhiuN2-lai5 hit te3-toe7, goa2 taN hou7 li2, pi2 li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 tit-tioh8 khah-ke.

[49]	Nga2-kok kio3 i hiah e5 kiaN2 lai5 kong2, Lin2 long2 chu7-chip8, goa2 beh chiong lin2 jit8-au7 sou2 oe7 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7 ka7 lin2 kong2.
2). 	Nga2-kok chiah e5 kiaN2, lin2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 lai5 thiaN,
	Tioh8 thiaN lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 oe7.
3).	Liu5-pian7 ah, li2 si7 goa2 e5 toa7-kiaN2, goa2 e5 koan5-se3, goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 e5 khi2-thau5,
	Ui-giam5 e5 tek8-sek--e5, koan5-leng5 e5 tek8-sek--e5.
4).	Chong2-si7 li2 chhin-chhiuN7 chui2 teh-kun2, tek-khak boe7 tit-tioh8 ku thau5-ui7;
	In-ui7 li2 peh-chiuN7 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 bin5-chhng5;
	Hit-si5 li2 phah la5-sam5 i; i peh-chiuN7 goa2 e5 phou.
5).	Se-bian7 Li7-bi7 si7 hiaN-ti7;
	In e5 to-kiam3 si7 hiong-ok e5 khi3-ku7.
6).	Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, li2 m7-thang kap in tang5 ke3-bou5;
	Goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 ah, li2 m7-thang kap in e5 hoe7-chiong3 lian5-lok8.
	In-ui7 in theng3-khi2 siu7-khi3, thai5-si2 lang5,
	In chhut-chai7 i3-su3 koah-tng7 gu5-thui2 e5 toa7-kun.
7).	In e5 siu7-khi3 so3-po7, thang chiu3-chou2;
	In e5 hun7-khi3 chan5-jim2, iah8 si7 thang chiu3-chou2;
	Goa2 beh pun-khui in ti7 Nga2-kok ke,
	Si3-soaN3 in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 chok8.
8).	Iu5-tai7 ah, li2 e5 hiaN-ti7 beh o-lo2 li2;
	Li2 e5 chhiu2 beh chhih8 tui3-tek8 e5 am7-kun2;
	Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 kiaN2 beh phak-pai3 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.
9).	Iu5-tai7 si7 soe3-chiah sai;
	Goa2 e5 kiaN2 ah, li2 tui3 sou2 jiau3--tioh8 e5 mih8, chiu7 chiuN7-khi3;
	I khut-loh8, i thiN3-kha, chhin-chhiuN7 sai;
	Iah8 chhin-chhiuN7 bu2 e5 sai, chi7-chui7 kaN2 jia2 i?
10).	Koan5-peng3 bo5 li7-khui Iu5-tai7,
	Ti7-li2--e5 bo5 li7-khui i nng7 ki kha e5 tiong-kan,
	Kau3 Si7-lo5 lai5;
	Liat8-pang long2 beh kui i.
11).	Pak8 i e5 lu5-a2 ti7 phu5-to5-chhiu7,
	Pak8 i e5 lu5-a2-kiaN2 ti7 ho2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7;
	Eng7 phu5-to5-chiu2 soe2 i e5 i-hok8,
	Eng7 phu5-to5-chiap soe2 i e5 i-chiuN5.
12).	I e5 bak8-chiu in-ui7 chiu2 lai5 ang5,
	I e5 chhui3-khi2 in-ui7 leng lai5 peh8.
13).	Se-pou3-lun5 beh khia7-khi2 hai2-khau2,
	Beh choe3 pha-chun5 e5 hai2-khau2;
	I e5 kai3 beh kau3 Se-tun3.
14).	I2-sat-ka si7 iong2 e5 lu5,
	To2 ti7 iuN5-tiau5 e5 tiong-kan;
15).	I khoaN3 an-cheng7 choe3 ho2, khoaN3 thou2-toe7 choe3 sui2;
	AN3 keng-thau5 taN-teh, chiaN5-choe3 lo5-khou2 e5 lou5-pok8.
16).	Tan3 beh phoaN3-toan3 i e5 peh-siN3,
	Chhin-chhiuN7 I2-sek-liat8 chi-phai3 e5 chit8-e5.
17).	Tan3 beh choe3 lou7--nih e5 choa5,
	Lou7-tiong e5 tok8-choa5;
	Ka7-siong be2-toe5, khia7 e5 lang5 hiaN3 tui3 au7-bin7 loh8--khi3.
18).	Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 u7 theng3-hau7 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3.
19).	Ka-tek beh hou7 kun-tui7 tui-pek,
	Chong2-si7 i beh tui-pek in e5 kha-au7-tiN.
20).	A-siat beh chhut ho2 e5 bi2-niu5,
	Koh chhut ong5 sou2 chiah8 e5 ho2-mih8.
21).	Na2-hut-tha-li7 si7 thau2-pang3 e5 lok8-bu2,
	Chhut ho2-thiaN e5 oe7.
22).	Iok-sek si7 gau5 kiat ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7-ki;
	I e5 chhiu7-ki chhun-chhut chhiuN5-goa7.
23).	Sia7-chiN3 e5 lang5 toa7 siong-hai7 i,
	Eng7 chiN3 sia7 i, khun2-pek i;
24).	Chong2-si7 i e5 keng iu5-goan5 an5,
	I e5 chhiu2 ia7 tit-tioh8 u7 lat8;
	Che si7 tui3 Nga2-kok e5 Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 chhiu2,
	(Tui3 che chiu7 u7 chhut bok8-chia2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 chioh8-poaN5),
25).	Iah8 tui3 li2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, I beh pang-chan7 li2;
	Koh tui3 hit e5 Choan5-leng5--e5, I beh su3-hok li2;
	Beh eng7 thiN-teng2 kang3-loh8 e5 hok-khi3,
	Chhim-ian sou2 khng3 e5 hok-khi3,
	I2-kip8 chiah8-leng seng-san2 e5 hok-khi3, long2 beh hou7 li2.
26).	Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 sou2 chiok e5 hok-khi3,
	IaN5-ke3 goa2 e5 pe7-kong sou2 chiok e5 hok-khi3,
	Tit8-kau3 eng2 se3-tai7 e5 soaN-nia2 kek8-thau5 e5 piN-kai3;
	Chiah e5 hok-khi3 beh kang3-loh8 ti7 Iok-sek e5 thau5-khak,
	Lim5-kau3 hit e5 kap hiaN-ti7 tek8-piat8-e5 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.
27).	Pian7-nga2-bin2 si7 gau5 peh-thiah e5 chhai5-long5;
	Cha2-khi2-si5 chiah8 i sou2 jiau3--tioh8-e5,
	E5-hng-si5 pun i sou2 chhiuN2--tioh8 e5.
	28). Che it-chhe3 si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3; che iah8 si7 in e5 lau7-pe7 tui3 in sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, ka7 in sou2 chiok-hok--e5; long2 si7 chiau3 tak8-lang5 e5 hok-hun7, ka7 in chiok-hok.  29). I koh hoan-hu3 in kong2, Goa2 beh to3-khi3 goa2 e5 liat8-chou2 hia, lin2 tioh8 chiong goa2 bai5-chong3 ti7 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8, kap goa2 e5 pe7-kong siang5 sou2-chai7;  30). chiu7-si7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 Ban7-li7 e5 bin7-cheng5, Bek8-pi2-lah8 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8; hit e5 hiat8 kap chhan5 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 boe2 choe3 giap8, lai5 choe3 bong7-toe7 e5.  31). Ti7-hia bai5-chong3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kap i e5 bou2 Sat-lah8; koh ti7-hia bai5-chong3 I2-sat kap i e5 bou2 Li7-pek-ka; goa2 iah8 ti7-hia bai5-chong3 Li7-a.  32). Hit khu chhan5 kap hit lai7-bin7 e5 hiat8, si7 tui3 Hek-lang5 boe2--e5.  33). Nga2-kok hoan-hu3 i hiah e5 kiaN2 beng5-pek8, kha kiu-chiuN7 chhng5, chiu7 khui3 tng7, to3--khi3 i e5 liat8-chou2 hia.

[50]	Iok-sek phak ti7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 bin7, thi5-khau3, chim--i.  2). Iok-sek hoan-hu3 su-hau7 i e5 i-seng, eng7 hiuN-liau7 koan3 i e5 lau7-pe7; i-seng chiu7 eng7 hiuN-liau7 koan3 I2-sek-liat8.  3). Koan3 sin-si tiaN7-tioh8 e5 le7 tioh8 si3-chap8 jit8; hit e5 si3-chap8 jit8 moa2, koh Ai-kip8 lang5 ui7 i thi5-khau3 chhit-chap8 jit8.
	4). Ui7-tioh8 i thi5-khau3 e5 jit8 i2-keng ke3, Iok-sek tui3 Hoat-lo2 ke-lai7 e5 lang5 kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, chhiaN2 lin2 thong-ti Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2,  5). Goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 kah goa2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh si2 lah, li2 tioh8 chiong goa2 bai5-chong3 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7, ti7 goa2 ui7 pun2-sin sou2 kut8 e5 bong7; taN kiu5 li2 chun2 goa2 chiuN7--khi3 bai5-chong3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7, jian5-au7 goa2 beh to3-tng2--lai5.  6). Hoat-lo2 kong2, Li2 thang chiuN7--khi3 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, chiau3 i sou2 kah li2 chiu3 e5 choa7.  7). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek chiuN7--khi3 bai5-chong3 i e5 lau7-pe7; kap i saN-kap chiuN7--khi3 e5, u7 Hoat-lo2 e5 cheng3 jin5-sin5, kap Hoat-lo2 ke-lai7 e5 tiong2-lo2, kap Ai-kip8 kok cheng3 tiong2-lo2.  8). Koh u7 Iok-sek choan5-ke, kap i hiah e5 hiaN-ti7, i2-kip8 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke-koan3; chi2-u7 in e5 gin2-a2, kap iuN5-kun5 gu5-kun5, long2 lau5 ti7 Ko-san toe7.  9). Koh u7 chhia kap khia5-be2--e5, hit-tin7 e5 lang5 put-chi2 choe7.  10). In kau3 Iok-tan3 ho5 goa7, A-tat8 e5 gou7-kak-tiuN5, chiu7 ti7-hia toa7 thi5-khau3, toa7 ai-siong; Iok-sek ui7-tioh8 lau7-pe7 pi-ai chhit-jit8.  11). Ka-lam5 toe7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-siN3 khoaN3-kiN3 A-tat8 gou7-kak-tiuN5 e5 thi5-khau3, chiu7 kong2, Che si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 chit8-tiuN5 e5 toa7 thi5-khau3; in-ui7 an2-ni, hit e5 toe7 mia5 kio3 A-pek-bek8-se, si7 ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 goa7.  12). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kiaN2 chiu7 chiau3 lau7-pe7 sou2 hoan-hu3--e5 ka7 i choe3;  13). hiah e5 kiaN2 chiong i un7 kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7, bai5-chong3 ti7 Ban7-li7 e5 thau5-cheng5, Bek8-pi2-lah8 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8, hit e5 hiat8 kap chhan5 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 boe2 choe3 giap8, lai5 choe3 bong7-toe7 e5.  14). Iok-sek bai5-chong3 in lau7-pe7 i2-au7, chiu7 kap cheng3 hiaN-ti7, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 kap i chiuN7-khi3 bai5-chong3 in lau7-pe7 e5 lang5, long2 to3-tng2 Ai-kip8.
	15). Iok-sek hiah e5 hiaN khoaN3 in lau7-pe7 i2-keng si2, chiu7 kong2, Kiam2-chhai2 Iok-sek beh oan3-hun7 lan2, chiau3 lan2 cheng5 khoan2-thai7 i long2-chong2 e5 phaiN2, it-chin7 po3-eng3 lan2.  16). In chiu7 thok lang5 khi3 kiN3 Iok-sek kong2, Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng, hoan-hu3 kong2,  17). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Iok-sek an2-ni kong2, Cheng5 li2 chiah e5 hiaN phaiN2 khoan2-thai7 li2, kiu5 li2 sia3-bian2 in e5 ke3-sit kap choe7-ok; taN kiu5 li2 sia3-bian2 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 lou5-pok8 e5 ke3-sit.  In tui3 Iok-sek kong2 chiah e5 oe7, Iok-sek chiu7 thi5-khau3.  18). I chiah e5 hiaN koh lai5 phak ti7 i bin7-cheng5 kong2, Goan2 si7 li2 e5 lou5-pok8.  19). Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, M7-bian2 kiaN; goa2 kiam2 thoe3 Siong7-te3 mah?  20). Cheng5 lin2 e5 i3-su3 si7 phaiN2, chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3 si7 ho2; beh po2-choan5 choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 siN3-mia7, chhin-chhiuN7 kin-a2-jit8.  21). TaN lin2 m7-bian2 kiaN; goa2 beh iuN2-chhi7 lin2, kap lin2 e5 kiaN2-ji5.  Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek eng7 chhin-ai3 e5 oe7 an-ui3 in.
	22). Iok-sek kap in lau7-pe7 e5 ke-koan3 long2 tiam3 Ai-kip8; Iok-sek chiah8 pah-it he3.  23). Iok-sek tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 I2-hoat-lian5 te7-saN tai7 e5 sun; Ma2-na2-se e5 sun Ma2-kiat e5 kiaN2, Iok-sek iah8 pho7 in ti7 kha-thau5-u.  24). Iok-sek tui3 i e5 hiaN-ti7 kong2, Goa2 beh si2 lah; chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 tek-khak khoaN3-kou3 lin2, chhoa7 lin2 tui3 chit sou2-chai7 chiuN7-khi3, kau3 I chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 hou7 A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok e5 toe7.  25). Iok-sek kah I2-sek-liat8 e5 kiaN2-sun chiu3-choa7 kong2, Siong7-te3 tek-khak chiau3-kou3 lin2, lin2 tioh8 chiong goa2 e5 kut-thau5 un7-chiuN7--khi3.  Iok-sek si2, tu2-a2 pah-it he3; lang5 eng7 hiuN-liau7 ka7 i koan3; chiong i siu-loh8 koan, theng5 ti7 Ai-kip8.
